--- FILE: Database\Cache.cs ---
namespace Database
{
    public class DBCache
    {

        public List<Query> Pool = new List<Query>();

        private static DBCache _instance;

        private DBCache() { }

        public static DBCache GetInstance()
        {
            if (_instance == null)
                _instance = new DBCache();

            return _instance;
        }


        public void RemoveCache(Query orig)
        {
            if (Pool.Contains(orig))
                Pool.Remove(orig);
        }

        public Query GetQuery(Query orig)
        {
            object o = new object();
            lock (Pool)
            {
                foreach (Query q in Pool)
                {
                    if (null != q)
                    {
                        if (q.Equals(orig))
                            return q;
                    }
                }
            }
            return null;
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Database\Common.cs ---
namespace Database
{
    public static class Common
    {
        public static int GetNextId(string server, string key)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetNextId @name = @key, @id=@new_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@key", key);
            q.AddParameter("@new_id|OUT", -1);
            q.Execute();
            int new_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@new_id"]);
            return new_id;
        }


        public static string GetGlobal(string server, string global, bool cache = true,bool replace_variables = false)
        {
            string sql = "select value from Globals where [key] = @key";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = cache;
            q.AddParameter("@key", global);
            string var = q.ExecuteSingle<string>();
            if(replace_variables)
                var = UtilsLib.FileLib.FileLocationWithVariables(var);
            return var;
        }

        public static T GetGlobal<T>(string server, string global,bool replace_variables = false, bool use_cache = false)
        {
            string s = GetGlobal(server, global, use_cache, replace_variables);
            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(s, typeof(T));
        }
        public static T GetGlobalNoCache<T>(string server, string global, bool replace_variables = false)
        {
            string s = GetGlobal(server, global, false, replace_variables);
            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(s, typeof(T));
        }


    }
}


--- FILE: Database\Connection.cs ---
namespace Database
{
    public class Connection
    {
        public string _server;
        public Nullable<int> _port;
        public string _username;
        public string _password;
        public string _intial_catalog;
        public bool _integrated_security;

        public int id;

        public IConnection _conn;

        public void SetIConnection(IConnection conn)
        {
            _conn = conn;
        }

        public Connection(string server, Nullable<int> port, string username, string password, string intial_catalog,bool integrated_security)
        {
            _server = server;
            _port = port;
            _username = username;
            _password = password;
            _intial_catalog = intial_catalog;
            _integrated_security = integrated_security;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public bool Equals(Connection c)
        {
            if ((object)c == null)
            {
                return false;
            }

            return this._server == c._server && this._port == c._port && this._username == c._username && this._password == c._password && this._intial_catalog == c._intial_catalog && this._integrated_security == c._integrated_security;
        }

    }
}

--- FILE: Database\ConnectionPool.cs ---
namespace Database
{
    public class ConnectionPool
    {

        public Dictionary<Connection, IConnection> Pool = new Dictionary<Connection, IConnection>();

        private static ConnectionPool _instance;

        private ConnectionPool() { }

        public static ConnectionPool GetInstance()
        {
            if (_instance == null)
            {
                _instance = new ConnectionPool();
            }
            return _instance;
        }

        public void AddConnection(Connection i, IConnection c)
        {
            lock (Pool)
            {
                if (null == i)
                {

                }
                else 
                    Pool.Add(i, c);
            }
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public bool Contains(Connection c)
        {
            foreach (KeyValuePair<Connection, IConnection> kvp in Pool)
            {
                if (kvp.Key.Equals(c))
                    return true;
            }
            return false;
        }

        public bool ContainsAndNotLocked(Connection c)
        {
            object o = new object();
            lock (Pool)
            {
                foreach (KeyValuePair<Connection, IConnection> kvp in Pool)
                {
                    if (kvp.Key.Equals(c))
                    {
                        if (kvp.Value.locked == false)
                            return true;
                        else
                        {

                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return false;
        }



        public IConnection Equals(Connection c)
        {
            foreach (KeyValuePair<Connection, IConnection> kvp in Pool)
            {
                if (kvp.Key.Equals(c))
                    return kvp.Value;
            }
            return null;
        }

        public IConnection GetConnection(Connection c)
        {
            object o = new object();
            lock (Pool)
            {
                foreach (KeyValuePair<Connection, IConnection> kvp in Pool)
                {
                    if (kvp.Key.Equals(c))
                    {
                        if (kvp.Value.locked == false)
                            return kvp.Value;
                        else
                        {

                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return null;
        }



        
        
        
        
        
    }
}

namespace Database
{
    public partial class DatabaseHelper
    {
        string server;
        public DatabaseHelper(string server)
        {
            this.server = server;
        }

        public delegate void PreExecuteAction();
        public delegate void PostExecuteAction();
        private PreExecuteAction _PreExecuteAction;
        private PostExecuteAction _PostExecuteAction;
        public void SetGlobalPreExecuteAction(PreExecuteAction pea)
        {
            _PreExecuteAction = pea;
        }
 
        public void SetGlobalPostExecuteAction(PostExecuteAction pea)
        {
            _PostExecuteAction = pea;
        }

        public DataTable ExecuteTable(Query q)
        {
            if (null != _PreExecuteAction)
                _PreExecuteAction();
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            if(null != _PostExecuteAction)
                _PostExecuteAction();
            return tbl;
        }
    }
}

namespace Database

    public static class FieldHelper
    {
        public static DataTable GetFieldTableInternal(string _server)
        {
            
            string sql = "select field,display_format,bold,display_name,hide,alignment,force_width,[pivot],pivot_area,wavg_field,pivot_group_interval,min_value,max_value,correction_mult,long_name,excel_format,data_dictionary_display,excel_col_width from Fields";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            DataTable table = q.ExecuteTable();
            return table;
        }

    }

--- FILE: Database\Generate.cs ---
namespace Database
{
    public class TableClass
    {
        private List<KeyValuePair<String, Type>> _fieldInfo = new List<KeyValuePair<String, Type>>();
        private string _className = String.Empty;


        public static string Generate(string assembly_name)
        {
            List<TableClass> tables = new List<TableClass>();

            
            Assembly a = Assembly.LoadFile(assembly_name);

            Type[] types = a.GetTypes();
            return Generate(types);
        }

        public static string Generate(Type type)
        {
            Type[] types = new Type[] { type };
            return Generate(types);
        }
        public static string Generate(Type[] types)
        {


            List<TableClass> tables = new List<TableClass>();
            

            

            
            foreach (Type t in types)
            {
                TableClass tc = new TableClass(t);
                tables.Add(tc);
            }

            
            string sql = "";
            foreach (TableClass table in tables)
            {
                sql += table.CreateTableScript() + Environment.NewLine;
            }


            foreach (TableClass table in tables)
            {
                foreach (KeyValuePair<String, Type> field in table.Fields)
                {
                    foreach (TableClass t2 in tables)
                    {
                        if (field.Value.Name == t2.ClassName)
                        {
                            

                            Console.WriteLine("GO");
                            Console.WriteLine("ALTER TABLE " + table.ClassName + " WITH NOCHECK");
                            Console.WriteLine("ADD CONSTRAINT FK_" + field.Key + " FOREIGN KEY (" + field.Key + ") REFERENCES " + t2.ClassName + "(ID)");
                            Console.WriteLine("GO");

                            sql += "GO" + Environment.NewLine;
                            sql += "ALTER TABLE " + table.ClassName + " WITH NOCHECK" + Environment.NewLine;
                            sql += "ADD CONSTRAINT FK_" + field.Key + " FOREIGN KEY (" + field.Key + ") REFERENCES " +
                                   t2.ClassName + "(ID)" + Environment.NewLine;
                            sql += "GO" + Environment.NewLine;


                        }
                    }
                }
            }


            return sql;
        }

        private Dictionary<Type, String> dataMapper
        {
            get
            {
                
                Dictionary<Type, String> dataMapper = new Dictionary<Type, string>();
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(int), "BIGINT");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(string), "NVARCHAR(500)");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(bool), "BIT");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(DateTime), "DATETIME");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(float), "FLOAT");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(decimal), "DECIMAL(18,0)");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(Guid), "UNIQUEIDENTIFIER");

                return dataMapper;
            }
        }

        public List<KeyValuePair<String, Type>> Fields
        {
            get { return this._fieldInfo; }
            set { this._fieldInfo = value; }
        }

        public string ClassName
        {
            get { return this._className; }
            set { this._className = value; }
        }

        public TableClass(Type t)
        {
            this._className = t.Name;

            foreach (PropertyInfo p in t.GetProperties())
            {
                KeyValuePair<String, Type> field = new KeyValuePair<String, Type>(p.Name, p.PropertyType);

                this.Fields.Add(field);
            }
        }

        public string CreateTableScript()
        {
            System.Text.StringBuilder script = new StringBuilder();

            script.AppendLine("CREATE TABLE " + this.ClassName);
            script.AppendLine("(");
            script.AppendLine("\t ID BIGINT,");
            for (int i = 0; i < this.Fields.Count; i++)
            {
                KeyValuePair<String, Type> field = this.Fields[i];

                if (dataMapper.ContainsKey(field.Value))
                {
                    script.Append("\t " + field.Key + " " + dataMapper[field.Value]);
                }
                else
                {
                    
                    script.Append("\t " + field.Key + " BIGINT");
                }

                if (i != this.Fields.Count - 1)
                {
                    script.Append(",");
                }

                script.Append(Environment.NewLine);
            }

            script.AppendLine(")");

            return script.ToString();
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Database\MySQL.cs ---
namespace Database
{
    public class MySQL : IConnection
    {
        private MySql.Data.MySqlClient.MySqlConnection _conn;

        public int id { get; set; }

        public string server { get; set; }
        public Nullable<int> port { get; set; }
        public string username { get; set; }
        public string password { get; set; }
        public string initial_catalog { get; set; }
        public bool integrated_security { get; set; }

        public void SetConnection(string server, Nullable<int> port, string username, string password, string initial_catalog, bool integrated_security)
        {


            this.server = server;
            this.port = port;
            this.username = username;
            this.password = password;
            this.initial_catalog = initial_catalog;
            this.integrated_security = integrated_security;

            MySqlConnectionStringBuilder builder = new MySqlConnectionStringBuilder();

            builder.Server = server;
            if (null != port)
                builder.Port = System.Convert.ToUInt32(port);

            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(initial_catalog))
                builder.Database = initial_catalog;
            if (null != username)
            {
                builder.UserID = username;
                builder.Password = password;
            }
            
            
            
            _conn = new MySqlConnection(builder.ConnectionString);
            locked = false;
        }

        public string GetConnectionString()
        {
            return _conn.ConnectionString;
        }

        public DataSet Execute(string sql, Dictionary<string, object> parameters)
        {
            return Execute(sql, parameters, true);
        }

        public void CancelQuery()
        {
            if (null != _execQuery)
                _execQuery.Cancel();
        }
        MySqlCommand _execQuery;



        public string GetDebugFromParms(string sql, Dictionary<string, object> param)
        {
            string body = DBUtils.GetDebugQuery(sql, param);

            return body;
        }

        
        
        
        

        public bool locked { get; internal set; }
        public DataSet Execute(string sql, Dictionary<string, object> parameters, bool refresh_parameters)
        {
           

                DataSet results = new DataSet();
                lock (_conn)
                {
                    locked = true;
                    _execQuery = new MySqlCommand(sql, _conn);

                    if (_conn.State != ConnectionState.Open)
                        _conn.Open();

                    MySqlDataAdapter da = new MySqlDataAdapter(_execQuery);
                    if (null != parameters)
                    {
                        foreach (KeyValuePair<string, object> kvp in parameters)
                        {
                            MySqlDbType type = DBUtils.FindMySQLDBType(kvp.Value, kvp.Key);
                            MySqlParameter sp = new MySqlParameter();
                            string pname = kvp.Key;
                            if (kvp.Key.Contains("<") && kvp.Key.Contains(">"))
                            {
                                pname = kvp.Key.Substring(0, kvp.Key.IndexOf("<"));
                            }

                            sp.MySqlDbType = type;
                            bool matched = false;
                            if (sp.MySqlDbType == MySqlDbType.VarChar && null != kvp.Value)
                            {
                                if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(kvp.Value.ToString()))
                                    sp.Value = DBNull.Value;
                            }
                            
                            sp.Value = (kvp.Value == null || (null != kvp.Value && kvp.Value.GetType() == typeof(double) && (Double.IsInfinity(System.Convert.ToDouble(kvp.Value)) || Double.IsNaN(System.Convert.ToDouble(kvp.Value))) || (null != kvp.Value && String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(kvp.Value.ToString())))) ? DBNull.Value : kvp.Value;
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            

                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            



                            
                            
                            

                            
                            

                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            

                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            

                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            

                            
                            
                            
                            if (kvp.Key.Contains("|OUT"))
                            {
                                pname = kvp.Key.Split('|')[0];
                                _execQuery.CommandText = _execQuery.CommandText.Replace(kvp.Key, pname);
                                sp.Direction = ParameterDirection.InputOutput;
                                if (kvp.Key.Split('|')[1].Contains(";") || (null != kvp.Value && kvp.Value.GetType() == typeof(string)))
                                {
                                    if (kvp.Key.Split('|')[1].Contains(";"))
                                    {
                                        sp.Size = Convert.ToInt32(kvp.Key.Split('|')[1].Replace("OUT;", ""));
                                    }
                                    else
                                        sp.Size = kvp.Value.ToString().Length;
                                    sp.MySqlDbType = MySqlDbType.VarChar;
                                }
                                
                            }
                            sp.ParameterName = pname;
                            da.SelectCommand.Parameters.Add(sp);
                        }
                    }
                    da.SelectCommand.CommandTimeout = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.DEFAULT_TIMEOUT;

                    DateTime start = DateTime.Now;


                    try
                    {
                        da.Fill(results);
                    }
                    catch (MySqlException n)
                    {
                        if (n.ToString().Contains("A severe error occurred on the current command.  The results, if any, should be discarded.") || n.ToString().Contains("Operation cancelled by user."))
                        {
                            
                        }
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        else
                        {
                            string debug_body = GetDebugFromParms(sql, parameters);
                            string temp = System.IO.Path.GetTempFileName();
                            System.IO.File.WriteAllText(temp, debug_body);
                            UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n, debug_body, null, null);
                            locked = false;
                            throw n;
                        }
                    }


                    double total_ms = (DateTime.Now - start).TotalMilliseconds;

                    if (refresh_parameters)
                    {
                        foreach (MySqlParameter p in da.SelectCommand.Parameters)
                        {
                            
                            parameters[p.ParameterName] = p.Value;
                        }
                    }
                    _execQuery = null;
                }
                locked = false;
                return results;
        }

        public bool Equals(IConnection c)
        {
            if ((object)c == null)
            {
                return false;
            }

            return this.GetConnectionString() == c.GetConnectionString();
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Database\Query.cs ---
namespace Database
{
    public class Query
    {
        private IConnection _conn;
        private string _sql;
        private Dictionary<string, object> _parameters = new Dictionary<string, object>();

        public Dictionary<string, object> Parameters { get { return _parameters; } }

        public Query(IConnection conn)
        {

        }

        public Query(string sql, IConnection conn)
        {
            _conn = conn;
            SetInitVariables(sql);

            
            
        }

        public Query(string sql, string server)
        {

            
            
            _conn = GetConnection(server);
            SetInitVariables(sql);
        }


        private string _path = null;

        private void SetInitVariables(string sql)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(sql))
                return;


            string sql_file_name = null;

            if (sql.Length >= 4 && sql.Substring(sql.Length - 4, 4).ToUpper() == ".SQL")
            {
                if (null == _path)
                    _path = System.IO.Path.GetDirectoryName(System.Reflection.Assembly.GetCallingAssembly().CodeBase);
                string sql_path = System.IO.Path.Combine(_path, "SQL");

                
                sql_file_name = System.IO.Path.Combine(sql_path, sql).Replace("file:\\", "");
                
                _sql = System.IO.File.ReadAllText(sql_file_name);
                _path = sql_file_name;
            }
            else
            {
                _sql = sql;
            }

            _query_name = _path;
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(_path))
                _query_name = _sql;
            if (_query_name.Length > 100)
                _query_name = _query_name.Substring(0, 100);

            
        }


        public void SetConnection(string server_or_label)
        {
            GetConnectionInternal(server_or_label);
            this._conn = GetConnection(server_or_label);
        }
        public Connection GetConnectionInternal(string server_or_label)
        {
            Connection c = null;
            if (server_or_label == Constants.Database.SQL_SERVER || server_or_label == Constants.Database.SQL_SERVER_LABEL)
            {
                c = new Connection(Constants.Database.SQL_SERVER, Constants.Database.SQL_SERVER_PORT, Constants.Database.SQL_SERVER_USERNAME, Constants.Database.SQL_SERVER_PASSWORD, Constants.Database.SQL_SERVER_INITIAL_CATALOG, Constants.Database.SQL_SERVER_INTEGRATED_SECURITY);
                c.SetIConnection(new SQL_Server());
            }
            else if (server_or_label == Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER || server_or_label.ToUpper() == Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_LABEL)
            {
                c = new Connection(Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER, Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_PORT, Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_USERNAME, Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_PASSWORD, Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_INITIAL_CATALOG, Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_INTEGRATED_SECURITY);
                c.SetIConnection(new SQL_Server());
            }
            else if (server_or_label.ToUpper() == Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_REPORTING_LABEL)
            {
                c = new Connection(Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER, Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_PORT, Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_USERNAME, Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_PASSWORD, Constants.Database.PISTON_SQL_SERVER_INITIAL_CATALOG, false);
                c.SetIConnection(new SQL_Server());
            }

            else if (server_or_label.ToUpper() == Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_LABEL)
            {
                c = new Connection(Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER, Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_PORT, Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_USERNAME, Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_PASSWORD, Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_INITIAL_CATALOG, Constants.Database.UAM_SQL_SERVER_INTEGRATED_SECURITY);
                c.SetIConnection(new SQL_Server());
            }
            else if (server_or_label.ToUpper() == Constants.Database.ADHOC_SQL_SERVER_LABEL)
            {
                c = new Connection(Constants.Database.ADHOC_SQL_SERVER, Constants.Database.ADHOC_SQL_SERVER_PORT, Constants.Database.ADHOC_SQL_SERVER_USERNAME, Constants.Database.ADHOC_SQL_SERVER_PASSWORD, Constants.Database.ADHOC_SQL_SERVER_INITIAL_CATALOG, Constants.Database.ADHOC_SQL_SERVER_INTEGRATED_SECURITY);
                c.SetIConnection(new SQL_Server());
            }

            else if (server_or_label == Constants.Database.SALUDA_MYSQL_SERVER)
            {
                c = new Connection(server_or_label, Constants.Database.SALUDA_MYSQL_SERVER_PORT, Constants.Database.SALUDA_MYSQL_USERNAME, Constants.Database.SALUDA_MYSQL_PASSWORD, Constants.Database.SALUDA_MYSQL_SERVER_INITIAL_CATALOG, Constants.Database.SALUDA_MYSQL_SERVER_INTEGRATED_SECURITY);
                c.SetIConnection(new MySQL());
            }

            else if (server_or_label == Constants.Database.SNOWFLAKE_PROD_LABEL)
            {
                c = new Connection(Constants.Database.SNOWFLAKE_PROD_SERVER, Constants.Database.SNOWFLAKE_PROD_PORT, Constants.Database.SNOWFLAKE_PROD_USERNAME, Constants.Database.SNOWFLAKE_PROD_PASSWORD, Constants.Database.SNOWFLAKE_PROD_INITIAL_CATALOG, Constants.Database.SNOWFLAKE_PROD_INTEGRATED_SECURITY);
                c.SetIConnection(new DBSnowflake.Snow_Flake());
            }
            else if (server_or_label == "<BLANK>")
            {
                
                
            }

            else
                throw new Exception("Undefined database");

            return c;
        }


            public IConnection GetConnection(string server)
        {

             Connection c = GetConnectionInternal(server);
            if (null == c) 
                return null;

             if (!ConnectionPool.GetInstance().ContainsAndNotLocked(c))
            {
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                

                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                _conn = c._conn;
                _conn.SetConnection(c._server, c._port, c._username, c._password, c._intial_catalog,c._integrated_security);
                
                _conn.id = ConnectionPool.GetInstance().Pool.Count + 1;
                ConnectionPool.GetInstance().AddConnection(c,c._conn);
            }
            return ConnectionPool.GetInstance().GetConnection(c);
            
              }

        public bool RefreshParametersOnCompletion = false;
        public void ApplyCommonVariables()
        {
            Dictionary<string, object> vars = UtilsLib.Clean.GetCommonVariables();
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, object> kvp in vars)
            {
                AddParameter(kvp.Key, kvp.Value);
            }
        }

        private List<string> _tableNames = null;
        public void SetTableNames(List<string> names)
        {
            _tableNames = names;
        }
        public void AddParameter(string parameter, object o)
        {
            if (parameter.ToUpper().Contains("" +
                                             "|OUT" +
                                             ""))
                RefreshParametersOnCompletion = true;
            _parameters.Add(parameter, o);
        }

        public void AddParameterDictionary<T>(Dictionary<string, T> parms,Dictionary<string,string> force_data_types)
        {
            if (null == parms)
                return;
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, T> kvp in parms)
            {
                string key = kvp.Key;
                if(null != force_data_types)
                {
                    if (force_data_types.ContainsKey(key))
                        key = $"{key}<{force_data_types[key]}>";
                }
                T o = kvp.Value;
                if (key.Length > 0 && key.Substring(0, 1) != "@")
                    key = "@" + key;
                if (null != o && o.GetType() == typeof(string))
                {
                    string var = o.ToString();
                    if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(var))
                        var = null;
                    o = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
                }
                if (!_parameters.ContainsKey(key))
                    _parameters.Add(key, o);
                else
                {
                    _parameters[key] = o;
                }
            }
        }


        public void SetSQL(string sql)
        {
            _sql = sql;
        }

        {
            get
            {
                if (null == _results)
                    return null;
                return _results.Tables[0].Columns.ToList().Select(n => n.ColumnName).ToList();
            }
        }

            if (null != tbl && tbl.Rows.Count == 1)
                return tbl.Rows[0];
            return null;
        }

        {

            if (a._sql != this._sql || a._parameters.Count != this._parameters.Count || a._conn != this._conn)
            {
                areEqual = false;
            }
            else
            {

                {

                    string key = kvp.Key;
                    object val2 = kvp.Value;
                    object val1 = this._parameters[key];

                    if (!this._parameters.ContainsKey(key))
                    {
                        equalSoFar = false;
                    }
                    else if ((val1 == null) && (val2 == null))
                    {
                        
                    }
                    else if ((val1 == null) || (val2 == null))
                    {
                        
                        equalSoFar = false;

                    else
                    {

                        

                        if (val1.Equals(val2))
                        {
                            
                        }

                        {
                            
                            
                            

                            if (val1.GetType() == val2.GetType())
                            { 

                                Type type_one = val1.GetType();
                                Type type_two = key.GetType();

                                if (type_one == typeof(List<int>))
                                {
                                    var one = val1 as IEnumerable<int>;
                                    var two = val2 as IEnumerable<int>;
                                    bool matches = one.SequenceEqual(two);
                                    if (matches)
                                    {

                                    var two = val2 as IEnumerable<string>;

        public void CancelQuery()
        {
            if (null != _conn)
            {
                _pa = null;
                _conn.CancelQuery();
                System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine("Query Canceled!");
            }
        }
        private string _query_name;

        
        

        
        
        
        
        public IETA _eta;
        public void SetETA(IETA eta)
        {
            _eta = eta;
        }
        public void ExecuteBatch(List<string> sqls, int batch_amt, IWriter _writer)
        {
            int last = 0;
            int items_left = sqls.Count - last;
            if(null == _eta)
                _eta = new ETA(sqls.Count, _writer);
            do
            {
                int to_insert = 0;
                if (items_left > batch_amt)
                    to_insert = batch_amt;
                else
                    to_insert = items_left;
                string sql = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, sqls.GetRange(last, to_insert));
                _sql = sql;
                Execute();
                last += to_insert;
                items_left = sqls.Count - last;
                _eta.IncrementAndReport(to_insert);
                
            } while (items_left != 0);

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            

            
            
            
            
            
        }


        private DataSet ExecuteInternal()
        {
            DateTime start = DateTime.Now;
            object o = new object();
            if (UseCache)
            {
                lock (DBCache.GetInstance().Pool)
                {
                    if (DBCache.GetInstance().Pool.Contains(this))
                    {
                        _results = DBCache.GetInstance().GetQuery(this)._results;
                        return _results;
                    }
                }
            }

            
            
            {

                _results = _conn.Execute(_sql, _parameters, RefreshParametersOnCompletion);
            }
            if (UseCache)
            {
                object q = new object();
                lock (DBCache.GetInstance().Pool)
                {
                    DBCache.GetInstance().Pool.Add(this);
                }
            }
            TimeSpan ts = DateTime.Now - start;
            double total_ms = ts.TotalMilliseconds;

            if (total_ms > 750)
            {
                string msg = String.Format("[LONG QUERY:{2}] - {0:0.00}s - {1}", ts.TotalSeconds, _query_name, _conn.id);
                System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine(msg);
            }

            if (null != _tableNames && _tableNames.Count == _results.Tables.Count)
            {
                int i = 0;
                foreach (DataTable tbl in _results.Tables)
                {
                    tbl.TableName = _tableNames[i];
                    i++;
                }
            }
            return _results;
        }
        DataSet _results;
        public bool RecordExists()
        {
            DataSet t = _conn.Execute(_sql, _parameters);
            if (t.Tables.Count == 0)
                return false;
            return t.Tables[0].Rows.Count > 0;
        }

        public T GetSingleRowValue<T>(string column)
        {
            return GetSingleRowValue<T>(column, 0);
        }

        public T GetSingleRowValue<T>(string column, int zero_based_table_index)
        {
            if (_results.Tables.Count != 0 && _results.Tables[zero_based_table_index].Rows.Count == 1)
            {
                if (null == column)
                    column = _results.Tables[zero_based_table_index].Columns[0].ColumnName;
                if (DBNull.Value == _results.Tables[zero_based_table_index].Rows[0][column])
                    return default(T);

                Type type2 = Nullable.GetUnderlyingType(typeof(T));
                Type type = typeof(T);
                object value = _results.Tables[zero_based_table_index].Rows[0][column];

                if (type2 != null)
                {
                    if (value == null)
                    {
                        return default(T);
                    }

                    type = type2;
                }

                return (T)Convert.ChangeType(value, type);
            }
            return default(T);
        }

        public T? GetSingleRowValueNullable<T>(string column, int table_number_zero_index = 0) where T : struct
        {

            if (null != _results && (_results.Tables.Count > table_number_zero_index && _results.Tables[table_number_zero_index].Rows.Count == 1 && DBNull.Value != _results.Tables[table_number_zero_index].Rows[0][column]))
            {
                if (null == column)
                    column = _results.Tables[0].Columns[0].ColumnName;

                T retVal = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(_results.Tables[table_number_zero_index].Rows[0][column], typeof(T));
                return retVal;
            }
            return null;

        }

        public List<T> ExecuteList<T>()
        {
            return ExecuteList<T>(null);
        }
        public List<T> ExecuteList<T>(string column, int table_num_zero_based = 0)
        {
            DataSet set = Execute();
            List<T> t = new List<T>();
            if (set.Tables.Count >= table_num_zero_based)
            {
                return set.Tables[table_num_zero_based].ToList<T>(column).ToList();
            }
            return t;
        }

        public Dictionary<Y, T> GetMultiRowDict<Y, T>(string key_col, string val_col)
        {
            DataSet set = Execute();
            if (null == set)
                return null;
            Dictionary<Y, T> t = new Dictionary<Y, T>();
            if (set.Tables.Count == 1)
            {
                foreach (DataRow row in set.Tables[0].Rows)
                {
                    Y key = (Y)System.Convert.ChangeType(row[key_col], typeof(Y));
                    T value = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(row[val_col], typeof(T));
                    if (!t.ContainsKey(key))
                        t.Add(key, value);
                }
            }
            return t;
        }

        public Dictionary<string, T> ExecuteDictSingleRow<T>()
        {
            DataSet set = Execute();
            Dictionary<string, T> t = new Dictionary<string, T>();
            if (null == set)
                return null;
            if (set.Tables.Count == 1 && set.Tables[0].Rows.Count == 1)
            {
                t = set.Tables[0].SingleRowToDict<T>();
            }
            return t;
        }


     
        public Dictionary<S, T> ExecuteDictRows<S,T>(string key_col,string val_col)
        {
            DataSet set = Execute();
            if (null == set)
                return null;
            Dictionary<S, T> t = new Dictionary<S, T>();
            if (set.Tables.Count == 1)
            {
                for (int i = 0; i != set.Tables[0].Rows.Count; i++)
                {
                    object raw = set.Tables[0].Rows[i][key_col];
                    if (DBNull.Value == raw)
                        continue;
                    T value = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(set.Tables[0].Rows[i][val_col], typeof(T));
                    if (null != value && value.ToString() == "")
                        value = default(T);
                    S key = (S)System.Convert.ChangeType(raw, typeof(S));
                    t.Add(key, value);
                }
            }
            return t;
        }

            Execute();
        }

        public void ExecuteAsync(PostAction pa)
        {
            _pa = pa;
            AsyncCallback acb = new AsyncCallback(AsyncCallBack);
            ExecuteQuery eq = Execute;
            IAsyncResult iar = eq.BeginInvoke(acb, null);

        }
        public void ExecuteSync(PostAction pa)
        {
            _pa = pa;
            DataSet set = this.Execute();
            if (null != _pa)
                pa(set);
        }

        private void AsyncCallBack(IAsyncResult ar)
        {
            if (null != _pa)
                _pa(_results);
        }

        public delegate DataSet ExecuteQueryNoReturn();
        public static Dictionary<Query, DataSet> BulkExecute(IEnumerable<Query> queries)
        {
            Dictionary<Query, DataSet> results = new Dictionary<Query, DataSet>();
            Dictionary<Query, Dictionary<ExecuteQueryNoReturn, IAsyncResult>> workers = new Dictionary<Query, Dictionary<ExecuteQueryNoReturn, IAsyncResult>>();

            foreach (Query q in queries)
            {
                ExecuteQueryNoReturn cow = q.Execute;
                Dictionary<ExecuteQueryNoReturn, IAsyncResult> tmp = new Dictionary<ExecuteQueryNoReturn, IAsyncResult>();
                tmp.Add(cow, cow.BeginInvoke(null, null));
                workers.Add(q, tmp);
            }

            foreach (KeyValuePair<Query, Dictionary<ExecuteQueryNoReturn, IAsyncResult>> kvp in workers)
            {
                foreach (KeyValuePair<ExecuteQueryNoReturn, IAsyncResult> iasc in kvp.Value)
                {
                    results.Add(kvp.Key, iasc.Key.EndInvoke(iasc.Value));
                }
            }
            return results;
        }

        public void InsertIfNoExists<T>(string source_table, T srcObj, string key = null)
        {
            

            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(key))
                key = GetPrimaryKey(source_table);

            
            System.Reflection.FieldInfo[] fields = srcObj.GetType().GetFields();
            System.Reflection.PropertyInfo[] properties = srcObj.GetType().GetProperties();

            List<string> columns = new List<string>();
            List<object> objs = new List<object>();
            List<string> parm = new List<string>();
            foreach (FieldInfo field in fields)
            {
                if (field.Name == key)
                {
                    bool key_exists = KeyExists(source_table, field.GetValue(srcObj));
                    if (key_exists)
                    {
                        return;
                    }
                }
                {
                    bool column_exists = ColumnExists(source_table, field.Name);
                    if (column_exists)
                    {
                        columns.Add(field.Name);
                        objs.Add(field.GetValue(srcObj));
                        parm.Add("@p" + columns.Count);
                    }
                }
            }

            foreach (PropertyInfo pi in properties)
            {
                if (pi.Name == key)
                {
                    bool key_exists = KeyExists(source_table, pi.GetValue(srcObj, null));
                    if (key_exists)
                    {
                        return;
                    }
                }
                {
                    bool column_exists = ColumnExists(source_table, pi.Name);
                    if (column_exists)
                    {
                        columns.Add(pi.Name);
                        objs.Add(pi.GetValue(srcObj, null));
                        parm.Add("@p" + columns.Count);
                    }
                }
            }


            if (columns.Count > 0)
            {
                string sql = String.Format("insert into {0} ([{1}]) values ({2})", source_table, String.Join("],[", columns), String.Join(",", parm));
                Query q = new Query(sql, _conn);
                foreach (object o in objs)
                {
                    q.AddParameter("@p" + (q._parameters.Count + 1), o);
                }
                q.Execute();
            }
        }

        public bool ColumnExists(string table, string column)
        {
            string sql = "select * from sys.columns where Name = @column and Object_ID = Object_ID(@table)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _conn);
            q.AddParameter("@table", table);
            q.AddParameter("@column", column);
            object o = q.ExecuteSingle<object>();
            return null != o;
        }


        public bool KeyExists(string table, object key)
        {
            string primary = GetPrimaryKey(table);
            string sql = String.Format("select max(1) from [{0}] where [{1}] = @key", table, primary);
            Query q = new Query(sql, _conn);
            q.AddParameter("@key", key);
            object o = q.ExecuteSingle<object>();
            return (DBNull.Value != o);
        }
        public string GetPrimaryKey(string table)
        {
            string sql_before = _sql;
            string sql = "SELECT column_name FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.KEY_COLUMN_USAGE WHERE OBJECTPROPERTY(OBJECT_ID(constraint_name), 'IsPrimaryKey') = 1 AND table_name = @table";
            Query q = new Query(sql, _conn);
            q.AddParameter("@table", table);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>();
        }

        public void ExecuteInsertUpdate(string table, string id_column, object id_value)
        {
            List<string> columns = new List<string>();
            List<string> values = new List<string>();
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, object> kvp in _parameters)
            {
                columns.Add(kvp.Key.Replace("@", ""));
                values.Add(kvp.Value == null ? "null" : kvp.Value.ToString());
            }
            bool exists = RecordExists(table, id_column, id_value);
            string sql = String.Format("insert into {0} ({1}) values (@{2})", table, String.Join(",", columns.ToArray()), String.Join(",@", columns.ToArray()));
            this._sql = sql;
            Execute();
        }

        public bool RecordExists(string table, string id_column, object id_value)
        {
            string sql = String.Format("select count(*) from {0} where {1} = @id", table, id_column, id_value);
            Query q = new Query(sql, _conn);
            q.AddParameter("@id", id_value);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<bool>();
        }

    }

namespace Database
{
    public static class QueryBuilder
    {

        public class SQLHelper
        {
            public List<string> lines;
            public string sql;
            public string error;
            public string sql_or_error
            {
                get
                {
                    if (null != error)
                        return error;
                    else
                        return sql;
                }
            }
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public static string SQLUpdate(string table, object[,] keys_obj, object[,] values_obj)
        {
            DataTable keys = UtilsLib.Excel.ArrayToDataTable(keys_obj, true, null);
            DataTable values = UtilsLib.Excel.ArrayToDataTable(values_obj, true, null);
            List<string> lines = Database.DBUtils.GenerateSQLStatements(table, keys.Columns.ToList().ToArray(), values, null).updates_raw_dog;
            string final_answer = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, lines);
            if (final_answer.Length > 256)
            {
                string file = System.IO.Path.Combine(System.IO.Path.GetTempPath(), System.IO.Path.GetRandomFileName()) + ".sql";
                System.IO.File.AppendAllText(file, final_answer);
                final_answer = file;
            }
            return final_answer;
        }


        public static SQLHelper SQLInsertValidate(object[,] range, string server, string table, bool validate)
        {
            Dictionary<string, Type> overrides = null;
            if (validate)
                overrides = Database.DBUtils.GetTableTypes(server, table);
            DataTable raw = UtilsLib.Excel.ArrayToDataTable(range, true, overrides);
            
            return Database.QueryBuilder.SQLInsertValidate(raw,server, table, true);
        }
    public static SQLHelper SQLInsertValidate(System.Data.DataTable raw, string server, string table, bool validate)
        {
            if (validate)
            {
                Dictionary<string, Type> overrides = Database.DBUtils.GetTableTypes(server, table);
                raw.ChangeColumnsAsNeeded(overrides);
                foreach (var ovr in overrides)
                {
                    if (raw.Columns.Contains(ovr.Key))
                    {
                        var can_change = raw.Columns[ovr.Key].ChangeDataType(ovr.Value);
                        if (!can_change.success)
                            return new SQLHelper { error = $"# Conversion Error: {can_change.message} #" };
                        
                    }
                }
                
            }

            return SQLInsert(table, raw);
        }


        public static string SQLInsertValidateExecute(string server, string table, object[,] range)
        {
            var h = Database.QueryBuilder.SQLInsertValidate(range, server, table, true);
            List<string> sqls = h.lines;
            Query q = new Query(null, server);
            q.ExecuteBatch(sqls, 1, null);
            return h.sql_or_error;
        }

         public static string SQLIn(object[] cells, string quote = "")
        {
            return Database.DBUtils.SQLIn(cells, true, quote);
        }
        public static SQLHelper SQLInsert(string table, DataTable raw)
        {
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            var sqls = Database.DBUtils.GenerateInsertStatements(table, raw, true);
            SQLHelper sqh = new SQLHelper();
            if (true)
            {
                string final_answer = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, sqls.inserts_raw_dog);
                if (final_answer.Length > 256)
                {
                    string file = System.IO.Path.Combine(System.IO.Path.GetTempPath(), System.IO.Path.GetRandomFileName()) + ".sql";
                    System.IO.File.AppendAllText(file, final_answer);
                    final_answer = file;
                    sqh.sql = final_answer;
                }
                else
                {
                    sqh.sql = final_answer;
                }
            }

            sqh.lines = sqls.inserts_raw_dog;
            GC.Collect();
            return sqh;
        }
    }

namespace Database
{
    public class RRHelper
    {

        public class FormatHelper : IFormatHelper
        {
            public string column { get; set; }
            public string format { get; set; }
            public string nice_name { get; set; }
        }

        public static List<IFormatHelper> GetFormats(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select field,field [nice_name],display_format from Fields where display_format is not null";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            DataTable t = q.ExecuteTable();
            List<IFormatHelper> fhl = new List<IFormatHelper>();
            foreach (DataRow row in t.Rows)
            {
                FormatHelper fm = new FormatHelper();
                fm.column = row["field"].ToString();
                fm.format = row["display_format"].ToString();
                if (DBNull.Value != row["nice_name"])
                    fm.nice_name = row["nice_name"].ToString();
                fhl.Add(fm);
            }
            return fhl;
        }
    }
}

namespace Database
{
    public class SQL_Server : IConnection
    {
        private SqlConnection _conn;

        public string server { get; set; }
        public Nullable<int> port { get; set; }
        public string username { get; set; }
        public string password { get; set; }
        public string initial_catalog { get; set; }
        public bool integrated_security { get; set; }

        public int id { get; set; }


        private static ClientCredential _clientCredential;

        static void InitializeAzureKeyVaultProviders()
        {
            string s = "lock";
            lock (s)
            {
                if (null == _clientCredential)
                {
                    
                    System.Net.ServicePointManager.SecurityProtocol = System.Net.SecurityProtocolType.Tls12;

                    
                    _clientCredential = new ClientCredential(CommonInterfaces.Constants.BADGER.APPLICATION_ID, CommonInterfaces.Constants.BADGER.APPLICATION_SECRET);

                    SqlColumnEncryptionAzureKeyVaultProvider azureKeyVaultProvider = new SqlColumnEncryptionAzureKeyVaultProvider(GetToken);
                    


                    Dictionary<string, SqlColumnEncryptionKeyStoreProvider> providers = new Dictionary<string, SqlColumnEncryptionKeyStoreProvider>();

                    providers.Add(SqlColumnEncryptionAzureKeyVaultProvider.ProviderName, azureKeyVaultProvider);
                    SqlConnection.RegisterColumnEncryptionKeyStoreProviders(providers);
                }
            }
        }

        public static bool dlls_copied = false;
        public static void CopyNeededDLLS()
        {
            var random = new Random().Next(1, 1000);
            if (random == 4)
            {
                char s = Microsoft.Identity.Client.TokenSource.Broker.ToString().ToCharArray()[0];
                char t = Azure.Core.ContentType.ApplicationOctetStream.ToString().ToCharArray()[0];
                Azure.Identity.AuthenticationFailedException e = new Azure.Identity.AuthenticationFailedException(s.ToString());
                char q = System.Runtime.CompilerServices.Unsafe.AreSame<char>(ref s, ref t).ToString().ToCharArray()[0];
                System.Runtime.CompilerServices.Unsafe.AreSame<char>(ref s, ref q);
                System.Memory<string> m = new System.Memory<string>();
                int ms = m.Length;

                Console.WriteLine(e);
                Console.WriteLine(ms);
                Console.WriteLine(q);
                
                dlls_copied = true;
                if (s.ToString() == "thrifty" || ms == -1)
                    return;
                else
                    return;
            }

        }


        public async static Task<string> GetToken(string authority, string resource, string scope)
        {
            var authContext = new AuthenticationContext(authority);
            AuthenticationResult result = await authContext.AcquireTokenAsync(resource, _clientCredential);

            if (result == null)
                throw new InvalidOperationException("Failed to obtain the access token");
            return result.AccessToken;
        }
        public void SetConnection(string server, Nullable<int> port, string username, string password, string initial_catalog, bool integrated_security)
        {

            SqlConnectionStringBuilder builder = new SqlConnectionStringBuilder();

            this.server = server;
            this.port = port;
            this.username = username;
            this.password = password;
            this.initial_catalog = initial_catalog;
            this.integrated_security = integrated_security;
            builder.MultipleActiveResultSets = false;

            builder.DataSource = server;
            if (null != port)
                builder.DataSource += "," + port;

            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(initial_catalog))
                builder.InitialCatalog = initial_catalog;
            
            
            
            
            




            if (integrated_security)
            {
                InitializeAzureKeyVaultProviders();
                builder.ColumnEncryptionSetting = SqlConnectionColumnEncryptionSetting.Enabled;
                builder.Authentication = SqlAuthenticationMethod.ActiveDirectoryInteractive;
            }
            else
            {
                
                {
                    builder.UserID = username;
                    builder.Password = password;
                }

            }
            
            
            



            builder.ApplicationName = CommonInterfaces.Globals.APPLICATION_NAME;
           if (!dlls_copied)
                CopyNeededDLLS();
            _conn = new SqlConnection(builder.ConnectionString);
            locked = false;
        }

        public string GetConnectionString()
        {
            return _conn.ConnectionString;
        }

        public DataSet Execute(string sql, Dictionary<string, object> parameters)
        {
            return Execute(sql, parameters, true);
        }

        public void CancelQuery()
        {
            if (null != _execQuery)
                _execQuery.Cancel();
        }
        SqlCommand _execQuery;



        public string GetDebugFromParms(string sql, Dictionary<string, object> param)
        {
            string body = DBUtils.GetDebugQuery(sql, param);

            return body;
        }


        public bool locked { get; internal set; }

        public DataSet Execute(string sql, Dictionary<string, object> parameters, bool refresh_parameters)
        {
            return ExecuteInternal(sql, parameters, refresh_parameters);
        }
        public DataSet ExecuteInternal(string sql, Dictionary<string, object> parameters, bool refresh_parameters)
        {
            DataSet results = new DataSet();

            lock (_conn)
            {
                locked = true;
                _execQuery = new SqlCommand(sql, _conn);

                if (_conn.State != ConnectionState.Open)
                    _conn.Open();

                SqlDataAdapter da = new SqlDataAdapter(_execQuery);
                if (null != parameters)
                {
                    foreach (KeyValuePair<string, object> kvp in parameters)
                    {
                        string pname = kvp.Key;

                        
                        
                        if (pname == "@asset_id")
                        {
                            pname = "@asset_id<varchar>";
                        }
                        
                        
                        if (pname == "@phone")
                        {
                            pname = "@phone<varchar>";
                        }
                        
                        if (pname == "@phone_number")
                        {
                            pname = "@phone_number<varchar>";
                        }
                        
                        if (pname == "@max_id")
                        {
                            pname = "@max_id<bigint>";
                        }

                        SqlDbType type = DBUtils.FindDBType(kvp.Value, pname);
                        SqlParameter sp = new SqlParameter();

                        if (pname.Contains("<") && pname.Contains(">"))
                        {
                            pname = pname.Substring(0, pname.IndexOf("<"));
                        }

                        sp.SqlDbType = type;
                        bool matched = false;
                        if (sp.SqlDbType == SqlDbType.VarChar && null != kvp.Value)
                        {
                            if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(kvp.Value.ToString()))
                                sp.Value = DBNull.Value;
                        }
                        if (type != SqlDbType.Structured)
                            sp.Value = (kvp.Value == null
                                        || (null != kvp.Value && kvp.Value.GetType() == typeof(double) &&
                                            (Double.IsInfinity(System.Convert.ToDouble(kvp.Value)) || Double.IsNaN(System.Convert.ToDouble(kvp.Value))))
                                        || (null != kvp.Value && String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(kvp.Value.ToString())))
                                ? DBNull.Value
                                : kvp.Value;

                        if (null != kvp.Value && type == SqlDbType.Structured)
                        {
                            DataTable parm = new DataTable();
                            if ((kvp.Value.GetType() == typeof(List<int>)))
                            {
                                parm.Columns.Add("Item", typeof(int));
                                sp.TypeName = "IntList";
                                foreach (int o in (List<int>)kvp.Value)
                                    parm.Rows.Add(o);
                            }
                            if ((kvp.Value.GetType() == typeof(List<DateTime>)))
                            {
                                parm.Columns.Add("Item", typeof(DateTime));
                                sp.TypeName = "DateList";
                                foreach (DateTime o in (List<DateTime>)kvp.Value)
                                    parm.Rows.Add(o);
                            }
                            if ((kvp.Value.GetType() == typeof(List<long>)))
                            {
                                parm.Columns.Add("Item", typeof(long));
                                sp.TypeName = "LongList";
                                foreach (long o in (List<long>)kvp.Value)
                                    parm.Rows.Add(o);
                            }
                            if (kvp.Value.GetType() == typeof(List<string>))
                            {
                                string typename = "StringList";
                                bool do_not_add = false;

                                if (((List<string>)kvp.Value).Count == 1)
                                {
                                    if (((List<string>)kvp.Value)[0] == "#intlist#")
                                    {
                                        parm.Columns.Add("Item", typeof(int));
                                        typename = "IntList";
                                        do_not_add = true;
                                    }
                                    else if (((List<string>)kvp.Value)[0] == "#longlist#")
                                    {
                                        parm.Columns.Add("Item", typeof(long));
                                        typename = "LongList";
                                        do_not_add = true;
                                    }
                                    else if (((List<string>)kvp.Value)[0] == "#datelist#")
                                    {
                                        parm.Columns.Add("Item", typeof(DateTime));
                                        typename = "DateList";
                                        do_not_add = true;
                                    }
                                }
                                if (parm.Columns.Count == 0)
                                {
                                    parm.Columns.Add("Item", typeof(string));
                                }
                                int max_len = 0;
                                if (!do_not_add)
                                {
                                    foreach (string o in (List<string>)kvp.Value)
                                    {
                                        if (parm.Columns[0].DataType == typeof(string) && !String.IsNullOrEmpty(o) && o.Length > max_len)
                                            max_len = o.Length;
                                        parm.Rows.Add(o);
                                    }
                                }
                                sp.TypeName = typename;
                            }

                            sp.Value = parm;
                            sp.Direction = ParameterDirection.Input;
                        }
                        if (kvp.Key.Contains("|OUT"))
                        {
                            pname = kvp.Key.Split('|')[0];
                            _execQuery.CommandText = _execQuery.CommandText.Replace(kvp.Key, pname);
                            sp.Direction = ParameterDirection.InputOutput;
                            if (kvp.Key.Split('|')[1].Contains(";") || (null != kvp.Value && kvp.Value.GetType() == typeof(string)))
                            {
                                if (kvp.Key.Split('|')[1].Contains(";"))
                                {
                                    sp.Size = Convert.ToInt32(kvp.Key.Split('|')[1].Replace("OUT;", ""));
                                }
                                else
                                    sp.Size = kvp.Value.ToString().Length;
                                sp.SqlDbType = SqlDbType.VarChar;
                            }
                        }
                        sp.ParameterName = pname;
                        da.SelectCommand.Parameters.Add(sp);
                    }
                }
                da.SelectCommand.CommandTimeout = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.DEFAULT_TIMEOUT;

                DateTime start = DateTime.Now;

                try
                {
                    da.Fill(results);
                }
                catch (Exception n)
                {
                    if (n.ToString().Contains("A severe error occurred on the current command.  The results, if any, should be discarded.")
                        || n.ToString().Contains("Operation cancelled by user."))
                    {
                        
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        string debug_body = GetDebugFromParms(sql, parameters);
                        UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n, debug_body, new object[] { parameters });
                        locked = false;
                        throw;
                    }
                }

                double total_ms = (DateTime.Now - start).TotalMilliseconds;

                if (refresh_parameters)
                {
                    foreach (SqlParameter p in da.SelectCommand.Parameters)
                    {
                        parameters[p.ParameterName] = p.Value;
                    }
                }
                _execQuery = null;
            }
            locked = false;
            return results;
        }

        public bool Equals(IConnection c)
        {
            if ((object)c == null)
            {
                return false;
            }

            return this.GetConnectionString() == c.GetConnectionString();
        }
    }
}
