namespace Database
{
    public static class DBUtils
    {


       
        public static SqlDbType FindDBType(object o, string pname)
        {

            SqlDbType def = SqlDbType.VarChar;
            if (null == o)
                return def;
            Double d;
            Type t = o.GetType();
            if (null != pname && pname.Contains("<") && pname.Contains(">"))
            {
                string which = pname.Substring(pname.IndexOf("<"), pname.Length - pname.IndexOf("<")).Replace("<", "").Replace(">", "").ToLower();
                if (which == "string")
                    return SqlDbType.VarChar;
                if (which == "varchar")
                    return SqlDbType.VarChar;
                if (which == "int")
                    return SqlDbType.Int;
                if (which == "float")
                    return SqlDbType.Float;
                if (which == "date")
                    return SqlDbType.Date;
                if (which == "datetime")
                    return SqlDbType.DateTime;

            }
            if (t == typeof(double) || t == typeof(int))
                def = SqlDbType.Float;
            else if (t == typeof(bool))
                def = SqlDbType.Bit;
            else if (t == typeof(DateTime))
            {
                DateTime dt = System.Convert.ToDateTime(o);
                if (dt.Year >= 2079)
                    def = SqlDbType.Date;
                else if (dt.Year <= 1752)
                    def = SqlDbType.DateTime2;
                else
                    def = SqlDbType.DateTime;
            }
            else if (t == typeof(DateTimeOffset))
            {
                def = SqlDbType.DateTimeOffset;
            }
            else if (t == typeof(byte[]))
                def = SqlDbType.Binary;
            else if (t == typeof(long))
                def = SqlDbType.Float;
            else if (t.Namespace.Contains("Collections"))
                def = SqlDbType.Structured;
            else if (!(o.ToString().Contains("E") || (o.ToString().Contains("e"))) && Double.TryParse(o.ToString(), out d))
            {
                if (!UtilsLib.Validate.IsCusip(o.ToString())) 
                {

                    if (o.ToString() == "Infinity" || o.ToString().Contains("."))
                    {
                        if (Math.Abs(d) > SqlInt32.MaxValue.ToSqlDouble())
                        {
                            def = SqlDbType.Float;
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        if (t != typeof(string)) 
                            def = SqlDbType.Int;
                    }
                }
            }
            return def;
        }



        public static MySqlDbType FindMySQLDBType(object o, string pname)
        {

            MySqlDbType def = MySqlDbType.VarChar;
            if (null == o)
                return def;
            Double d;
            Type t = o.GetType();
            if (null != pname && pname.Contains("<") && pname.Contains(">"))
            {
                string which = pname.Substring(pname.IndexOf("<"), pname.Length - pname.IndexOf("<")).Replace("<", "").Replace(">", "").ToLower();
                if (which == "string")
                    return MySqlDbType.VarChar;
                if (which == "varchar")
                    return MySqlDbType.VarChar;
                if (which == "int")
                    return MySqlDbType.Int32;
                if (which == "float")
                    return MySqlDbType.Float;
                if (which == "date")
                    return MySqlDbType.Date;
                if (which == "datetime")
                    return MySqlDbType.DateTime;

            }
            if (t == typeof(double) || t == typeof(int))
                def = MySqlDbType.Float;
            else if (t == typeof(bool))
                def = MySqlDbType.Bit;
            else if (t == typeof(DateTime))
            {
                DateTime dt = System.Convert.ToDateTime(o);
                if (dt.Year >= 2079)
                    def = MySqlDbType.Date;
                else
                    def = MySqlDbType.DateTime;
            }
            else if (t == typeof(byte[]))
                def = MySqlDbType.Binary;
            else if (t == typeof(long))
                def = MySqlDbType.Float;
            
            
            else if (!(o.ToString().Contains("E") || (o.ToString().Contains("e"))) && Double.TryParse(o.ToString(), out d))
            {
                if (!UtilsLib.Validate.IsCusip(o.ToString())) 
                {

                    if (o.ToString() == "Infinity" || o.ToString().Contains(".") || Math.Abs(d) > SqlInt32.MaxValue.ToSqlDouble())
                        def = MySqlDbType.Float;
                    else
                    {
                        def = MySqlDbType.Int32;
                    }
                }
            }
            return def;
        }


        public static string FindDBTypeForSQL(Type t)
        {

            SqlDbType def = SqlDbType.VarChar;
            Double d;

            if (t == typeof(string))
                return "varchar(max)";
            if (t == typeof(int))
                return "int";
            if (t == typeof(DateTime))
                return "datetime";
            if (t == typeof(float))
                return "float";
            if (t == typeof(double))
                return "float";
            else
                return "varchar(max)";

        }

        public static Type FindNETTypeForSQL(string db_type)
        {
            if (db_type.Contains("char"))
                return typeof(string);
            else if (db_type.Contains("bigint"))
                return typeof(long);
            else if (db_type.Contains("int"))
                return typeof(int);
            else if (db_type.Contains("bit"))
                return typeof(bool);
            else if (db_type.Contains("numeric") || db_type.Contains("float") || db_type.Contains("decimal"))
                return typeof(double);
            else if (db_type.Contains("date"))
                return typeof(DateTime);
            else if (db_type.Contains("xml"))
                return typeof(string);

            throw new Exception("No Match: " + db_type);
        }

        public static string GetDebugQuery(string sql, Dictionary<string, object> param)
        {
            string body = "";
            List<string> parm = new List<string>();
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, object> kvp in param)
            {
                string p = String.Format("[{0}] - {1}", kvp.Key, kvp.Value);
                Type t = typeof(object);
                if (null != kvp.Value)
                    t = kvp.Value.GetType();

                string write_string = UtilsLib.DB.DbWriteString(t, kvp.Key, kvp.Value);
                string type = Database.DBUtils.FindDBQueryType(kvp.Value, kvp.Key);
                string new_str = String.Format("declare {0} {1} = {2}", kvp.Key, type.ToLower(), write_string);
                if (type.Contains("dbo."))
                {
                    new_str = String.Format("declare {0} {1}", kvp.Key, type.ToLower());
                    if (write_string != "null")
                        new_str += "\n" + write_string + "\n";
                }

                parm.Add(new_str);
            }
            body += "--Parameters: " + Environment.NewLine + String.Join("\n", parm.ToArray()) + "\n";
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(sql))
                body += "\n\n--SQL:\n" + sql + "\n\n\n";
            return body;
        }

        public static Type FindNETType(object o)
        {
            Type def = typeof(string);
            if (null == o || (null != o && o.ToString() == ""))
                return def;

            double test;
            string str = o.ToString();
            if (Double.TryParse(str, out test))
            {
                return typeof(double);
            }
            return def;
        }

        public static string FindDBQueryType(object o, string pname)
        {
            var v = DBUtils.FindDBType(o, pname);
            string type = v.ToString();
            if (v == SqlDbType.Structured)
            {
                if (null != o && typeof(List<string>) == o.GetType())
                {
                    type = "dbo.StringList";
                }
                if (null != o && typeof(List<int>) == o.GetType())
                {
                    type = "dbo.IntList";
                }
                if (null != o && typeof(List<long>) == o.GetType())
                {
                    type = "dbo.LongList";
                }
                if (null != o && typeof(List<DateTime>) == o.GetType())
                {
                    type = "dbo.DateList";
                }
            }
            if (v == SqlDbType.VarChar)
                return "varchar(max)";
            return type;
        }


        public class LazyResults
        {
            public List<Query> updated = new List<Query>();
            public List<Query> inserted = new List<Query>();
            public List<Query> deleted = new List<Query>();
            public DataTable results = null;
        }
        public static LazyResults LazyTableUpdater(string server, string table, IEnumerable<DataColumn> keys, DataTable values, bool check_if_exists, Dictionary<string, string> next_ids_to_populate,List<string> cols_to_return_on_insert)
        {
            LazyResults lr = new LazyResults();
            var sqls = GenerateSQLStatements(table, keys, values, next_ids_to_populate, cols_to_return_on_insert);
            

            if (sqls.updates_only.Count != sqls.inserts_only.Count || sqls.inserts_all.Count != sqls.updates_all.Count || sqls.deletes_only.Count + sqls.inserts_only.Count != sqls.updates_all.Count) 
            {
                throw new Exception("Should never happen");
            }

            foreach (Query del in sqls.deletes_only)
            {
                del.SetConnection(server);
                del.Execute();

                lr.deleted.Add(del);
            }


            for (int i = 0; i != sqls.updates_only.Count; i++)
            {
                bool exists = true;
                if (check_if_exists)
                {
                    Query ins = sqls.exists_only[i];
                    ins.SetConnection(server);
                    exists = ins.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count != 0;
                }
                Query q = null;
                if (exists)
                {
                    q = sqls.updates_only[i];
                    lr.updated.Add(q);
                }
                else
                {
                    q = sqls.inserts_only[i];
                    lr.inserted.Add(q);
                    if (null != next_ids_to_populate)
                    {
                        foreach (KeyValuePair<string, string> kvp in next_ids_to_populate)
                        {
                            int next_id = Database.Common.GetNextId(server, kvp.Value);
                            q.Parameters["@" + kvp.Key] = next_id;
                        }
                    }
                }

                q.SetConnection(server);
                DataTable results = q.ExecuteTable();
                if (null != results && null == lr.results)
                    lr.results = results.Clone();
                if (null != lr.results)
                {
                    foreach (DataRow row in results.Rows)
                    {
                        lr.results.Rows.Add(row.ItemArray);
                    }
                }
            }
            return lr;
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            
        }




        public static int LazyTableInsertUpdater(string server, string table2update, string csv_keys, DataRow row, List<DataColumn> cols_modified, Dictionary<string, string> key_remap = null, List<string> do_not_update_insert = null, Dictionary<string, string> next_ids_to_generate = null, List<string> columns_to_return_on_insert = null)
        {
            if (row.Table.Rows.Count != 1)
                throw new Exception("Should never happen");


            DataTable values = row.Table.CopyAndTrimColumns(cols_modified);
            DataTable keys = row.Table.CopyAndTrimColumns(csv_keys);
            if (null != key_remap)
            {
                foreach (KeyValuePair<string, string> kvp in key_remap)
                {
                    if (keys.Columns.Contains(kvp.Key))
                        keys.Columns[kvp.Key].Rename(kvp.Value);
                    if (values.Columns.Contains(kvp.Key))
                        values.Columns[kvp.Key].Rename(kvp.Value);
                }
            }
            if (null != do_not_update_insert)
            {
                foreach (string col in do_not_update_insert)
                {
                    if (values.Columns.Contains(col))
                        values.Columns.Remove(col);
                }
            }
            Database.DBUtils.LazyTableUpdater(server, table2update, keys.Columns.ToList(), values, true, next_ids_to_generate, columns_to_return_on_insert);
            row.AcceptChanges();

            return 1;
        }
        public class GeneratedSQLStatements
        {
            public List<string> updates_raw_dog;
            public List<string> inserts_raw_dog;

            public List<Query> inserts_all;
            public List<Query> inserts_only;

            public List<Query> updates_all;
            public List<Query> updates_only;

            public List<Query> deletes_all;
            public List<Query> deletes_only;

            public List<Query> exists_all;
            public List<Query> exists_only;
        }



        public static GeneratedSQLStatements GenerateSQLStatements(string table, IEnumerable<DataColumn> keys, DataTable values, Dictionary<string, string> next_ids_to_populate,List<string> insert_output_columns = null)
        {
            List<string> sqls = new List<string>();


            List<string> sets = new List<string>();
            List<string> sets_p = new List<string>();

            List<Query> updates_only = new List<Query>();
            List<Query> updates_all = new List<Query>();

            List<Query> exists_only = new List<Query>();
            List<Query> exists_all = new List<Query>();

            List<Query> deletes_only = new List<Query>();
            List<Query> deletes_all = new List<Query>();

            List<Query> inserts_only = new List<Query>();
            List<Query> inserts_all = new List<Query>();

            Dictionary<string, object> dict = new Dictionary<string, object>();


            List<string> wheres = new List<string>();
            List<string> wheres_p = new List<string>();
            List<DataColumn> where_cols = new List<DataColumn>();

            int value_rows = values.Rows.Count;
            foreach (DataColumn key in keys)
            {
                if (key.Table.Rows.Count != value_rows)
                    throw new Exception("Keys & Value Rows Mismatch");
            }

            foreach (DataColumn col in keys)
            {
                where_cols.Add(col);
            }

            int row_num = 0;
            string any_column = null;
            foreach (DataRow row in values.Rows)
            {
                string delete_p = null;
                Dictionary<string, object> row_obj = row.ToDictionary<object>();
                Dictionary<string, object> row_obj_insert = row.ToDictionary<object>();
                foreach (DataColumn col in keys)
                {
                    if (!row_obj_insert.ContainsKey(col.ColumnName))
                    {


                        
                        object o = col.Table.Rows[row_num].GetRowValueEvenIfDeleted(col);
                        if (null != o && DBNull.Value != o || (null != next_ids_to_populate && next_ids_to_populate.ContainsKey(col.ColumnName)))
                            row_obj_insert.Add(col.ColumnName, o);
                        else
                        {

                        }
                    }
                }

                foreach (DataColumn where in where_cols)
                {

                    DataRow where_row = where.Table.Rows[row_num];
                    
                    object rowval = where_row.GetRowValueEvenIfDeleted(where);

                    string colStr = UtilsLib.DB.DbWriteString(where.DataType, null, rowval);
                    wheres.Add(String.Format("[{0}] = {1}", where.ColumnName, colStr));
                    if (!dict.ContainsKey(where.ColumnName))
                        dict.Add(where.ColumnName, rowval);
                    else
                    {

                    }

                    
                    
                    

                    
                    
                    
                    
                    

                    
                    
                    
                    
                    

                    wheres_p.Add(String.Format("[{0}] = @{1}", where.ColumnName, where.ColumnName));

                    if (null == any_column)
                        any_column = where.ColumnName;
                }


                foreach (DataColumn valCol in values.Columns)
                {
                    object rowval = row.GetRowValueEvenIfDeleted(valCol);

                    string valString = UtilsLib.DB.DbWriteString(valCol.DataType, null, rowval);
                    sets.Add("[" + valCol.ColumnName + "] = " + valString);
                    sets_p.Add("[" + valCol.ColumnName + "] = @" + valCol.ColumnName);
                    if (!dict.ContainsKey(valCol.ColumnName))
                        dict.Add(valCol.ColumnName, rowval);
                }

                string sql = String.Format("update [{0}] set {1} where {2}", table, String.Join(", ", sets.ToArray()), String.Join(" and ", wheres.ToArray()));
                string sql_p = String.Format("update [{0}] set {1} where {2}", table, String.Join(", ", sets_p.ToArray()), String.Join(" and ", wheres_p.ToArray()));
                string exist_p = String.Format("select top 1 [{2}] from [{0}] where {1}", table, String.Join(" and ", wheres_p.ToArray()), any_column);
                if (row.RowState == DataRowState.Deleted)
                    delete_p = String.Format("delete from [{0}] where {1}", table, String.Join(" and ", wheres_p.ToArray()), any_column);


                sqls.Add(sql);


                Query delete = ProcessLazyQuery(delete_p, dict);
                Query update = ProcessLazyQuery(sql_p, dict);
                Query exists = ProcessLazyQuery(exist_p, dict);


                Query insert = GenerateParamaterizedInsertStatementQuery(table, row_obj_insert, null, insert_output_columns);

                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(delete_p))
                    deletes_only.Add(delete);
                else
                {
                    updates_only.Add(update);
                    inserts_only.Add(insert);
                    exists_only.Add(exists);
                }

                inserts_all.Add(insert);
                deletes_all.Add(delete);
                updates_all.Add(update);
                exists_all.Add(exists);


                wheres.Clear();
                sets.Clear();

                row_num++;

            }

            GeneratedSQLStatements d = new GeneratedSQLStatements();
            d.updates_raw_dog = sqls;
            d.deletes_only = deletes_only;
            d.deletes_all = deletes_all;
            d.updates_all = updates_all;
            d.updates_only = updates_only;
            d.inserts_all = inserts_all;
            d.inserts_only = inserts_only;
            d.exists_all = exists_all;
            d.exists_only = exists_only;
            return d;
        }

        public static Query ProcessLazyQuery(string sql, Dictionary<string, object> list)
        {
            Query q = new Query(sql, "<BLANK>");
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, object> kvp in list)
            {
                q.AddParameter($"@{kvp.Key}", kvp.Value);
            }
            return q;
        }


        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        



        public static bool ColumnExistsInServer(string server, string table, string column)
        {
            
            string sql = "SELECT COLUMN_NAME, DATA_TYPE FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS where TABLE_NAME = @table and COLUMN_NAME = @COLUMN";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@table", table);
            q.AddParameter("@column", column);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }


        public static string GenerateParamaterizedInsertStatement<T>(string destTable, Dictionary<string, T> raw, string server_if_you_want_to_only_include_columns = null,List<string> insert_output_columns = null)
        {
            List<string> cols = new List<string>();
            List<string> vals = new List<string>();
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, T> col in raw)
            {
                if (null != server_if_you_want_to_only_include_columns)
                {
                    bool exists = ColumnExistsInServer(server_if_you_want_to_only_include_columns, destTable, col.Key);
                    if (!exists)
                        continue;
                }

                cols.Add(col.Key);
                if (null == col.Value)
                    vals.Add(null);
                else
                    vals.Add(col.Value.ToString());
            }


            string insert = String.Format("insert into [{0}]  ([{1}]) values (@{2})", destTable, String.Join("],[", cols.ToArray()), String.Join(", @", cols.ToArray()));
            if(null != insert_output_columns && insert_output_columns.Count > 0)
            {
                insert = String.Format("insert into [{0}] ([{1}]) output inserted.[{3}] values (@{2})", destTable, String.Join("],[", cols.ToArray()), String.Join(", @", cols.ToArray()), String.Join("],inserted.[", insert_output_columns.ToArray()));
            }
            return insert;
        }

        public static Query GenerateParamaterizedInsertStatementQuery<T>(string destTable, Dictionary<string, T> raw, string server_if_you_want_to_only_include_columns = null,List<string> cols_to_return_on_insert = null)
        {
            string ssql = Database.DBUtils.GenerateParamaterizedInsertStatement<T>(destTable, raw, server_if_you_want_to_only_include_columns, cols_to_return_on_insert);
            Query q = new Query(ssql, "<BLANK>");
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(server_if_you_want_to_only_include_columns))
                q.SetConnection(server_if_you_want_to_only_include_columns);

            q.AddParameterDictionary<T>(raw, null);
            return q;
        }

        public static GeneratedSQLStatements GenerateInsertStatements(string destTable, DataTable raw, bool ignore_blank_rows, bool RawDogOnly = false)
        {
            GeneratedSQLStatements gss = new GeneratedSQLStatements();
            List<string> cols = new List<string>();
            List<string> rows = new List<string>();
            List<Query> qs = new List<Query>();
            foreach (DataColumn col in raw.Columns)
                cols.Add(col.ColumnName);
            foreach (DataRow row in raw.Rows)
            {
                string in_str = null;
                if (row.RowState == DataRowState.Deleted)
                {
                    List<object> array = new List<object>();
                    foreach (DataColumn col in raw.Columns)
                    {
                        array.Add(row[col, DataRowVersion.Original]);
                    }
                    in_str = SQLIn(array.ToArray(), ignore_blank_rows);
                }
                else
                    in_str = SQLIn(row.ItemArray, ignore_blank_rows);
                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(in_str))
                    continue;
                string insert = String.Format("insert into {0}  ([{1}]) values {2}", destTable, String.Join("],[", cols.ToArray()), in_str);

                if (!RawDogOnly)
                {
                    string insert_q = String.Format("insert into [{0}]  ([{1}]) values (@{2})", destTable, String.Join("],[", cols.ToArray()), String.Join(", @", cols.ToArray()));
                    Query q = new Query(insert_q, "<BLANK>");
                    foreach (string col in cols)
                    {
                        if (row.RowState != DataRowState.Deleted)
                            q.AddParameter($"@{col}", UtilsLib.Clean.CleanObject(row[col]));
                        else
                            q.AddParameter($"@{col}", UtilsLib.Clean.CleanObject(row[col, DataRowVersion.Original]));
                    }
                    qs.Add(q);
                }
                
                rows.Add(insert);
                in_str = null;
                insert = null;
                
            }
            
            

            gss.inserts_raw_dog = rows;
            gss.inserts_all = qs;
            GC.Collect();
            return gss;
        }

        public static string SelectColumns(IEnumerable<string> headers)
        {
            return $"[{String.Join("], [", headers.ToArray())}]";
        }
        public static string SQLIn(object[] cells, bool ignore_blank_rows = true, string quote = "")
        {
            List<string> items = new List<string>();
            
            
            foreach (object o in cells)
            {
                object o_cpy = o;
                Type o_t = typeof(object);
                if (null != o_t)
                    o_t = o.GetType();
                o_cpy = UtilsLib.Clean.CleanObject(o);
                
                
                
                
                

                string last = UtilsLib.DB.DbWriteString(o_t, null, o_cpy);
                if (quote != "")
                    last = quote + last + quote;
                items.Add(last);
            }

            string final_answer = "(" + String.Join(",", items) + ")";

            if (ignore_blank_rows)
            {
                var s = (items.Distinct().Count() == 1 && "null" == items[0]);
                
                if (s)
                    final_answer = "";
            }

            if (final_answer.Length > 30000)
            {
                string file = System.IO.Path.Combine(System.IO.Path.GetTempPath(), System.IO.Path.GetRandomFileName());
                System.IO.File.AppendAllText(file, final_answer);
                final_answer = file;
            }
            return final_answer;
        }

        public static Dictionary<string, Type> GetTableTypes(string server, string table)
        {

            Dictionary<string, Type> results = new Dictionary<string, Type>();
            var cols = GetTableColumns(server, table,true);
            foreach (var col in cols)
            {
                
                var t = FindNETTypeForSQL(col.Value);
                results.Add(col.Key, t);
            }
            return results;
        }

        public static Dictionary<string, string> GetTableColumns(string server, string table,bool include_computed)
        {
            
            string sql = "SELECT t.* ,convert(bit,case when c.is_computed is null then 0 else is_computed end) [is_computed] FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS t LEFT join sys.computed_columns c on t.table_name = object_name(c.object_id) AND C.NAME = T.COLUMN_NAME  where t.TABLE_NAME = @table and (convert(bit,case when c.is_computed is null then 0 else is_computed end) = @is_computed or @is_computed=1)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@table", table);
            q.AddParameter("@is_computed", include_computed);
            q.UseCache = true;
            Dictionary<string, string> cols = q.ExecuteDictRows<string, string>("COLUMN_NAME", "DATA_TYPE");
            return cols;
        }
        public static string GetCSVEditableTableColumns(string server, string table)
        {
            var cols = GetTableColumns(server, table,false);
            return String.Join(",", cols.Select(n => n.Key));
        }

        public static int RowsInTable(string server,string table)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT SUM(p.rows) FROM sys.partitions AS p  INNER JOIN sys.tables AS t  ON p.[object_id] = t.[object_id]  INNER JOIN sys.schemas AS s  ON s.[schema_id] = t.[schema_id]  WHERE t.name = @table  AND s.name = N'dbo'  AND p.index_id IN (0,1);";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@table", table);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
        }
        public static DataTable GetTableColumnsTable(string server, string table,bool sorting)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT column_name, data_type FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS where TABLE_NAME = @table order by case when @sorting=1 then column_name else column_name end";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@table", table);
            q.AddParameter("@sorting", sorting);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }



    }
}


--- FILE: CommonLib\ColumnCacher.cs ---
namespace CommonLib
{
    public class ColumnCacher
    {
        private static readonly Lazy<ColumnCacher> lazy = new Lazy<ColumnCacher>(() => new ColumnCacher());

        public static ColumnCacher Instance { get { return lazy.Value; } }

        public List<string> simple = new List<string>();
        public List<string> complex = new List<string>();
        public bool es_listo = false;

        public static void EnsureColumnsCached(string server,string simple_sql,string complex_sql)
        {

            if (!ColumnCacher.Instance.es_listo)
            {
                string sql = simple_sql;
                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.Execute();
                ColumnCacher.Instance.simple.AddRange(q.ColumnListFromTable);
                q.SetSQL(complex_sql);
                q.Execute();
                ColumnCacher.Instance.complex.AddRange(q.ColumnListFromTable);
                ColumnCacher.Instance.es_listo = true;
            }
        }

    }
}

namespace UtilsLib

        public static bool ValidateUserCredentials(string domain, string username, string password)
        {
            IntPtr tokenHandler = IntPtr.Zero;
            bool isValid = LogonUser(username, domain, password, 2, 0, ref tokenHandler);
            return isValid;
        }
        [System.Runtime.InteropServices.DllImport("advapi32.dll")]
        public static extern bool LogonUser(string search_value, string domainName, string password, int LogonType, int LogonProvider, ref IntPtr phToken);

        public static List<T> GetGroupMemberList<T>(string search_value, string property_to_search, string property_to_return, bool recursive)
        {
            PrincipalContext ctx = new PrincipalContext(ContextType.Domain);
            List<T> members = new List<T>();
            List<DirectoryEntry> princs = new List<DirectoryEntry>();
            DirectorySearcher ds = new DirectorySearcher();
            if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(search_value))
                return members;

            
            ds.Filter = "(" + property_to_search + "=" + search_value + ")";

            var sr = ds.FindAll();
            foreach (SearchResult s in sr)
            {
                var de = s.GetDirectoryEntry();
                
                {
                    foreach (var dee in de.Children)
                    {
                        if (!princs.Contains(de))
                            princs.Add(de);
                    }
                }
                
                {
                    if (!princs.Contains(de))
                        princs.Add(de);
                }
            }


            foreach (DirectoryEntry de in princs)
            {
                
                

                if (de.Properties[property_to_return].GetType().Name == "PropertyValueCollection")
                {
                    foreach (var f in de.Properties[property_to_return])
                    {
                        T peep = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(f.ToString(), typeof(T));

                        if (!members.Contains(peep))
                            members.Add(peep);
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    T peep = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(de.Properties[property_to_return].Value, typeof(T));
                    if (!members.Contains(peep))
                        members.Add(peep);
                }
            }

            return members;
        }

        
        
        
        

        

        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

    }
}

namespace UtilsLib

    public class BBGHeaderConfig
    {
        public string name;
        public int length;
        public int length_with_header_space
        {
            get
            {
                return length + right_seperator.Length;
            }
        }

        public string format;
        public string right_seperator;
        public enum ALIGNMENT { RIGHT, LEFT, CENTER }
        public ALIGNMENT text_align;
        public ALIGNMENT header_align;
        public BBGHeaderConfig(string name, int length, string format, string right_seperator, ALIGNMENT text_align, ALIGNMENT header_align)
        {
            this.name = name;
            this.length = length;
            this.format = format;
            this.right_seperator = right_seperator;
            this.text_align = text_align;
            this.header_align = header_align;
            if (name.Length > length)
                throw new Exception("Name too long");
        }

        public override string ToString()
        {
            return name;
        }
    }

--- FILE: Utils\Clean.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public static class Clean
    {
        public static string CommonVariables(string subject, string seperator, Dictionary<string, object> additional_variables = null)
        {
            Dictionary<string, object> c = GetCommonVariables();
            if (null != additional_variables)
            {
                foreach (var more in additional_variables)
                {
                    if(!c.ContainsKey(more.Key))
                        c.Add(more.Key, more.Value);
                }
                    
            }
            return ApplyDictionary<object>(c, subject, seperator);
        }

        public enum SCALE_FACTOR { ACTUAL, MILLIONS }


        public static object CleanObject(object o)
        {
            if (null == o || DBNull.Value == o)
                return DBNull.Value;
            else if (o.ToString().Contains("-21468262"))
                return DBNull.Value;
            else if (o.ToString() == "ExcelDna.Integration.ExcelEmpty")
                return DBNull.Value;
            else if (o.ToString() == "N/A")
                return DBNull.Value;
            else if (null != o && o.GetType() == typeof(string))
                o = o.ToString().Trim();
            return o;
        }

        public static string StripHTML(string input)
        {
            if (null == input)
                return null;
            return Regex.Replace(input, "<.*?>", String.Empty);
        }
        public static Nullable<DateTime> FindFirstDateIn(string stringWithDate)
        {
            
            string raw = stringWithDate;
            stringWithDate = stringWithDate.Replace(Environment.NewLine, " ");
            var matches = Regex.Matches(stringWithDate, @"\d{2}\/\d{2}\/\d{4}");
            
            string[] formats = new string[] { "MM/dd/yyyy","M/d/yyyy","MM/d/yyyy","M/d/yyyy","mmmm d yyyy" };
            List<Match> matchesList = new List<Match>();
            foreach (Match s in matches)
                matchesList.Add(s);
            matchesList.Reverse();
            
            foreach(string s in stringWithDate.Split(' '))
            {
                
                string date = s;
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(date))
                {
                    DateTime date_val;
                    if (DateTime.TryParseExact(date, formats, System.Globalization.CultureInfo.CurrentCulture, System.Globalization.DateTimeStyles.AssumeLocal, out date_val))
                    {
                        return date_val;
                    }
                    

                    
                }
            }
            return null;
        }
        public static string SelectOnlyLetters(string checkString)
        {
            
            object result = Regex.Match(checkString, @"[^A-Z$]").Value;
            string cow = "";
            double stupid;
            foreach (char s in checkString.ToCharArray())
            {
                if (!Double.TryParse(s.ToString(), out stupid))
                {
                    if (s != '.')
                        cow += s;
                }
            }
            return cow;
        }


        public static Nullable<double> ConvertOface(string s, SCALE_FACTOR return_factor = SCALE_FACTOR.ACTUAL)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(s))
                return null;
            if (s == "-")
                return null;

            string oface = s.Replace("$", "").Replace(",", "").ToUpper().Trim();
            Nullable<double> mult_by = null;
            if (oface.ToUpper().Contains("MM"))
            {
                oface = oface.Replace("MM", "");
                mult_by = 1000000;
            }
            if (oface.ToUpper().Contains("M"))
            {
                oface = oface.Replace("M", "");
                mult_by = 1000;
            }
            if (oface.ToUpper().Contains("K"))
            {
                oface = oface.Replace("K", "");
                mult_by = 1000;
            }

            double o;
            if (!Double.TryParse(oface, out o))
            {
                return null;
            }
            if (null == mult_by)
            {
                if (o < 1000)
                    mult_by = 1000000;
                else if (o < 10000)
                    mult_by = 1000;
                else
                    mult_by = 1;
            }
            o = o * mult_by.Value;
            if (return_factor == SCALE_FACTOR.MILLIONS)
                return o / 1e6;
            return o;
        }

        public static string ApplySimpleVariable<T>(string variable, T answer, string subject)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(subject) || null == variable)
                return subject;

            subject = subject.Replace(variable, answer.ToString().Replace("12:00:00 AM", ""));
            return subject;
        }

        public static string ApplyDictionary<T>(Dictionary<string, T> parms, string subject, string seperator)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(subject) || null == parms)
                return subject;
            if (null == parms)
            {
                var defaults = GetCommonVariables();
                foreach (var s in defaults)
                {
                    parms.Add(s.Key, (T)s.Value);
                }
            }

            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, T> kvp in parms)
            {
                

                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                

                
                
                string s = kvp.Value.ToString();
                if (kvp.Value.GetType() == typeof(List<string>))
                {
                    if (null == seperator)
                        seperator = "/";
                    List<string> list = kvp.Value as List<string>;
                    s = String.Join(seperator, list.ToArray());
                }

                if (kvp.Value.GetType() == typeof(List<int>))
                {
                    if (null == seperator)
                        seperator = ",";
                    List<int> list = kvp.Value as List<int>;
                    s = String.Join(seperator, list.ToArray());
                }

                subject = subject.ReplaceIns(kvp.Key, s.Replace(" 12:00:00 AM", ""));
            }
            return subject;
        }



        public static Dictionary<string, object> GetCommonVariables()
        {
            UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime d = new Dates.XDateTime(DateTime.Today);
            Dictionary<string, object> vars = new Dictionary<string, object>();
            vars.Add("@todayYYYYMMDD@", DateTime.Today.ToString("yyyyMMdd"));
            vars.Add("@today_yyyy_MM_dd@", DateTime.Today.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd"));
            vars.Add("@today_spelled@", DateTime.Today.ToString("MMMM d, yyyy"));
            vars.Add("@today_alt1@", DateTime.Today.ToString("M.d.yyyy"));

            vars.Add("@today", DateTime.Today.ToString("M/d/yyyy"));

            vars.Add("@yesterday", DateTime.Today.Date.AddDays(-1));
            vars.Add("@prevbday", d.PreviousBusinessDay());
            vars.Add("@nextbday", d.NextBusinessDay());
            vars.Add("@previous_month_name", d.FirstBizDayOfMonth().AddDays(-1).ToString("MMMM"));
            vars.Add("@previous_month_short_name", d.FirstBizDayOfMonth().AddDays(-1).ToString("MMM"));
            vars.Add("@previous_month_year", d.FirstBizDayOfMonth().AddDays(-1).ToString("yyyy"));
            return vars;
        }

        public static string SelectOnlyNumbers(string val)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(val))
                return null;
            return Regex.Replace(val, "[^0-9]", "");
        }

        public static double? SelectOnlyNumbersDbl(string val)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(val))
                return null;
            string s = Regex.Replace(val, "[^0-9]", "");
            double d;
            if (double.TryParse(s, out d))
                return d;
            return null;
        }


        public static string SSNFormatted(string ssn, bool throw_error)
        {
            
            string ssn_clean = null;
            if (null != ssn)
            {
                string clean = UtilsLib.Clean.SelectOnlyNumbers(ssn);
                double ss;
                if (Double.TryParse(clean, out ss))
                    ssn_clean = $"{ss:000-00-0000}";

                if (null != ssn_clean && ssn_clean.Length != 11)
                {
                    if (throw_error)
                        throw new Exception("SSN isn't right: " + ssn);
                }
                return ssn_clean;
            }
            return null;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public static string NiceColumnName(DataColumn col)
        {
            return NiceColumnName(col.Caption);
        }
        public static string NiceColumnName(string ret)
        {

            ret = ret.Replace("_$$", "");
            ret = ret.Replace("_$", "");
            ret = ret.Replace("_time", "");
            ret = ret.Replace("_%", "");
            ret = ret.Replace("_,", "");
            ret = ret.Replace("_MM/dd/yyyy", "");
            if (ret.Contains("|") && ret.Substring(ret.Length - 1, 1) == "|")
            {
                ret = ret.Substring(0, ret.IndexOf('|'));
            }
            if (ret.Contains("_asis"))
            {
                ret = ret.Replace("_asis", "");
                ret = ret.Replace("_", " ");
            }
            else
            { 
                ret = ret.Replace("_", " ").ToUpperInvariant();
            }
            return ret;
        }

        public static string CleanFilename(string name, bool include_excel_restrctions, bool robust =false)
        {
            if (null == name)
                return null;
            name = name.Replace("|", "-");
            name = name.Replace(">", "greater than");
            name = name.Replace("<", "less than");
            name = name.Replace(":", "-");
            name = name.Replace("\"\"", "'");
            name = name.Replace("/", "-");
            name = name.Replace("\\", "-");
            name = name.Replace("?", "");
            name = name.Replace("*", "^");
            if (include_excel_restrctions)
            {
                name = name.Replace("[", "");
                name = name.Replace("]", "");
            }

            if (robust)
            {
                char[] invalidChars = System.IO.Path.GetInvalidFileNameChars();
                foreach (char c in invalidChars)
                    name = name.Replace(c.ToString(), "");
            }
            return name;
        }

        public static string HtmlFormat(DataColumn col, object obj)
        {
            return HtmlFormat(col.ColumnName, obj);
        }

        public static Dictionary<string, object> HtmlFormat<T>(Dictionary<string,T> vals)
        {
            Dictionary<string, object> results = new Dictionary<string, object>();
            foreach(KeyValuePair<string,T> kvp in vals)
            {
                string formatted = UtilsLib.Clean.HtmlFormat(kvp.Key, kvp.Value);
                results.Add(kvp.Key, formatted);
            }
            return results;
        }

        public static string HtmlFormat(string col_name, object obj)
        {
            if (null != obj)
            {
                string format = GetFormatFromColumnName(col_name);
                Type t = typeof(string);


                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(format))
                {
                    if (obj.GetType() == typeof(DateTime) && !col_name.Contains("_time"))
                    {
                        format = "M/d/yy";
                        t = typeof(DateTime);
                    }
                    if (obj.GetType() == typeof(double))
                    {
                        format = "0.000";
                        t = typeof(double);
                    }
                }
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(format))
                {
                    object o = obj;
                    if (t != typeof(string))
                    {
                        o = System.Convert.ChangeType(obj, t);
                    }
                    format = "{0:" + format + "}";
                    object ob_typed = o;
                    
                    if (null != ob_typed)
                    {
                        double d;
                        if (Double.TryParse(o.ToString(), out d))
                            ob_typed = d;
                    }
                    return String.Format(format, ob_typed);
                }
                string retVal = obj.ToString();
                retVal = HTMLUtils.EscapeSequenceReverse(retVal);
                return retVal;
            }
            return "";
        }

        public static string GetFormatFromColumnName(string col_name)
        {
            if (col_name.Contains("_$$"))
                return "$#,##0";
            if (col_name.Contains("_$"))
                return "#,##0";
            if (col_name.Contains("_,"))
                return "#,##0";
            if (col_name.Contains("_%"))
                return "0%";
            if (col_name.Contains("_MM/dd/yyyy"))
                return "MM/dd/yyyy";
            if (col_name.Contains("_|") && col_name.Substring(col_name.Length - 1, 1) == "|")
            {
                string fmt = col_name.Split('|')[1];
                
                return fmt;
            }
            return null;

        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Utils\ClipboardHelper.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class ClipboardHelper
    {
        public static bool EmptyClipboard()
        {
            return Win32ClipboardAPI.EmptyClipboard();
        }
        public static bool SetClipboard(ReadOnlyCollection<DataClip> clipData)
        {
            
            if (!Win32ClipboardAPI.OpenClipboard(IntPtr.Zero))
                return false;

            
            EmptyClipboard();

            
            IEnumerator<DataClip> cData = clipData.GetEnumerator();
            while (cData.MoveNext())
            {
                DataClip cd = cData.Current;

                
                IntPtr alloc = Win32MemoryAPI.GlobalAlloc(Win32MemoryAPI.GMEM_MOVEABLE | Win32MemoryAPI.GMEM_DDESHARE, cd.Size);
                IntPtr gLock = Win32MemoryAPI.GlobalLock(alloc);

                
                if ((int)cd.Size > 0)
                {
                    Marshal.Copy(cd.Buffer, 0, gLock, cd.Buffer.GetLength(0));
                }
                else
                {
                }
                
                Win32MemoryAPI.GlobalUnlock(alloc);
                Win32ClipboardAPI.SetClipboardData(cd.Format, alloc);
            };
            
            Win32ClipboardAPI.CloseClipboard();
            return true;
        }
        public static void SaveToFile(ReadOnlyCollection<DataClip> clipData, string clipName)
        {
            
            IEnumerator<DataClip> cData = clipData.GetEnumerator();
            
            int i = 0;

            
            
            if (Directory.Exists(clipName))
            {
                Directory.Delete(clipName, true);
            }
            
            DirectoryInfo di = Directory.CreateDirectory(clipName);
            UtilsLib.FileLib.WaitForDirectoryToBeCreated(di.FullName, 5000);


            while (cData.MoveNext())
            {
                
                XmlSerializer xml = new XmlSerializer(typeof(DataClip));
                
                using (StreamWriter sw = new StreamWriter(di.FullName + @"\" + i.ToString() + ".cli", false))
                {
                    
                    xml.Serialize(sw, cData.Current);
                }

                i++;
            }



        }
        private static ReadOnlyCollection<DataClip> ReadFromFile(string clipName)
        {
            
            List<DataClip> clips = new List<DataClip>();
            
            if (Directory.Exists(clipName))
            {
                DirectoryInfo di = new DirectoryInfo(clipName);

                
                for (int x = 0; x < di.GetFiles().GetLength(0); x++)
                {
                    
                    XmlSerializer xml = new XmlSerializer(typeof(DataClip));
                    
                    FileInfo fi = new FileInfo(di.FullName + "\\" + x.ToString() + ".cli");
                    
                    using (FileStream fs = fi.Open(FileMode.Open))
                    {
                        
                        clips.Add((DataClip)xml.Deserialize(fs));
                    }
                }
            }
            return new ReadOnlyCollection<DataClip>(clips);
        }

        private static List<string> clipboards = new List<string>();
        public static void Serialize(string clipName)
        {
            if (!clipboards.Contains(clipName))
                clipboards.Add(clipName);
            
            ReadOnlyCollection<DataClip> clipData = GetClipboard();
            
            SaveToFile(clipData, clipName);
        }

        public static void CleanUpAllDirectories()
        {
            foreach (string clip in clipboards)
            {
                Directory.Delete(clip, true);
            }
        }
        public static bool Deserialize(string clipName)
        {
            
            ReadOnlyCollection<DataClip> clipData = ReadFromFile(clipName);
            
            return SetClipboard(clipData);
        }
        public static ReadOnlyCollection<DataClip> GetClipboard()
        {
            
            List<DataClip> clipData = new List<DataClip>();

            
            if (!Win32ClipboardAPI.OpenClipboard(IntPtr.Zero))
                return new ReadOnlyCollection<DataClip>(clipData);

            
            uint format = 0;
            while ((format = Win32ClipboardAPI.EnumClipboardFormats(format)) != 0)
            {
                
                string formatName = "0";
                DataClip cd;
                if (format > 14)
                {
                    StringBuilder res = new StringBuilder();
                    if (Win32ClipboardAPI.GetClipboardFormatName(format, res, 100) > 0)
                    {
                        formatName = res.ToString();
                    }

                }
                
                int tries = 5;
                bool success = false;
                int i = 0;
                IntPtr pos = IntPtr.Zero;
                do
                {
                    pos = Win32ClipboardAPI.GetClipboardData(format);
                    i++;
                } while (pos == IntPtr.Zero && i < tries);

                
                if (pos == IntPtr.Zero)
                    continue;
                
                UIntPtr lenght = Win32MemoryAPI.GlobalSize(pos);
                IntPtr gLock = Win32MemoryAPI.GlobalLock(pos);
                byte[] buffer;
                if ((int)lenght > 0)
                {
                    
                    buffer = new byte[(int)lenght];
                    int l = Convert.ToInt32(lenght.ToString());
                    
                    Marshal.Copy(gLock, buffer, 0, l);
                }
                else
                {
                    buffer = new byte[0];
                }
                
                cd = new DataClip(format, formatName, buffer);
                cd.FormatName = formatName;
                


                clipData.Add(cd);
            }
            
            Win32ClipboardAPI.CloseClipboard();
            
            return new ReadOnlyCollection<DataClip>(clipData);
        }




        [Serializable]
        public class DataClip
        {
            private uint format;
            public uint Format
            {
                get { return format; }
                set { format = value; }
            }

            private string formatName;
            public string FormatName
            {
                get { return formatName; }
                set { formatName = value; }
            }
            private byte[] buffer;

            private int size;
            public byte[] Buffer
            {
                get { return buffer; }
                set { buffer = value; }
            }
            public UIntPtr Size
            {
                get
                {
                    if (buffer != null)
                    {
                        
                        return new UIntPtr(Convert.ToUInt32(buffer.GetLength(0)));
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        
                        return new UIntPtr(Convert.ToUInt32(size));
                    }
                }
            }
            public DataClip(uint format, string formatName, byte[] buffer)
            {
                this.format = format;
                this.formatName = formatName;
                this.buffer = buffer;
                this.size = 0;
            }
            public DataClip() { }
        }

        {

            public const uint GMEM_MOVEABLE = 0x2;
        }

--- FILE: Utils\CommandLineArgs.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class CommandLineArgs
    {
        public Dictionary<string, object> _args = new Dictionary<string, object>();

        public CommandLineArgs(string[] args)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i != args.Length; i++)
            {
                if (args[i].Substring(0, 1) == "-")
                {
                    string key = args[i].Substring(1, args[i].Length - 1);
                    object value = true;
                    if (args.Length > i + 1)
                        value = args[i + 1];
                    _args.Add(key.ToUpper(), value);
                }
            }
        }

        public string ArgDump
        {
            get
            {
                string dump = "";
                foreach (KeyValuePair<string, object> kvp in _args)
                {
                    dump += String.Format("{0} : {1}{2}", kvp.Key, kvp.Value, System.Environment.NewLine);
                }

                dump += "FULL CMD:" + Environment.CommandLine + System.Environment.NewLine;
                return dump;
            }
        }



        public string this[string key]
        {
            get
            {
                
                
                return _args[key.ToUpper()].ToString().Trim();
            }
        }

        public bool ContainsFlag(string key)
        {
            return _args.ContainsKey(key.ToUpper());
        }

        public List<T> GetArray<T>(string key, char splitter)
        {
            List<T> t = new List<T>();
            foreach (object o in _args[key.ToUpper()].ToString().Split(splitter))
            {
                T obj = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T)); ;
                t.Add(obj);
            }
            return t;
        }


        public Dictionary<string, T> GetDictionary<T>(string parm) where T : class
        {
            Dictionary<string, T> answer = new Dictionary<string, T>();
            string[] parms = parm.Split(';');
            foreach (string p in parms)
            {
                string key = p.Split('|')[0].ToUpper();
                T o = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(p.Split('|')[1], typeof(T));
                if (null != o)
                {
                    if (o.ToString().Contains("{") && o.ToString().Contains("}"))
                    {

                        string s = o.ToString().Replace("{", "").Replace("}", "");
                        List<int> ints;
                        List<string> strings = new List<string>();
                        o = strings as T;
                        int i;
                        bool is_int = false;
                        bool force_string = false;
                        if (s.Split(',')[0].Length > 0)
                        {
                            ints = new List<int>();

                            foreach (string n in s.Split(','))
                            {
                                if (int.TryParse(n, out i))
                                {
                                    ints.Add(System.Convert.ToInt32(n));
                                }
                                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(n) && n == "force_string")
                                {
                                    force_string = true;
                                }
                                else
                                    strings.Add(n);
                            }
                            if (ints.Count == strings.Count && force_string == false)
                                o = ints as T;
                            else
                                o = strings as T;
                        }


                    }
                }
                answer.Add(key, o);
            }

            return answer;
        }
        
        public T ArgIfAvailableNotNull<T>(string key,T return_if_null = default(T))
        {
            key = key.ToUpper();
            if (_args.ContainsKey(key))
            {
                object arg = _args[key];

                if (null == arg)
                {
                    return return_if_null;
                }
                return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(arg, typeof(T));

            }
            return return_if_null;
        }


        public Nullable<T> ArgIfAvailable<T>(string key, T? default_if_not_present) where T : struct
        {
            key = key.ToUpper();
            if (_args.ContainsKey(key))
            {
                object arg = _args[key];
                    
                return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(arg, typeof(T));

            }
            if (null == default_if_not_present)
                return null;
            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(default_if_not_present, typeof(T)); ;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
    }

--- FILE: Utils\Compression.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class Compression
    {
        public static string CompressString(string s)
        {
            var bytes = Encoding.Unicode.GetBytes(s);
            using (var msi = new MemoryStream(bytes))
            using (var mso = new MemoryStream())
            {
                using (var gs = new GZipStream(mso, CompressionMode.Compress))
                {
                    msi.CopyTo(gs);
                }
                return System.Convert.ToBase64String(mso.ToArray());
            }
        }
        public static string DecompressString(string s)
        {
            var bytes = Convert.FromBase64String(s);
            using (var msi = new MemoryStream(bytes))
            using (var mso = new MemoryStream())
            {
                using (var gs = new GZipStream(msi, CompressionMode.Decompress))
                {
                    gs.CopyTo(mso);
                }

                return Encoding.Unicode.GetString(mso.ToArray());
            }
        }

        public static string Zip(string filename, IEnumerable<string> files)
        {
            string full_path = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), filename);
            if (File.Exists(full_path))
                File.Delete(full_path);
            using (ZipFile zip = new ZipFile(full_path))
            {
                zip.AddFiles(files, false, "/");
                zip.CompressionLevel = Ionic.Zlib.CompressionLevel.BestCompression;
                zip.Save();
            }
            return full_path;
        }

        public static void UnZip(string full_path_of_zip,string extract_to)
        {
            ZipFile zip = new ZipFile(full_path_of_zip);
            zip.ExtractAll(extract_to);
   
            {
                
                
                
            }
        }
    }

namespace UtilsLib
