        public static double AnnualizeMonthly(double mdr)
        {
            mdr = mdr * 100;
            double num = (1 - (Math.Pow((100 - mdr) / 100, 12))) * 100;
            return num;
        }


        public static double ConvertMetersToMiles(double meters)
        {
            return (meters / 1609.344);
        }

        public static Nullable<int> ToQuarter(DateTime date)
        {
            if (date == DateTime.MinValue)
                return null;
            if (date.Month <= 3)
                return 1;

            if (date.Month <= 6)
                return 2;

            if (date.Month <= 9)
                return 3;

            return 4;
        }
        public static Int64 ToHash(ref string data)
        {
            return Farmhash.Sharp.Farmhash.Hash32(data);
        }

        public static double[] VectorStringToVector(string vector_arrayvector)
        {
            List<double> vector_array = new List<double>();
            foreach (string s in vector_arrayvector.Split(' '))
            {
                double d;
                if (!Double.TryParse(s, out d))
                    return null;
                vector_array.Add(d);
            }
            return vector_array.ToArray();
        }
        public static double[] SingleNumberToVector(double vector_arrayvector, int how_many_months)
        {
            List<double> vector_array = new List<double>();
            for (int i = 0; i != how_many_months; i++)
                vector_array.Add(vector_arrayvector);
            return vector_array.ToArray();
        }



        public static double[] RampToVector(string ramp, int vector_length)
        {
            string[] rmps = ramp.Split(' ');
            double tmp;
     
            int offset = 0;
            List<double> answer = new List<double>();
            string last = null;
            double? last_dbl = null;
            for (int i = 0; i < rmps.Length;i++)
            {
                string num = rmps[i];
                double test;
                if(Double.TryParse(num,out test))
                {
                    answer.Add(test);
                }

                if (num.ToUpper() == "FOR")
                {
                    int over_how_many = System.Convert.ToInt32(rmps[i + 1]);
                    for (int f = 0; f != over_how_many-1; f++)
                    {
                        answer.Add(last_dbl.Value);
                    }
                    i++;
                }
                if (num.ToUpper() == "RAMP")
                {
                    int over_how_many = System.Convert.ToInt32(rmps[i + 1]);
                    double dest_num = System.Convert.ToDouble(rmps[i + 2]);
                    double step = (dest_num - last_dbl.Value) / (over_how_many - 1);
                    
                    
                    for (int n = 0; n != over_how_many - 2; n++)
                    {
                        double next = last_dbl.Value + step;
                        answer.Add(next);
                        last_dbl = next;
                    }
                    i = i + 2;
                    test = dest_num;
                    answer.Add(dest_num);
                }
                last_dbl = test;
                last = num;
            }

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            

            
            
            
            
            
            return answer.ToArray();
        }



        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        

        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        


        public static Nullable<DateTime> ConvertSimpleMonthToDate(string month)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(month))
                return null;

            if (month.Length == 3)
            {
                DateTime d = System.Convert.ToDateTime(month + " " + DateTime.Now.Year);
                TimeSpan year_check = DateTime.Today - d;
                if (year_check.Days <= -90)
                    return d.AddDays(year_check.Days);
                return d.Date;
            }
            return null;
        }
        public static object[] JaggedVerticleToSingle(object[,] array, int zero_based_row)
        {
            List<object> arr = new List<object>();
            for (int i = 0; i != array.GetLength(0); i++)
            {
                arr.Add(array[i, zero_based_row]);
            }
            return arr.ToArray();
        }

        public static double SurvivalToAgeBasedCPR(double survivalRate, int age)
        {
            double result = (1.0 - Math.Pow( (1.0 -( 1.0 - survivalRate)),12.0/age)) * 100.0;
            
            return result;
        }


        public static double CPRtoSMM(double cpr)
        {
            double result = 1.0 - Math.Pow(1.0 - cpr / 100.0, (1.0 / 12.0));
            
            return result;
        }
        public static double SMMtoCPR(double smm)
        {
            return (1 - (Math.Pow(1 - smm, 12))) * 100.0;
            
        }
        public static double CPRtoPSA(double cpr, double age)
        {
            age = Math.Max(1.0, age);
            return cpr / Math.Max(30.0, age) / .2 * 100;
        }
        public static double PSAtoCPR(double psa, double age)
        {
            age = Math.Max(1, age);
            
            double cpr = psa / 100.0 * .2 * Math.Min(30, age);
            return Math.Min(100, cpr);

        }
        public static double SMMtoPSA(double smm, double age)
        {
            return CPRtoPSA(SMMtoCPR(smm), age);
        }

        public static double MDRtoCDR(double mdr)
        {
            return MonthlyNumberToAnnual(mdr);
        }

        public static Nullable<double> PriceTalkToPrice(string str)
        {
            string str_raw = str;
            if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(str))
                return null;
            try
            {
                double d;

                List<string> ignores = new List<string>(new string[] { "CVR", "DONKEY", "TRADED", "TRADES", "TRADE", "COVERED", "COVER", "BIN", ":", "BEST", " - ", "DNT,", "DNT", "*", "SAW" });
                if (Double.TryParse(str, out d))
                    return d;
                Nullable<double> px = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.TicDec(str);
                if (null != px)
                    return px;
                str = str.ToUpper();
                foreach (string s in ignores)
                    str = str.Replace(s, "");
                str = str.Trim();

                if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(str))
                    return null;

                if (Double.TryParse(str, out d))
                    return d;

                string right_letters = str.LettersFromTheRight()?.Trim();
                string left_letters = str.LettersFromTheLeft()?.Trim();
                
                double? left_base = Get_H_NumberBump(left_letters);

                double? mid = UtilsLib.Clean.SelectOnlyNumbersDbl(str);

                if (null == mid)
                    return null;

                
                if (right_letters == "H" || right_letters == "A")
                {
                    if (right_letters == "H" && String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(left_letters))
                    {
                        return mid.Value + .5;
                    }
                    else if (right_letters == "A" && String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(left_letters))

                    {
                        return mid.Value;
                    }
                    else
                        return mid.Value + left_base;
                }
                else if (right_letters == "S")
                {
                    left_base = Get_S_NumberBump(left_letters);
                    return mid.Value + left_base;
                }
                else if (left_letters == "L" || left_letters == "M" || left_letters == "H")
                {
                    left_base = Get_H_NumberBump(left_letters);
                    return mid.Value + left_base;
                }

            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n, "Raw Price Talk to Dec: " + str_raw);
            }

            return null;
        }

        public static Nullable<double> Get_H_NumberBump(string num)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(num))
                return null;
            num = UtilsLib.Clean.SelectOnlyLetters(num);
            switch (num)
            {
                case "VL":
                    return .125;
                case "L":
                    return .25;
                case "LM":
                    return .375;
                case "M":
                    return .5;
                case "MH":
                    return .625;
                case "H":
                    return .75;
                case "VH":
                    return .875;
                case "A":
                    return 0.0;

            }
            return null;
        }

        public static Nullable<double> Get_S_NumberBump(string num)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(num))
                return null;
            num = UtilsLib.Clean.SelectOnlyLetters(num);
            switch (num)
            {
                case "VL":
                    return .5;
                case "L":
                    return 1.5;
                case "LM":
                    return 3.5;
                case "M":
                    return 5;
                case "MH":
                    return 6.5;
                case "H":
                    return 8.5;
                case "VH":
                    return 9.5; ;

            }
            return null;
        }


        private static double GetFlagWorth(string flag, double baseNum)
        {
            double root = 0;
            flag = flag.ToUpper().Trim();
            flag = flag.Replace(" S", "");
            if (flag.Length != 0 && flag.LastIndexOf('S') == flag.Length - 1)
                flag = flag.Substring(0, flag.Length - 1);

            double L = 2.5 / (baseNum / 10);
            double M = 5.0 / (baseNum / 10);
            double H = 7.5 / (baseNum / 10);
            switch (flag)
            {
                case "AREA":
                    return root;
                case "L/M":
                case "M/L":
                case "ML":
                case "LM":
                    return (L + M) / 2;
                case "L":
                    return L;
                case "M":
                    return M;
                case "H":
                    return H;
                case "H/M":
                case "M/H":
                case "MH":
                case "HM":
                    return (M + H) / 2;
                default:
                    {
                        return 0;
                    }
            }

        }

        public static string PriceToPriceTalk(double model)
        {
            string retVal = "";
            string retValT = "";
            string numberPortion = "";
            double baseNum = 1.0 / 3.0;
            double L = baseNum / 2;
            double M = baseNum * 2;
            double H = (baseNum * 3) - .000000000001;
            int RoundNumber = ((int)System.Math.Round(model * 10, 0) / 100) * 10;
            double ImportantNumber = (model - RoundNumber) / 10;
            if (RoundNumber == 0)
                numberPortion = "SD";
            else if (RoundNumber == 10)
                numberPortion = "TEEN";
            else
                numberPortion = RoundNumber.ToString();

            if (ImportantNumber <= .1 || ImportantNumber >= .9)
            {
                if (ImportantNumber >= .9)
                    numberPortion = (RoundNumber + 10).ToString();
                return numberPortion + "A";
            }
            else if (ImportantNumber < L)
                retVal = "L";
            else if (ImportantNumber < M)
                retVal = "M";
            else if (ImportantNumber < H)
                retVal = "H";

            
            if (0 < ImportantNumber && ImportantNumber < L + (baseNum / 2) - .001 && retVal != "L")
                retValT = "L";
            if (L < ImportantNumber && ImportantNumber < M + (baseNum / 2) - .001 && retVal != "M")
                retValT = "M";
            if (M < ImportantNumber && ImportantNumber > M + (baseNum / 2) - .001 && retVal != "H")
                retValT = "H";

            return retValT + retVal + numberPortion + "s";
        }

        public static double MonthlyNumberToAnnual(double mdr)
        {
            mdr = mdr * 100;
            double num = (1 - (Math.Pow((100 - mdr) / 100, 12))) * 100;
            return num;
        }
        public static double PSAtoSMM(double psa, double age)
        {
            return CPRtoSMM(PSAtoCPR(psa, age));
        }


        public string ArrayToString(double[] array)
        {
            return String.Join(" ", array);
        }


        public static string DecTicRound(double dNumber)
        {
            double rounded = Math.Round(dNumber * 64, 0) / 64;
            return DecTic(rounded);
        }
        
        public static string DecTic(double dNumber)
        {
            if (0 == dNumber)
                return "0-0";
            String ticks = "";
            string handleStr, tickStr = "00", lastChar = "";
            bool isNegative = dNumber < 0;
            dNumber = Math.Abs(dNumber); 
            double thirty2nds = (dNumber - Math.Floor(dNumber)) * 32; 
            int dEigths = (int)Math.Round((thirty2nds - Math.Floor(thirty2nds)) * 8, 0, MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero);
            lastChar = dEigths + "";
            if ((dEigths) == 4)
                lastChar = "+";
            else if (dEigths == 8) 
            {
                thirty2nds += 1;
                lastChar = "";
            }
            else if (dEigths == 0)
                lastChar = "";
            if (((int)Math.Floor(thirty2nds)) == 32)
                dNumber += 1;
            else
            {
                tickStr = ((int)Math.Floor(thirty2nds)).ToString();
                if (tickStr.Length == 1) tickStr = "0" + tickStr; 
            }
            handleStr = ((int)Math.Floor(dNumber)).ToString(); 
            ticks = handleStr + "-" + tickStr + lastChar;
            if (isNegative)
                return "(" + ticks + ")";
            return ticks;
        }

        
        public static Nullable<double> TicDec(string str)
        {
            string orig = str;
            double sign = 1;

            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(str) || (null != str && str.Trim().Length == 0))
                return default(double);

            str = orig.Replace("$", "").Trim();
            if (str.Contains(" ") && str.Split(' ')[1].Contains("/")) 
            {
                double first = System.Convert.ToDouble(str.Split(' ')[1].Split('/')[0]);
                double last = System.Convert.ToDouble(str.Split(' ')[1].Split('/')[1]);

                if (last == 2)
                    str = str.Substring(0, str.IndexOf(" ")) + (first * 4).ToString();
                if (last == 4)
                    str = str.Substring(0, str.IndexOf(" ")) + (first * 2).ToString();
                if (last == 8)
                    str = str.Substring(0, str.IndexOf(" ")) + (first).ToString();
            }

            if (str.Split('-').Length == 3 && str.Substring(0, 1) == "-") 
            {
                str = str.Substring(1, str.Length - 1);
                sign = -1;
            }
            if (str.Contains(")") && str.Contains("("))
            {
                str = str.Replace("(", "").Replace(")", "");
                sign = -1;
            }
            if (str.Contains("-"))
                str = str.Replace(":", "");
            else
                str = str.Replace(":", "-");
            double result = 0;
            if (Double.TryParse(str, out result))
            {
                return result * sign;
            }
            int TicSize = 32;
            string value = "";
            double returnValue = 0;

            if (str.Substring(0, 1) == "-")
            {
                sign = -1;
                value = str.Substring(1, str.Length - 1);
            }
            else
                value = str;


            int dash_location = str.Substring(1, str.Length - 1).IndexOf('-');
            if (dash_location == -1)
                dash_location = str.IndexOf('.');
            if (dash_location == -1)
                dash_location = str.IndexOf("'");
            if (dash_location == -1)
                TicSize = 64;
            int len_after_tic = str.Length - (dash_location + 2);
            if (len_after_tic == 1)
            {
                value = value.Insert(dash_location + 2, "0");
            }
            value = value.Trim() + "000";

            if (dash_location == -1)
            {
                if (Double.TryParse(value, out result) == false)
                    return null;
                if (value == "")
                    returnValue = 5;
                else
                    returnValue = sign * (System.Convert.ToInt32(value)) / 1000;
                return returnValue;
            }
            string handle_str = value.Substring(0, dash_location + 1);
            string tics_str = value.Substring(dash_location + 2, 2);
            string numbers = Clean.SelectOnlyNumbers(tics_str);
            tics_str = value.Substring(dash_location + 2, numbers.Length);
            if (Double.TryParse(handle_str, out result) == false)
                return null;
            double handle = result;
            if (Double.TryParse(tics_str, out result) == false)
                return null;
            double tics = result;
            double eights = 0;

            if (value[dash_location + 4] == '+' || value[dash_location + 3] == '+')
                eights = 4;
            else
            {
                string eights_str = value.Substring(dash_location + 4, 1);
                if (Double.TryParse(eights_str, out result) == false)
                    return null;
                eights = result;
            }

            return sign * (handle + tics / TicSize + eights / (8 * TicSize));
        }


        public static Nullable<T> NullIfNot<T>(object o) where T : struct
        {
            if ((null == o || DBNull.Value == o) || (null != o && o.GetType() == typeof(string) && String.IsNullOrEmpty(o.ToString())))
                return null;

            string o_str = o.ToString();


            if (typeof(T) == typeof(double))
            {
                double d;
                if (Double.TryParse(o_str, out d))
                    return d as T?;
                return null;
            }
            if (typeof(T) == typeof(int))
            {
                int i;
                if (Int32.TryParse(o_str, out i))
                    return i as T?;
                return null;
            }
            if (typeof(T) == typeof(DateTime))
            {
                DateTime dt;
                if (DateTime.TryParse(o_str, out dt))
                    return dt as T?;
                return null;
            }

            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));

        }

        public static string ColumnNumberToLetter(int intCol)
        {

            int intFirstLetter = ((intCol) / 676) + 64;
            int intSecondLetter = ((intCol % 676) / 26) + 64;
            int intThirdLetter = (intCol % 26) + 65;

            char FirstLetter = (intFirstLetter > 64) ? (char)intFirstLetter : ' ';
            char SecondLetter = (intSecondLetter > 64) ? (char)intSecondLetter : ' ';
            char ThirdLetter = (char)intThirdLetter;

            return string.Concat(FirstLetter, SecondLetter, ThirdLetter).Trim();
        }
        public static string GetExcelColumnNameAlt(int columnNumber)
        {
            int dividend = columnNumber;
            string columnName = String.Empty;
            int modulo;

            while (dividend > 0)
            {
                modulo = (dividend - 1) % 26;
                columnName = Convert.ToChar(65 + modulo).ToString() + columnName;
                dividend = (int)((dividend - modulo) / 26);
            }

            return columnName;
        }
        public static T NullIfNotAlt<T>(object o)
        {
            if (null == o)
                return default(T);
            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
        }

    public class Dates

        public enum DayCount { Act360, Act365, ActAct, Days360 }


        public static double Yearfrac(DateTime startDate, DateTime endDate, DayCount daycount = DayCount.ActAct)
        {
            var nbDaysInPeriod = (double)(endDate - startDate).Days;

            switch (daycount)
            {
                case (DayCount.Act360):
                    return nbDaysInPeriod / (double)360;
                case (DayCount.Act365):
                    return nbDaysInPeriod / (double)365;
                case (DayCount.ActAct):
                
                
                
                
                
                case (DayCount.Days360):
                    var result = (endDate.Year - startDate.Year) * 360.0 + (endDate.Month - startDate.Month) * 30.0 + (Math.Min(endDate.Day, 30.0) - Math.Min(startDate.Day, 30.0));
                    return result / 360;
                default:
                    return nbDaysInPeriod / (double)365;
            }
        }




        public static DateTime CalcAsOf(DateTime now, string time)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(time) || !time.Contains(":"))
                return DateTime.MinValue;
            int hour = System.Convert.ToInt32(time.Split(':')[0]);
            int minutes = System.Convert.ToInt32(time.Replace("AM", "").Replace("PM", "").Trim().Split(':')[1]);
            if (time.ContainsIns("PM"))
                hour = hour + 12;
            
            DateTime clear_time = now.SetTime(hour, minutes);
            if (now > clear_time)
                return now.Date;
            else
            {
                UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime xdt = new Dates.XDateTime(now.Date);
                return xdt.PreviousBusinessDay();
            }
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public static double GetActAct(DateTime startDate, DateTime endDate)
        {
            
            var nbDaysInPeriod = (double)(endDate - startDate).Days;
            if (startDate.Year == endDate.Year || (endDate.Year - 1 == startDate.Year && (startDate.Month > endDate.Month || startDate.Month == endDate.Month && (startDate.Day >= endDate.Day))))
            {
                var den = 365.0;
                if (startDate.Year == endDate.Year && DateTime.IsLeapYear(startDate.Year))
                {
                    den++;
                }
                else
                {

                    if (endDate.Day == 29 && endDate.Month == 2)
                    {
                        den++;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        if (DateTime.IsLeapYear(startDate.Year))
                        {
                            var feb = new DateTime(startDate.Year, 2, 29);
                            if (startDate <= feb && feb <= endDate) den++;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            if (DateTime.IsLeapYear(endDate.Year))
                            {
                                var feb = new DateTime(endDate.Year, 2, 29);
                                if (startDate <= feb && feb <= endDate) den++;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            else
            {
                var nbYears = endDate.Year - startDate.Year + 1;
                var den = nbYears * 365.0;
                for (var i = 0; i < nbYears; i++)
                {
                    if (DateTime.IsLeapYear(startDate.Year + i)) den++;
                }
                den /= nbYears;
                return nbDaysInPeriod / den;
            }
            return nbDaysInPeriod / 365.0;
        }
        public static DateTime ConvertDateInputString(DateTime anchor_date, string dateinput_raw)
        {
            
            
            
            
            
            
            if (dateinput_raw.ContainsIns("LIVE"))
            {
                if (anchor_date.SameDay(DateTime.Today))
                {
                    return anchor_date;
                }
                else
                {
                    throw new Exception("Can only price LIVE with todays anchor date");
                }
            }
            int days = 3;
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(dateinput_raw))
            {
                if (dateinput_raw.Contains('-') || dateinput_raw.Contains('+'))
                {
                    days = ParseTradeDays(dateinput_raw);
                    UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime d = new Dates.XDateTime(anchor_date);
                    d.AddBusinessDays(days);
                    return d.Date;
                }
                else if (dateinput_raw.ContainsIns("PEOM"))
                {
                    return anchor_date.AddMonths(-1).LastDayOfMonth();
                }
                else if (dateinput_raw.ContainsIns("EOM"))
                {
                    return anchor_date.LastDayOfMonth();
                }
                else if (dateinput_raw.ContainsIns("FOM"))
                {
                    return anchor_date.SetDay(1);
                }
                else
                {
                    DateTime s;
                    if (DateTime.TryParse(dateinput_raw, out s))
                        return s;
                }
            }
            throw new Exception("Settle Date Not in Correct Format");
        }


        public static int ParseTradeDays(string day_str)
        {
            int days = -999999999;
            char splitter; ;
            if (day_str.Contains('-'))
                splitter = '-';
            else if (day_str.Contains('+'))
                splitter = '+';
            else
                throw new Exception("Don't know what to do with date");
            days = System.Convert.ToInt32(day_str.Split(splitter)[1]);
            if (splitter == '-')
                days = -days;
            return days;
        }

            public void AddBusinessDays(short days)
            {
                double sign = Convert.ToDouble(Math.Sign(days));
                int unsignedDays = Math.Sign(days) * days;
                for (int i = 0; i < unsignedDays; i++)
                {
                    do
                    {
                        _date = _date.AddDays(sign);
                    }
                    while (!this.IsWorkDay || _holidays.ContainsKey(System.Convert.ToDateTime(_date.ToString(_format))));
                }
            }

            public DateTime CheckIfBDayorGetNext()
            {
                return (this.IsBankOpen) ? _date : this.NextBusinessDay(); 
            }

            public DateTime CheckIfBDayorGetPrev()
            {
                return (this.IsBankOpen) ? _date : this.PreviousBusinessDay();
            }


            public DateTime LastBizDayOfMonth()
            {
                DateTime date = _date;
                date = date.LastDayOfMonth();
                
                while (date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Saturday || date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Sunday || _holidays.ContainsKey(date))
                {
                    date = date.AddDays(-1.0);
                }

                return date;
            }

            public DateTime LastCalendarDayOfMonth()
            {
                DateTime date = _date;
                date = date.LastDayOfMonth();
                return date;
            }
            public DateTime FirstBizDayOfMonth()
            {
                DateTime date = _date;
                date = date.FirstDayOfMonth();
                while (date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Saturday || date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Sunday || _holidays.ContainsKey(date))
                {
                    date = date.AddDays(1.0);
                }

                return date;
            }
            public DateTime NextBusinessDay()
            {
                DateTime date = _date;
                do
                {
                    date = date.AddDays(1.0);
                }
                while (date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Saturday || date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Sunday ||
                    _holidays.ContainsKey(date));
                return date;
            }

            public Nullable<int> BizDatesInBetween(DateTime start, DateTime end)
            {
                DateTime date = start;
                if (start > end)
                    throw new Exception("Wrong Dates (start is after end)");
                int how_many = 0;
                while (date <= end)
                {
                    date = date.AddDays(1.0);
                    if (!_holidays.ContainsValue(date.ToString(_format)) && (date.DayOfWeek != DayOfWeek.Saturday && date.DayOfWeek != DayOfWeek.Sunday))
                        how_many += 1;
                }


                return how_many;
            }
            public DateTime PreviousBusinessDay(int? hour_to_roll_if_current_day_24 = null)
            {
                DateTime date = _date;
                if (null != hour_to_roll_if_current_day_24 && (date == DateTime.Today && DateTime.Now.Hour >= hour_to_roll_if_current_day_24))
                {
                    return date;
                }
                do
                {
                    date = date.AddDays(-1.0);
                }
                while (date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Saturday || date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Sunday || _holidays.ContainsKey(date)); 
                return date;
            }
            public DateTime CheckBusinessDay()
            {
                DateTime date = _date;
                while (date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Saturday || date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Sunday ||
                    _holidays.ContainsValue(date.ToString(_format)))
                {
                    date = date.AddDays(-1.0);
                }
                return date;
            }
            public int NumberOfBusinessDaysFrom(DateTime date)
            {
                double dayToAdd = -1;
                int numberOfBusinessDays = 0;

                if (date < _date)
                {
                    dayToAdd = 1;
                }
                while (_date != date)
                {
                    date = date.AddDays(dayToAdd);
                    if (!(date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Saturday || date.DayOfWeek == DayOfWeek.Sunday || _holidays.ContainsValue(date.ToString(_format))))
                    {
                        
                        numberOfBusinessDays++;
                    }
                }
                return numberOfBusinessDays;
            }

            private void check()
            {
                if (_type == XDateTimeType.Business && !this.IsWorkDay)
                {
                    _date = this.NextBusinessDay();
                }
            }

            #endregion
        }


        public static int CalcAge(DateTime cutoff, DateTime origination_date)
        {
            DateTime cutoff_m = cutoff.SetDay(1);
            int age = 0;
            DateTime close_m = origination_date.SetDay(1);
            
            int days360 = cutoff_m.Days360(close_m);

            if (origination_date.Year < 1901)
            {
                age = 1;
            }
            else
            {
                age = days360 / 30;
            }
            
            
            
            
            return age;
        }

    }

--- FILE: Utils\DB.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public static class DB
    {

        private static string GetInsertsFromList<T>(string parmName, List<T> values)
        {
            List<string> inserts = new List<string>();
            foreach (T t in values)
            {
                string db_write_string = DbWriteString(typeof(T), parmName, t);
                string sql = String.Format("insert into {0} values ({1})", parmName, db_write_string);
                inserts.Add(sql);
            }
            return String.Join(Environment.NewLine, inserts);
        }
        public static string DbWriteString(Type t, string parmName, object val)
        {
            if (null != val)
            {
                if (val.GetType() == typeof(List<string>))
                    val = GetInsertsFromList<string>(parmName, val as List<string>);
                if (val.GetType() == typeof(List<int>))
                    val = GetInsertsFromList<int>(parmName, val as List<int>);
                if (val.GetType() == typeof(List<long>))
                    val = GetInsertsFromList<long>(parmName, val as List<long>);
                if (val.GetType() == typeof(List<DateTime>))
                    val = GetInsertsFromList<DateTime>(parmName, val as List<DateTime>);
                else
                    val = val.ToString().Trim();
            }
            if (null == val)
                return "null";
            if (t == typeof(string) || t == typeof(DateTime) || t == typeof(DateTimeOffset) || t == typeof(TimeSpan) || t == typeof(Char) || t == typeof(object) && (null != val && val.ToString().Length > 0))
            {
                val = "'" + val.ToString().Replace("'", "''") + "'";
            }
            else if (null != val && !String.IsNullOrEmpty(val.ToString()) && t == typeof(bool))
            {
                val = System.Convert.ToBoolean(val) ? 1 : 0;
            }



            if (null == val || val == DBNull.Value || String.IsNullOrEmpty(val.ToString()) || (null != val && val.ToString() == "''") || (t == typeof(double) && val.ToString() == "Infinity"))
                return "null";
            else
                return val.ToString();
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Utils\DDE.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class BBGDDE
    {
        NDde.Client.DdeClient _client;
        int timeout = 30;
        public BBGDDE()
        {
            
        }

        public static BBGDDE _dde;
        public static BBGDDE GetInstance()
        {
            if (null == _dde)
                _dde = new BBGDDE();
            return _dde;
        }


        public void Send(string msg)
        {
            if (null == _client)
                _client = new NDde.Client.DdeClient("winblp", "bbk");

            if (!_client.IsConnected)
                _client.Connect();

            try
            {
                _client.Execute(msg.SwitchCase(), this.timeout);
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {

            }
        }

        public void SendCommandLazy(string ticker, string sector, string command)
        {
            string format = String.Format("{0} <{2}> {1}<go>", ticker, command, sector);
            this.Send(format);
        }
        public void SendMSGE(string to, string subject, string msg)
        {
            this.Send("<blp-1><home>msge<go>" + to + "<tabr>" + subject + "<tabr>" + msg);
        }

        public void SendMSGE(string to, string subject, BBGMSGHelper bmh)
        {
            
            
            this.Send("<blp-1><cancel><home>msge /norte<go>" + to + "<tabr>" + subject + "<tabr>");
            
            System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.SetText(bmh.Message);
            System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(1500);

            this.Send("<paste>");

            

        }


        public void BlastLines(BBGMSGHelper hh)
        {
            
            
            
            
        }

    }


    public class BBGMSGHelper
    {
        public List<string> lines = new List<string>();
        int max_len = 80;
        public BBGMSGHelper()
        {

        }

        public List<string> exempt_spaces = new List<string>();

        public string blast_subject = null;

        public void AddBreak(char break_char)
        {
            string msg = "";
            for (int i = 0; i != max_len; i++)
                msg += break_char;
            lines.Add(msg);
        }

        public void AddLine(string line)
        {
            if (line.Length > max_len)
                throw new Exception("Line Too Long");
            else
                line = line.PadRight(max_len);
            lines.Add(line);
        }

        List<BBGHeaderConfig> _headers = new List<BBGHeaderConfig>();

        public BBGHeaderConfig GetHeader(string which)
        {
            foreach (BBGHeaderConfig bhc in _headers)
            {
                if (bhc.name == which)
                    return bhc;
            }
            return null;
        }

        public DataTable _tbl;
        public void AddHeader(BBGHeaderConfig bhc)
        {
            if (null == _tbl)
                _tbl = new DataTable();
            _tbl.Columns.Add(bhc.name, typeof(string));
            _headers.Add(bhc);
        }

        private string _current_line = "";
        private DataRow _active_row;
        public void AppendNonHeaderTxt(string header_name, object value, string format_override)
        {
            BBGHeaderConfig bhc = FindHeader(header_name);


            if (null == bhc)
                return;
            AppendNonHeaderTxt(bhc, value, format_override);
        }

        public void AppendNonHeaderTxt(string header_name, object value)
        {
            BBGHeaderConfig bhc = FindHeader(header_name);
            if (null == bhc)
                return;
            AppendNonHeaderTxt(bhc, value, null);
        }




        public void AppendNonHeaderTxt(BBGHeaderConfig bhc, object value, string format_override)
        {

            if (null == value)
                value = "";
            string raw = value.ToString();
            string message = "";
            string formatted = raw;
            string format = bhc.format;
            if (null != format_override)
                format = format_override;
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(format))
            {
                string fmt = "{0:" + format + "}";
                formatted = String.Format(fmt, value);
            }

            if (bhc.text_align == BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT)
                message += formatted.PadLeft(bhc.length);
            else if (bhc.text_align == BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT)
                message += formatted.PadRight(bhc.length);
            else if (bhc.text_align == BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER)
                message += formatted.PadCenter(bhc.length);

            if (null == _active_row)
                _active_row = _tbl.Rows.Add();
            _active_row[bhc.name] = message;

            message += bhc.right_seperator;
            _current_line += message;
        }


        public BBGHeaderConfig FindHeader(string header_name)
        {
            foreach (BBGHeaderConfig bhc in _headers)
            {
                if (bhc.name.ToUpper() == header_name.ToUpper())
                {
                    return bhc;
                }
            }
            return null;
        }

        public void AppendLineFinalize()
        {
            _active_row.AcceptChanges();
            _active_row = null;
            lines.Add(_current_line);
            _current_line = "";
        }



        public void AddHeaderLine()
        {
            string message = "";
            foreach (BBGHeaderConfig bhc in _headers)
            {

                if (bhc.header_align == BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT)
                    message += bhc.name.PadLeft(bhc.length);
                else if (bhc.header_align == BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT)
                    message += bhc.name.PadRight(bhc.length);
                else if (bhc.header_align == BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER)
                    message += bhc.name.PadCenter(bhc.length);

                message += bhc.right_seperator;
            }
            lines.Add(message);
        }

        public string Message
        {
            get
            {
                return String.Join(Environment.NewLine, lines.ToArray());
            }
        }

    }



}


--- FILE: Utils\Docs.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public static class Docs
    {




        public static List<string> GenerateDoc<T>(string source_file, string final_file_name, Dictionary<string, T> fields_raw, bool silent,FieldLib.Fields f)
        {

            var fields = UtilsLib.Clean.HtmlFormat<T>(fields_raw);
            List<string> errors = new List<string>();
            try
            {
                List<string> missing = UtilsLib.Docs.GenerateDoc(fields, source_file, final_file_name,f,null);
                if (missing.Count != 0)
                {
                    string missing_msg = String.Join("\n", missing);
                    errors.AddRange(missing);
                    if(!silent)
                        MessageBox.Show(missing_msg, "Hey Genius...You're missing some required merge fields");
                }

              
            }
            catch(Exception n)
            {
                  errors.Add(n.Message);
            }
            return errors;
        }

        public delegate void PostReplaceOperation(UtilsLib.WordLib w);

    
        
        public static List<string> GenerateDoc(Dictionary<string,object> fields, string source_file, string full_file_name,Fields fieldHelper, PostReplaceOperation pro)
        {

            lock (fields)
            {
                var common_variables = UtilsLib.Clean.GetCommonVariables().ToDictionary(x => x.Key.Replace("@", ""), k => k.Value as string);
                var unique_common_variables = common_variables.Where(x => !fields.ContainsKey(x.Key));

                foreach (var f in unique_common_variables)
                {
                    fields.Add(f.Key, f.Value);
                }
            }
            UtilsLib.WordLib w = new UtilsLib.WordLib();
            w.OpenFile(source_file,false);

            
            List<string> blanks = w.MergeFields<object>(fields, null, fieldHelper);
            List<string> remaining = w.RemainingMergeFields();
            var res = remaining.Distinct().ToDictionary(x => x, x => $"{x.ToUpper()}");
            w.MergeFields(res, w.ChangeSelectedColor, fieldHelper);
            
            foreach(var f in fields)
            {
                if (f.Key.ContainsIns("html_"))
                {
                    w.InsertHTML(f.Key, f.Value as string);
                }

                if (f.Key.ContainsIns("table_"))
                {
                    w.InsertTable(f.Key,(DataTable) f.Value,fieldHelper);
                }
            }

            
            
            if (null != pro)
                pro(w);
            if(full_file_name.ContainsIns(".pdf"))
                w.SaveAsPDF(full_file_name, true);
            else
                w.SaveAs(full_file_name, true);
            w.Close(false);
            w.Exit(false);

            return remaining;
        }



    }
}


--- FILE: Utils\Environment.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public static class EnviornmentLib
    {
        public static string GetEnvironmentVariableFirstNonNull(IEnumerable<string> vars)
        {
            foreach(string s in vars)
            {
                string value = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(s);
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(value))
                    return value;
            }
            return null;
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Utils\Error.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class Error
    {
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        



        public static void SendDefaultError(Exception n, string extra = null, IEnumerable<object> debug_variables = null, IEnumerable<string> attach_files = null)
        {
            SendError(null, null, null, n, extra,true, true, debug_variables, attach_files);
        }


        public static void SendScreenshot(string filename_base, string to)
        {
            string file = UtilsLib.Windows.GetScreenshotActiveWindow(filename_base);
            UtilsLib.Mail m = new Mail(null, CommonInterfaces.Constants.SMTP_SERVER, null, null, null);
            m.SendSMTPMail(to, null, null, filename_base, null, new string[] { file }, false, true, UtilsLib.Mail.MyEmail);
        }

        private static string GetApplicationName()
        {
            return System.Reflection.Assembly.GetCallingAssembly()?.ManifestModule.Name.Replace(".exe", "");
        }
        private static string GetErrorEmail()
        {
            string default_mail = CommonInterfaces.Constants.ERROR_EMAIL;
            string application = GetApplicationName();

            string my_email = UtilsLib.Mail.MyEmail;
            if (Environment.UserName.Contains("Dan") || (null != my_email && my_email.ContainsIns("saluda")))
                default_mail = "dan@unlock.com";
            return default_mail;
        }
        public static void SendError(string to, string from, string subject, Exception n, string extra, bool smtp = true, bool include_screenshot = false, IEnumerable<object> variable_dump = null,IEnumerable<string> attach_files = null)
        {

           var build_time = Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().GetBuildTime();
            string dump = "";
            if (null != variable_dump)
            {
                foreach (object o in variable_dump)
                {
                    using (var writer = new System.IO.StringWriter())
                    {
                        dump += writer.ToString() + "\n\n";
                    };
                }
            }
            string body = $"MACHINE: {Environment.MachineName}\n";
            string external_ip = UtilsLib.Network.GetExternalIPAddress();
            body += $"OS VERSION: {Environment.OSVersion}\n";
            body += $"BUILD TIME: {build_time}\n";
            body += $"EXTERNAL IP: {external_ip}\n\n";
            



            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(extra))
                body += extra + Environment.NewLine;

            List<string> files = new List<string>();

            if(include_screenshot)
            {
                string file = UtilsLib.Windows.GetScreenshotActiveWindow("Debug Screenshot");
                files.Add(file);
            }
            if(null != attach_files)
            {
                files.AddRange(attach_files);
            }


            if (null != n)
                body += n.ToString() + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine + n.StackTrace;
            
            
            if (null != n)
                body += n.InnerException + Environment.NewLine;

            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(subject))
            {
                string application = GetApplicationName();
                subject = String.Format("[{0} ERROR] - {1}", application, DateTime.Now);
            }
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(from))
                from = Environment.UserName + "@" + CommonInterfaces.Constants.DEFAULT_EMAIL_DOMAIN;
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(to))
            {
                to = GetErrorEmail();
            }
            Mail m = new Mail(from, CommonInterfaces.Constants.SMTP_SERVER, CommonInterfaces.Constants.SMTP_USER, CommonInterfaces.Constants.SMTP_PASS, CommonInterfaces.Constants.SMTP_PORT);
            try
            {
                if (smtp)
                    m.SendSMTPMail(to, null, null, subject, body, files, false, true, from,
                        System.Net.Mail.MailPriority.High);
                else
                    m.SendMail(to, null, null, subject, body, files, false, true, from);
            }
            catch (Exception new_e)
            {
                if (!smtp)
                    m.SendSMTPMail(to, null, null, "FAILSAFE MODE: " + subject, body, files, false, true, from, System.Net.Mail.MailPriority.High);
                else
                    m.SendMail(to, null, null, "FAILSAFE MODE: " + subject, body, files, false, true, from);
            }

        }

    }
}


--- FILE: Utils\ETA.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class ETA : IETA
    {
        private double _total;
        public double total { get {  return _total; } }
        private double _count;
        public bool do_summary_on_completion { get; set; }
        private DateTime _start;
        private IWriter _writer;
        private string report_string = "[{4}] - {0} of {1} - {2:0.0}% ETA: {3}";
        private string completion_string = "Operation Complete - Avg Time: {0:hh\\:mm\\:ss} - Total Time: {1:hh\\:mm\\:ss} - Finish Time: {2}";

        public IWriter writer { get { return _writer; } }
        

        public string GetElapsedTime(string format)
        {
            return (DateTime.Now - _start).ToString(format);
        }
        public ETA(int total, IWriter writer)
        {
            ETAInternal(total, writer);
        }

        public void SetWriter(IWriter writer)
        {
            _writer = writer;
        }
        private void ETAInternal(int total, IWriter writer)
        {
            SetTotal(total);
            if (null == _writer)
                _writer = writer;
            do_summary_on_completion = false;
        }

        public virtual void SetTotal(int total)
        {
            _total = total;
            _start = DateTime.Now;
        }
        public void Reset(int total, IWriter writer)
        {
            ETAInternal(total, writer);
        }

        public void SetReportString(string report_string)
        {
            this.report_string = report_string;
        }

        public void SetCompletionString(string completion_string)
        {
            this.completion_string = completion_string;
        }
        public System.Windows.Forms.Control _parent;
        public void SetParent(System.Windows.Forms.Control ctrl)
        {
            _parent = ctrl;
        }


        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public virtual void Complete()
        {
            if (null != _writer)
                _writer(null);
        }
        public virtual void IncrementAndReport(Nullable<int> work_done = 1)
        {
            IncrementAndReport(work_done, 1);
        }
        public virtual void IncrementAndReport(Nullable<int> work_done, int report_every)
        {
            if (null != work_done)
                _count += work_done.Value;
            else
                _count++;
            TimeSpan ts = DateTime.Now - _start;
            double secs_avg = ts.TotalSeconds / _count;

            if (null != _writer)
            {
                DateTime eta = DateTime.Now.AddSeconds(secs_avg * (_total - _count));
                string finish_time_string = "h:mm tt";
                if (eta.Day != DateTime.Today.Day)
                    finish_time_string = "M/d h:mm tt";
                string msg = String.Format(report_string, _count, _total, (_count / _total) * 100.0,
                    eta.ToString(finish_time_string), DateTime.Now);
                if (_count == _total)
                {
                    if (do_summary_on_completion)
                    {
                        TimeSpan avg = new TimeSpan(0, 0, (int)secs_avg);
                        TimeSpan total = (DateTime.Now - _start);
                        msg = String.Format(completion_string, avg, total, DateTime.Now);
                    }
                }
                double each = _count % report_every;
                if (each == 0 && null != _writer)
                {
                    
                    _writer(msg);
                }
            }

            if (_count == _total)
            {
                Complete();
            }
        }
    }
}

        public Excel(string filename)
        {
            _app = new Application();
            if(null != filename)
                _app.Workbooks.Open(filename);
            IntPtr hwnd = new IntPtr(_app.Hwnd);
            IntPtr processId;
            UtilsLib.Windows.GetWindowThreadProcessId(hwnd, out processId);
            _process = Process.GetProcessById(processId.ToInt32());
        }

            return _process.Id;
        }

        public static ExcelVersion GetExcelVersion(object applicationClass)
        {
            if (applicationClass == null)
                throw new ArgumentNullException("applicationClass");

            PropertyInfo property = applicationClass.GetType().GetProperty("HinstancePtr", BindingFlags.Instance | BindingFlags.Public);
            if (property == null)
                return ExcelVersion.Excel;

            return (System.Runtime.InteropServices.Marshal.SizeOf(property.GetValue(applicationClass, null)) == 8) ? ExcelVersion.Excel2010_64 : ExcelVersion.Excel2010_32;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public enum ExcelVersion
        {
            Excel, 
            Excel2010_32,
            Excel2010_64
        }

        public static string RangeToHTML(Application _app, Range r)
        {

            r.Copy();
            string temp = Path.GetTempFileName() + ".html";
            Workbook wb = _app.Workbooks.Add(1);
            Worksheet ws = (Worksheet)wb.Sheets[1];
            
            
            
            ws.get_Range("A1").PasteSpecial(XlPasteType.xlPasteValues);
            ws.get_Range("A1").PasteSpecial(XlPasteType.xlPasteFormats);
            ws.get_Range("A1").PasteSpecial(XlPasteType.xlPasteColumnWidths);
            ws.UsedRange.Columns.Select();
            ws.UsedRange.Columns.AutoFit();
            ws.Select();
            _app.CutCopyMode = (Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlCutCopyMode)0;
            wb.PublishObjects.Add(XlSourceType.xlSourceSheet, temp, ws.Name, ws.Name, XlHtmlType.xlHtmlStatic, "dsg", "").Publish(true);
            string html = File.ReadAllText(temp);
            File.Delete(temp);
            wb.Close(false);
            return html.Replace("�", "");
        }

        public enum EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE { XLSB, CSV, XLSX, XLS}

        public static string GetExtensionFromFormat(EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE fmt)
        {
            if (fmt == EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSB)
                return ".xlsb";
            if (fmt == EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.CSV)
                return ".csv";
            if (fmt == EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSX)
                return ".xlsx";
            if (fmt == EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLS)
                return ".xls";
            return ".xls";
        }

        public static XLFileFormatSimple GetXLFileFormatSimple(EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE fmt)
        {
            if (fmt == EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSB)
                return XLFileFormatSimple.BINARY;
            if (fmt == EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.CSV)
                return XLFileFormatSimple.CSV;
            if (fmt == EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLS)
                return XLFileFormatSimple.XLS;
            if (fmt == EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSX)
                return XLFileFormatSimple.XLSX;
            return XLFileFormatSimple.NORMAL;
        }

        public static EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE GetXLFileFormatSimple(string fmt)
        {
            fmt = fmt.ToUpper();
            if (fmt == "XLSB")
                return EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSB;
            fmt = fmt.ToUpper();
            if (fmt == "XLS")
                return EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLS;
            fmt = fmt.ToUpper();
            if (fmt == "XLSX")
                return EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSX;
            if (fmt == "CSV")
                return EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.CSV;
            return EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSB;
        }
        public static string CreateQuickExcel(string base_file, IEnumerable<DataTable> results, bool apply_foster_pref, EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE output_format = EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSB, bool do_timestamp = true, Fields fields = null)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(base_file))
                base_file = "QuickExport";
            string temp = UtilsLib.FileLib.GetQuickUniqueFile(base_file, ".csv", true, do_timestamp);
            string final_ext = GetExtensionFromFormat(output_format);
            string final = UtilsLib.FileLib.GetQuickUniqueFile(base_file, final_ext, true, do_timestamp);
            
            UtilsLib.Excel xl = new Excel(null);
            int q = 1;
            
            xl.ClearAndSetupSheets(results.Select(n => n.TableName));
            

  

            foreach (DataTable table in results)
            
            {
                
                xl.WriteRange(table.TableName, "A1", table, true); 
                int colnum = 0;
                foreach(DataColumn col in table.Columns)
                {
                    if(null != fields)
                    {
                        var fh = fields[col.ColumnName];
                        string entire_colum = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.ColumnNumberToLetter(colnum);
                        if (null != fh)
                        {
                            string format = (null != fh.excel_format) ? fh.excel_format : fh.display_format;
                            if(!String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(format))
                                xl.FormatEntireColumn(table.TableName, entire_colum, format);


                        }
                        if(col.DataType == typeof(DateTime) || col.DataType == typeof(double) || col.DataType == typeof(Decimal))
                        {
                            xl.AlignEntireColumn(table.TableName, entire_colum, XlHAlign.xlHAlignRight);
                        }
                    }
                    colnum++;
                }
                q++;
            }
            if (apply_foster_pref)
                ApplyFosterPreferenceStatic(xl._app);

            var fmt = GetXLFileFormatSimple(output_format);
            xl.SelectWorksheet(1);
            xl.Save(final, fmt);
            xl.Close();

            UtilsLib.FileLib.WaitForFile(final, 3000);
            
            return final;
        }

        public static void ApplyFosterPreferenceStatic(Application _app)
        {

            foreach (Worksheet ws in _app.Worksheets)
            {
                ws.Activate();
                _app.ActiveWindow.Zoom = 85;
                SetPreferredHeadersInternal(ws);
                ws.UsedRange.EntireColumn.AutoFit();
            }
        }

        public Range GetRange(string worksheet, string address)
        {
            Range r;
            try
            {
                if (null == worksheet)
                    r = _app.get_Range(address);
                else
                    r = ((Worksheet)_app.Sheets[worksheet]).get_Range(address);
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                return null;
            }
            return r;
        }


        public static int SetPreferredHeadersInternal(Worksheet worksheet)
        {

            
            
            int last_col = worksheet.UsedRange.Columns.Count - 1;
            string col = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.ColumnNumberToLetter(last_col);
            Range r = ((Range)worksheet.get_Range("A1:" + col + "1"));
            r.Font.Bold = true;
            r.Font.TintAndShade = 0;
            r.Font.ThemeColor = XlThemeColor.xlThemeColorDark1;
            r.HorizontalAlignment = XlHAlign.xlHAlignCenter;
            r.Interior.ThemeColor = XlThemeColor.xlThemeColorLight1;
            r.Interior.TintAndShade = 0;
            var v = r.Application.Calculation;
            r.Application.Calculation = XlCalculation.xlCalculationManual;
            bool is_header_row = false;
            foreach (Range s in r.Cells)
            {
                if (null != s.Text && !String.IsNullOrEmpty(s.Text.ToString()))
                {
                    s.Value = s.Text.ToString().ToUpper();
                    if (s.Row == 1)
                    {
                        is_header_row = true;
                        r.Application.ScreenUpdating = false;
                        r.Application.ActiveWindow.SplitRow = 1;
                        r.Application.ActiveWindow.FreezePanes = true;
                        r.EntireRow.Font.Bold = true;
                        if (null != s.Value)
                        {
                            string format = UtilsLib.Clean.GetFormatFromColumnName(s.Text as string);
                            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(format))
                            {
                                s.EntireColumn.NumberFormat = format;
                                string replace_col = UtilsLib.Clean.NiceColumnName(s.Text as string);
                                s.Value = replace_col;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            if (is_header_row)
            {
                
                
                
                
                
                
                           
                           
                           
                r.Select();
                ((dynamic) r.Application.Selection).AutoFilter();
            }
            r.EntireColumn.AutoFit();
            r.Application.Calculation = v;
            return r.Row;
        }

        public void ClearAndSetupSheets(IEnumerable<string> sheet_names)
        {
            List<string> sheets_to_delete = new List<string>();
            if (null == _app.ActiveWorkbook)
                _app.Workbooks.Add();
            foreach (Worksheet v in _app.ActiveWorkbook.Worksheets)
            {
                sheets_to_delete.Add(v.Name);
            }
            Worksheet last = null;
            int i = _app.ActiveWorkbook.Sheets.Count;
            foreach (string new_sheet in sheet_names)
            {
                Worksheet ws = (Worksheet)_app.ActiveWorkbook.Sheets.Add(Type.Missing, (Worksheet)_app.Worksheets[i]);
                ws.Name = new_sheet;
                last = ws;
                i++;
            }
            foreach (string del in sheets_to_delete)
            {
                ((Worksheet)_app.Worksheets[del]).Delete();
            }
        }


        public static void WriteRange(string worksheet, string range, DataTable table, Application _app, int row_offset_zero_based, int column_offset_zero_based, bool include_headers)
        {
            if (null == table || table.Rows.Count == 0)
                return;
            object[,] arr = DataTableToArray(table, include_headers);
            Range r = null;
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(worksheet))
            {
                
                r = ((Worksheet)_app.Sheets[worksheet]).get_Range(range);
            }
            else
                r = ((Range)_app.get_Range(range));
            Range f = r.get_Offset(row_offset_zero_based, column_offset_zero_based);
            int rows = f.Rows.Count;
            int columns = r.Columns.Count;
            Range one = f.get_Resize(rows - row_offset_zero_based, columns - column_offset_zero_based);

            Range two = one.get_Resize(table.Rows.Count + (include_headers == true ? 1 : 0), table.Columns.Count);
            string address = two.get_Address();
            _app.Calculation = XlCalculation.xlCalculationManual;
            
            two.NumberFormat = "@";
            two.Value = arr;
            _app.Calculation = XlCalculation.xlCalculationAutomatic;
        }

        public static ushort GetImageArchitecture(string filepath)
        {
            using (var stream = new System.IO.FileStream(filepath, System.IO.FileMode.Open, System.IO.FileAccess.Read))
            using (var reader = new System.IO.BinaryReader(stream))
            {
                
                if (reader.ReadUInt16() != 23117)
                    throw new BadImageFormatException("Not a valid Portable Executable image", filepath);

                
                stream.Seek(0x3A, System.IO.SeekOrigin.Current);
                stream.Seek(reader.ReadUInt32(), System.IO.SeekOrigin.Begin);

                
                if (reader.ReadUInt32() != 17744)
                    throw new BadImageFormatException("Not a valid Portable Executable image", filepath);

                
                stream.Seek(20, System.IO.SeekOrigin.Current);
                return reader.ReadUInt16();
            }
        }
        public void LoadAddins(string path, bool attempt_bit_specific)
        {
            
            
            if (!Directory.Exists(path))
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Warning: Addin directory not found");
                return;
            }
            foreach (string file in System.IO.Directory.GetFiles(path, "*.xl*"))
            {
                FileInfo f = new FileInfo(file);
                string full_name = Path.Combine(f.Directory.FullName, Path.GetFileName(file));
                if (full_name.Contains("~"))
                    continue;
                bool success = false;
                if (f.Extension == ".xll")
                {
                    if (attempt_bit_specific)
                    {
                        var ver = UtilsLib.Excel.GetExcelVersion(_app);
                        string filename_without_ext = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(file);
                        string filename_ext = Path.GetExtension(file);
                        string full_name_64 = Path.Combine(f.Directory.FullName, filename_without_ext + "-x64" + filename_ext);
                        if (ver == ExcelVersion.Excel2010_64 && System.IO.File.Exists(full_name_64))
                        {
                            continue;
                        }
                        if ((ver == ExcelVersion.Excel2010_32 || ver == ExcelVersion.Excel) && full_name.Contains("-x64"))
                        {
                            continue;
                        }
                    }
                    success = _app.RegisterXLL(file);
                }
                else
                    _app.Workbooks.Open(full_name, false, true);
                
                
                
            }
            

        }


        public void Save()
        {
            Save(_app.ActiveWorkbook.FullName, null);
        }

        public enum XLFileFormatSimple { NORMAL, BINARY , CSV, XLS, XLSX}
        private Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlFileFormat GetFileType(Nullable<XLFileFormatSimple> fmt)
        {
            if (null == fmt)
                return Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlFileFormat.xlOpenXMLWorkbook;

            else if (fmt.Value == XLFileFormatSimple.XLSX)
                return Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlFileFormat.xlOpenXMLWorkbook;
            else if (fmt.Value == XLFileFormatSimple.XLS)
                return Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlFileFormat.xlWorkbookNormal;
            else if (fmt.Value == XLFileFormatSimple.BINARY)
                return Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlFileFormat.xlExcel12;
            else if (fmt.Value == XLFileFormatSimple.CSV)
                return Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlFileFormat.xlCSV;
            return Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlFileFormat.xlWorkbookNormal;
        }

        public void Save(string full_name, Nullable<XLFileFormatSimple> file_format)
        {
            Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlFileFormat fmt = Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlFileFormat.xlWorkbookNormal;
            if (null != file_format)
            {
                fmt = GetFileType(file_format.Value);
            }

            _app.DisplayAlerts = false;
            _app.ActiveWorkbook.SaveAs(full_name, fmt, Type.Missing, Type.Missing, false, false, Microsoft.Office.Interop.Excel.XlSaveAsAccessMode.xlNoChange, Type.Missing, Type.Missing, Type.Missing, Type.Missing, Type.Missing);
            _app.DisplayAlerts = true;
            
        }

        public void Close()
        {
            _app.Application.Quit();

            int pid = _process.Id;
            _process.Kill(); 
            
            UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.KillProcess(pid, 3000);

            System.GC.Collect();
            System.GC.WaitForPendingFinalizers();
            System.GC.Collect();
            System.GC.WaitForPendingFinalizers();

        }

            return filename;
        }


        public static DataTable InsertHeadersInDataTable(DataTable dt)
        {
            DataTable clone = dt.Clone();
            foreach (DataColumn col in clone.Columns)
                col.DataType = typeof(object);

            DataRow header = clone.NewRow();
            for (int i = 0; i != clone.Columns.Count; i++)
            {
                header[i] = clone.Columns[i].Caption;
            }
            clone.Rows.InsertAt(header, 0);

            foreach (DataRow row in dt.Rows)
            {
                clone.Rows.Add(row.ItemArray);
            }

            return clone;
        }
        public static object[,] DataTableToArray(DataTable dt, bool include_headers)
        {

            if (include_headers)
            {
                dt = InsertHeadersInDataTable(dt);
            }

            object[,] arr = new object[dt.Rows.Count, dt.Columns.Count];

            for (int r = 0; r < dt.Rows.Count; r++)
            {
                DataRow dr = dt.Rows[r];
                for (int c = 0; c != dt.Columns.Count; c++)
                {
                    arr[r, c] = dr[c];
                }
            }
            return arr;


            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        public static object[] GetRowFromObjectArray(object[,] array, int zero_based_row)
        {
            List<object> arr = new List<object>();
            for (int i = 0; i != array.GetLength(1); i++)
            {
                object o = array[zero_based_row, i];
                if (null != o && o.ToString() == "ExcelDna.Integration.ExcelEmpty" || (null != o && String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(o.ToString())))
                    o = null;
                
                arr.Add(o);
            }
            return arr.ToArray();
        }



        public static DataTable ArrayToVerticleDataTable<T>(T[] array)
        {
            DataTable tbl = new DataTable();
            tbl.Columns.Add("lost_interest", typeof(T));
            foreach (T cow in array)
            {

                DataRow row = tbl.Rows.Add(cow);
                
                
            }
            return tbl;
        }

        public static object[,] ArrayToVerticleObjectArray<T>(T[] array)
        {
            object[,] new_array = new object[1, array.Length];

            for (int i = 0; i != array.Length; i++)
            {
                new_array[0, i] = array[i];
            }
            return new_array;
        }



        public static DataTable ArrayToDataTable(object[,] array, bool first_row_contains_headers,Dictionary<string,Type> overrides)
        {
            DataSet set = new DataSet();
            DataTable tbl = set.Tables.Add();
            


            int start = 0;
            if (first_row_contains_headers)
                start = 1;


            
            {
                for (int i = 0; i != array.GetLength(1); i++)
                {
                    Type t = typeof(object);
                    
                    
                    
                    object column_name_raw = array[0, i];
                    string column_name = null;
                    if (array.GetLength(0) > 0)
                    {
                        t = typeof(object);
                        if (null != array[0, i])
                            t = array[0, i].GetType();
                    }
                    if (!first_row_contains_headers || null == column_name_raw || (null != column_name_raw && String.IsNullOrEmpty(column_name_raw.ToString())))
                        column_name = "Column" + i.ToString().Trim();
                    else
                        column_name = column_name_raw.ToString().Trim();
                    if (tbl.Columns.Contains(column_name))
                    {
                        string base_column_name = column_name;
                        for (int n = 1; n != 1000; n++)
                        {
                            column_name = base_column_name + (n.ToString().Trim());
                            if (!tbl.Columns.Contains(column_name))
                                break;
                        }
                    }
                    if(null != overrides && overrides.ContainsKeyIns(column_name))
                    {
                        t = overrides.GetKeyIns(column_name);
                    }
                    tbl.Columns.Add(column_name, t);
                }
            }

            for (int i = start; i != array.GetLength(0); i++)
            {
                object[] arr = GetRowFromObjectArray(array, i);
                DataRow row = tbl.Rows.Add(arr);
                
                
                
            }
            List<DataColumn> cols2change = new List<DataColumn>();
            if (null == overrides)
            {
                
                foreach (DataColumn col in tbl.Columns)
                {
                    bool all_columns_date = AllColumnValuesDates(col);
                    if (all_columns_date == true && (col.Caption.ToUpper().Contains("INVESTMENT_PAYMENT") || col.Caption.ToUpper().Contains("NET_WIRE_AMT") || col.Caption.ToUpper().Replace("_"," ").Contains("LOAN ID")))
                        all_columns_date = false;
                    if (all_columns_date && col.DataType != typeof(DateTime))
                    {
                        cols2change.Add(col);
                        
                    }
                }
            }

            cols2change.ForEach(n => n.ChangeDataType(typeof(DateTime)));
            return tbl;
        }

        public static bool AllColumnValuesDates(DataColumn col)
        {
            
            
            IEnumerable<DataRow> rows = null;
            
            
            
                rows = col.Table.AsEnumerable();

            
            foreach (DataRow row in rows)
            {
                object val = row[col];
                if (null == val)
                    continue;
                double d;
                if(Double.TryParse(val.ToString(),out d))
                {
     
                    if((d > 0 && d <73051) && !d.ToString().Contains("."))
                    {
                        try
                        {
                            DateTime dt = DateTime.FromOADate(d);
                            if (dt.Year < 1980 || dt.Year > 2050)
                            {
                                return false;
                            }

                        }
                        catch(Exception n)
                        {
                            return false;
                        }

                    }
                    else
                        return false;

                }
                else
                {
                    return false;
                }
                
            }

            return true;
        }



    }
}

namespace UtilsLib
