        public static bool ContainsInvalidCharacters(string filename)
        {
            return ContainsInvalidCharacters(filename, false);
        }

        public static string LastModifiedFileInFolder(string folder_name)
        {
            var directory = new DirectoryInfo(folder_name);

            var myFile = directory.GetFiles()
                         .OrderByDescending(f => f.LastWriteTime)
                         .First();
            return myFile.FullName;
        }
        public static bool ContainsInvalidCharacters(string filename, bool include_excel_restrictions)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(filename))
                return true;
            string illegal = "\"M\"\\a/ry/ h**ad:>> a\\/:*?\"| li*tt|le|| la\"mb.?";
            if (include_excel_restrictions)
                illegal += "[]";
            string invalid = new string(Path.GetInvalidFileNameChars()) + new string(Path.GetInvalidPathChars());

            foreach (char c in invalid)
            {
                if (filename.Contains(c))
                    return true;
                
            }
            return false;
        }

        public static string PickRandomFileFromDir(string full_dir)
        {
            string[] all_files = System.IO.Directory.GetFiles(full_dir);
            if (all_files.Length == 0)
                return null;
            Random r = new Random();
            int rInt = r.Next(0, all_files.Length);
            return all_files[rInt];
        }

            Directory.CreateDirectory(directory);

            File.SetAttributes(full_file_path, FileAttributes.ReadOnly);

        public static string CopyFileToDirectorySmartly(string source_full, string target_directory, bool overwrite)
        {

            DirectoryInfo source = new DirectoryInfo(source_full);
            DirectoryInfo target = new DirectoryInfo(target_directory);

            Directory.CreateDirectory(target.FullName);

            string filename = Path.GetFileName(source_full);
            string final_full = Path.Combine(target_directory, filename);

            FileInfo fi = new FileInfo(source_full);
            
            fi.CopyTo(final_full, overwrite);
            return final_full;
        }
        public static void CopyFileReallySmartly(string source_full, string target_filename, bool overwrite)
        {

            DirectoryInfo source = new DirectoryInfo(source_full);

            string directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(target_filename);
            if (!Directory.Exists(directory))
                Directory.CreateDirectory(directory);

            

            
            

            FileInfo fi = new FileInfo(source_full);
            
            fi.CopyTo(target_filename, overwrite);

        }


        public static void WriteFileSmartly(string full_path, bool overwrite, string contents)
        {
            string directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(full_path);
            DirectoryInfo source = new DirectoryInfo(directory);

            if (!Directory.Exists(directory))
                Directory.CreateDirectory(directory);

            if (overwrite && File.Exists(full_path))
                File.Delete(full_path);
            File.WriteAllText(full_path, contents);

        }


        public static void RoboCopy(string src, string dst)
        {
            Process p = new Process();
            p.StartInfo.Arguments = string.Format("Robocopy \"{0}\" \"{1}\"", src, dst);
            p.StartInfo.FileName = "CMD.EXE";
            
            
            p.Start();
            p.WaitForExit();
        }


        public static List<string> CopyFullDirectory(string source_full, string target_full, IETA _eta,bool overwrite,bool truncate_long_names,Nullable<DateTime> only_files_modified_before = null)
        {


            List<string> files = new List<string>();



            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            

            
            

            DirectoryInfo source = new DirectoryInfo(source_full);
            DirectoryInfo target = new DirectoryInfo(target_full);

            if (null != _eta && _eta.total == -1)
            {
                int total = (new DirectoryInfo(source_full).GetFiles("*", SearchOption.AllDirectories)).Length;
                _eta.SetTotal(total);
            }
            if(!Directory.Exists(target.FullName))
                Directory.CreateDirectory(target.FullName);
            
            

            try
            {
                foreach (FileInfo fi in source.GetFiles())
                {
                    if (null != only_files_modified_before && fi.LastWriteTime > only_files_modified_before.Value)
                        continue;
                    
                    
                    
                    if (null != _eta)
                    {
                        _eta.IncrementAndReport();
                    }
                    
                    string new_file = Path.Combine(target.FullName, fi.Name);
                    

                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    

                    if (File.Exists(new_file) && !overwrite)
                    {

                    }
                    else
                    {
                        try
                        {
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                              
                            fi.CopyTo(new_file, true);
                            
                            
                            files.Add(new_file);
                        }
                        catch (DirectoryNotFoundException de)
                        {
                            Console.WriteLine("Directory Failed: " + new_file);
                        }
                        catch (IOException io)
                        {
                            Console.WriteLine("Filed Failed: " + new_file);
                        }

                    }
  
                }
            }
            catch(System.Exception n)
            {

            }
            finally
            {
        
            }


            
            if (!source.Exists)
            {

            }
            else
            {
                foreach (DirectoryInfo diSourceSubDir in source.GetDirectories())
                {
                    
                    DirectoryInfo nextTargetSubDir = target.CreateSubdirectory(diSourceSubDir.Name);
                    

                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    var files_each = CopyFullDirectory(diSourceSubDir.FullName, nextTargetSubDir.FullName, null, overwrite, truncate_long_names,only_files_modified_before);
                    files.AddRange(files_each);
                }
            }
            return files;
        }

        public static bool CreateCommonStartMenuIfNotExists(string program_location, string program_name, string hotkey)
        {
            bool exists = CommonStartMenuExists(program_location, program_name);
            if (!exists)
            {
                string commonStartMenuPath = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.CommonStartMenu);
                string appStartMenuPath = Path.Combine(commonStartMenuPath, "Programs", program_name + ".lnk");

                CreateShortCutGeneric(appStartMenuPath, program_location, program_name, hotkey);
                return true;
            }
            return false;

        }
        public static bool CreateQuickLaunchIfNotExists(string shortcut_location, string program_name, string program_location, string hotkey)
        {
            bool exists = QuickLaunchExists(shortcut_location, program_name);
            if (!exists)
            {
                string location = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.ApplicationData) + "\\Microsoft\\Internet Explorer\\Quick Launch\\" + program_name + ".lnk";
                CreateShortCutGeneric(location, program_location, program_name, hotkey);
                return true;
            }
            return false;

        }

        public static void CreateShortCutGeneric(string shortcutAddress, string program_location, string program_name, string hotkey)
        {
            WshShell shell = new WshShell();
            IWshShortcut shortcut = (IWshShortcut)shell.CreateShortcut(shortcutAddress);

            
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(hotkey))
            {
                shortcut.Description = "New shortcut for " + program_name;
                shortcut.Hotkey = hotkey;
            }
            shortcut.TargetPath = program_location;
            shortcut.Save();
        }

        public static void CreateQuickLaunchShortCut(string program_location, string program_name, string hotkey)
        {

            WshShell shell = new WshShell();
            string shortcutAddress = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.ApplicationData) + "\\Microsoft\\Internet Explorer\\Quick Launch\\" + program_name + ".lnk";
            CreateShortCutGeneric(shortcutAddress, program_location, program_name, hotkey);
        }

        public static bool WaitForFile(string filename, int max_wait_time_in_ms)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(filename))
                return false;
            int current_wait = 0;
            int interval = 150;
            while (UtilsLib.FileLib.IsFileReady(filename) == false)
            {
                current_wait += interval;
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(interval);

                if (current_wait > max_wait_time_in_ms)
                    return false;
            }
            return true;
        }

        public static bool WaitForDirectoryToBeCreated(string path, int max_wait_time_in_ms)
        {
            int current_wait = 0;
            int interval = 150;
            while (Directory.Exists(path) == false)
            {
                current_wait += interval;
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(interval);

                if (current_wait > max_wait_time_in_ms)
                    return false;
            }
            return true;
        }
        public static string WaitForAnyNewFile(string directory, int max_wait_time_in_ms, IEnumerable<string> files)
        {
            int current_wait = 0;
            int interval = 150;

            if (null == files)
                files = Directory.GetFiles(directory);


            while (Directory.GetFiles(directory).Length == files.Count())
            {
                current_wait += interval;
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(interval);

                if (current_wait > max_wait_time_in_ms)
                {
                    return null;
                }
            }

            string[] files_new = Directory.GetFiles(directory);
            foreach (string file in files_new)
            {
                if (!files.Contains(file))
                    return file;
            }
            return null;
        }

            return "";
        }

        public static bool IsFileReady(String sFilename, Nullable<int> timeout_in_seconds, Nullable<int> polling_interval)
        {
            if (null == polling_interval)
                polling_interval = 10;
            if (null == timeout_in_seconds)
                timeout_in_seconds = 60;
            DateTime start = DateTime.Now;
            TimeSpan elapsed = (DateTime.Now - start);
            do
            {
                bool is_file_ready = IsFileReady(sFilename);
                if (is_file_ready)
                    return true;
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(polling_interval.Value * 1000);
                elapsed = (DateTime.Now - start);
            } while (elapsed.TotalSeconds < timeout_in_seconds);

            return false;

        }

        public static string MoveFileSmart(string source_file,string destination_file)
        {
            string filename = Path.GetFileName(source_file);
            string new_location = Path.Combine(destination_file, filename);
            new_location = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(new_location);
            source_file = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(source_file);
            if (File.Exists(new_location))
                File.Delete(new_location);
            File.Move(source_file, new_location);
            return new_location;
        }

        public static string MoveDirectorySmart_TESTMEFIRST(string source_full_dir, string destination_dir)
        {
            if (!Directory.Exists(destination_dir))
                Directory.CreateDirectory(destination_dir);
            source_full_dir = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(source_full_dir);
            destination_dir = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(destination_dir);
            foreach (string file in Directory.GetFiles(source_full_dir))
            {
                FileInfo fi = new FileInfo(file);
                string full_new = Path.Combine(destination_dir, fi.Name);
                MoveFileSmart(fi.FullName, full_new);
            }
            return destination_dir;
        }
        public static string CopySmart(string source, string destination)
        {
            
            
            if (source == destination)
                return source;
            destination = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(destination);
            source = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(source);
            if (File.Exists(destination))
                File.Delete(destination);
            File.Copy(source, destination);
            return destination;
        }

        public static string FindSingleFile(string base_dir, IEnumerable<string> matching, IEnumerable<string> ignores)
        {
            List<string> s = FindSingleFiles(base_dir, matching, ignores);
            if (s.Count > 0)
                return s[0];
            return null;
        }
        public static List<string> FindSingleFiles(string base_dir, IEnumerable<string> matching,IEnumerable<string> ignores,SearchOption so = SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)
        {
            List<string> final = new List<string>();

            foreach (string single in matching)
            {
                var directory = new DirectoryInfo(base_dir);
                if (!directory.Exists)
                    continue;
                var files = directory.GetFiles(single,so).OrderByDescending(f => f.LastWriteTime).Select(n => n.FullName).ToList();
                
                
                foreach(var f in files)
                {
                    if (!final.Contains(f))
                        final.Add(f);
                }
                
                if(null != ignores)
                {
                    foreach(string s in ignores)
                    {
                        if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(s))
                            continue;
                        
                        
                        var temp_ignores = files.Where(n => n.IsWildcardMatch(s,false)).ToList().Select(n=> n);
                        foreach(string i in temp_ignores)
                        {
                            final.Remove(i);
                        }
                        
                        
                    }
                }
                    
            }
            return final;
        }

        public static string FindSingleDirectory(string base_dir, IEnumerable<string> matching, bool return_first_if_multiple)
        {
            foreach (string single in matching)
            {
                var directory = new DirectoryInfo(base_dir);
                if (!directory.Exists)
                    continue;
                var files = directory.GetDirectories(single).OrderByDescending(f => f.LastWriteTime);
                int count = files.Count();
                
                if ((return_first_if_multiple && files.Count() > 1) || files.Count() == 1)
                {
                    return files.First().FullName;
                }

            }
            return null;
        }

            public static bool IsFileReady(String sFilename)
        {
            
            
            try
            {
                using (FileStream inputStream = System.IO.File.Open(sFilename, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read, FileShare.None))
                {
                    if (inputStream.Length > 0)
                    {
                        return true;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        return false;
                    }

                }
            }
            catch (System.Exception)
            {
                return false;
            }
        }

        public static string AddFileTag(string full_file_name, char separator, string tag, bool snip_last_tag)
        {
            string directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(full_file_name);
            string filename = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(full_file_name);
            string extension = Path.GetExtension(full_file_name);
            int last_index = filename.LastIndexOf(separator);
            if (last_index == -1 || !snip_last_tag)
                last_index = filename.Length;
            string file_base = filename.Substring(0, last_index);
            string final_file_name = file_base + separator + tag;
            return Path.Combine(directory, final_file_name) + extension;
        }
        public static string ChangeExtension(string full_filename, string new_extension_without_period)
        {
            string simple_filename = Path.Combine(Directory.GetParent(full_filename).ToString(), Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(full_filename) + "." + new_extension_without_period);
            return simple_filename;
        }

        public static string GetQuickUniqueFile(string base_name, string filetype, bool create, bool do_timestamp = true)
        {
            if (filetype.Contains("."))
                filetype = filetype.Replace(".", "");
            string temp = Path.GetTempFileName() + "." + filetype;

            
            string temp_dir = Path.GetTempPath();
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(base_name) && do_timestamp)
            {
                string timestamp_format = "M.d.yy - H.mm";
                
                temp = Path.Combine(temp_dir, base_name + "." + DateTime.Now.ToString(timestamp_format) + "." + filetype);
            }
            else
            {
                temp = Path.Combine(temp_dir, base_name + "." + filetype);
            }
            if (create && !File.Exists(temp))
                File.WriteAllText(temp, null);
            return temp;
        }

        public static string GenerateQuickNameFull(string subject, string base_name, Dictionary<string, object> parms)

        }
        public static string GenerateQuickName(string subject, string base_name, Dictionary<string, object> parms, string path)
        {


            
            
            
            
            
            if (null == subject)
                subject = base_name;
            base_name = UtilsLib.Clean.CleanFilename(subject, true);
            if (null != parms)
                base_name = UtilsLib.Clean.ApplyDictionary<object>(parms, base_name, ",");
            if (UtilsLib.FileLib.ContainsInvalidCharacters(base_name, true))
                base_name = "QuickExport";

            if (null != path)
                base_name = Path.Combine(path, base_name);
            return base_name;

        }

        
        
        

        

        public static void SpawnProcess(string file, bool async,bool expand_variables = true)
        {
            if(expand_variables)
                file = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(file);
            if((!File.Exists(file) && !Directory.Exists(file)) && !file.ToLower().Contains("http"))
            {
                System.Windows.Forms.MessageBox.Show("File Doesn't Exist");
                return;
                
            }
            Process p = new Process();
            p.StartInfo.FileName = file;
            p.Start();
            if(!async)
                p.WaitForExit();
        }

        public static void SpawnLatestFileInFolder(string base_folder)
        {
            
            string latest_file = UtilsLib.FileLib.LastModifiedFileInFolder(base_folder);
            UtilsLib.FileLib.SpawnProcess(latest_file, true, true);
        }
        public static string GetArchiveName(string archive_dir, string filename, string timestamp_format, Nullable<DateTime> asOf, bool ignore_extension)
        {
            string simple_filename = filename;
            string ext = Path.GetExtension(filename);
            if (ignore_extension)
                ext = "";
            if (File.Exists(filename))
            {
                simple_filename = Path.GetFileName(filename);
            }
            if (null != timestamp_format)
            {
                simple_filename = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(filename) + "." + DateTime.Now.ToString(timestamp_format) + ext;
            }
            if (null != asOf)
            {
                if (null != timestamp_format)
                    simple_filename = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(filename) + ".(ASOF " + asOf.Value.ToString("MM.dd.yyyy") + ").(TS " + DateTime.Now.ToString(timestamp_format) + ")" + ext;
                else
                    simple_filename = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(filename) + "-" + asOf.Value.ToString("MM.dd.yyyy") + "-" + ext;
            }

            string archive_filename = Path.Combine(archive_dir, simple_filename);
            int iteration = 1;
            while (File.Exists(archive_filename))
            {
                string simple_filename_new = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(simple_filename) + "_" + iteration + ext;
                archive_filename = Path.Combine(archive_dir, simple_filename_new);
                iteration++;
            }
            return archive_filename;
        }
        public static string ArchiveFile(string archive_dir, string filename, string timestamp_format, bool delete_when_moved, Nullable<DateTime> asOf, bool ignore_ext, bool zip)
        {
            
            
            
            

            string archive_filename = GetArchiveName(archive_dir, filename, timestamp_format, asOf, ignore_ext);
            if (zip)
            {
                archive_filename += ".zip";
                UtilsLib.Compression.Zip(archive_filename, new string[] { filename });
                if (delete_when_moved)
                    File.Delete(filename);
            }
            else
            {
                if (!delete_when_moved)
                    File.Copy(filename, archive_filename);
                else
                    File.Move(filename, archive_filename);
            }
            return archive_filename;
        }


        public static bool DeleteIfExists(string file)
        {
            if (File.Exists(file))
            {
                File.Delete(file);
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        }
        public static bool CreateDirIfNoExist(string directory)
        {
            if (Directory.Exists(directory))
                return false;
            Directory.CreateDirectory(directory);
            return true;
        }


        public static string WriteRandomFileAndSpawn(List<string> text)
        {
            return WriteRandomFileAndSpawn(String.Join(Environment.NewLine, text.ToArray()));
        }

        public static string WriteRandomFileAndSpawn(string text)
        {
            string filename = Path.GetTempFileName() + ".txt";
            File.WriteAllText(filename, text);
            ProcessHelper.StartProcess(filename, null);
            return filename;
        }
        public static string CreateUniqueDir(string base_directory)
        {
            string folder_name = DateTime.Today.Ticks.ToString();
            string new_dir = PathLib.Combine(base_directory, folder_name);
            Directory.CreateDirectory(new_dir);
            return new_dir;
        }

namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class HTMLUtils
    {


        public static string EscapeSequences(string response)
        {
            response = response.Replace("&aacute;", "á");
            response = response.Replace("&Aacute;", "Á");
            response = response.Replace("&acirc;", "â");
            response = response.Replace("&Acirc;", "Â");
            response = response.Replace("&aelig;", "æ");
            response = response.Replace("&AElig;", "Æ");
            response = response.Replace("&agrave;", "à");
            response = response.Replace("&Agrave;", "À");
            response = response.Replace("&amp;", "&");
            response = response.Replace("&aring;", "å");
            response = response.Replace("&Aring;", "Å");
            response = response.Replace("&atilde;", "ã");
            response = response.Replace("&Atilde;", "Ã");
            response = response.Replace("&auml;", "ä");
            response = response.Replace("&Auml;", "Ä");
            response = response.Replace("&ccedil;", "ç");
            response = response.Replace("&Ccedil;", "Ç");
            response = response.Replace("&cent;", "¢");
            response = response.Replace("&copy;", "©");
            response = response.Replace("&divide;", "÷");
            response = response.Replace("&eacute;", "é");
            response = response.Replace("&Eacute;", "É");
            response = response.Replace("&ecirc;", "ê");
            response = response.Replace("&Ecirc;", "Ê");
            response = response.Replace("&egrave;", "è");
            response = response.Replace("&Egrave;", "È");
            response = response.Replace("&euml;", "ë");
            response = response.Replace("&Euml;", "Ë");
            response = response.Replace("&euro;", "€");
            response = response.Replace("&gt;", ">");
            response = response.Replace("&iacute;", "í");
            response = response.Replace("&Iacute;", "Í");
            response = response.Replace("&icirc;", "î");
            response = response.Replace("&Icirc;", "Î");
            response = response.Replace("&iexcl;", "¡");
            response = response.Replace("&igrave;", "ì");
            response = response.Replace("&Igrave;", "Ì");
            response = response.Replace("&iquest;", "¿");
            response = response.Replace("&iuml;", "ï");
            response = response.Replace("&Iuml;", "Ï");
            response = response.Replace("&laquo;", "«");
            response = response.Replace("&ldquo;", "“");
            response = response.Replace("&lsquo;", "‘");
            response = response.Replace("&lt;", "<");
            response = response.Replace("&mdash;", "—");
            response = response.Replace("&micro;", "µ");
            response = response.Replace("&middot;", "·");
            response = response.Replace("&ndash;", "–");
            response = response.Replace("&ntilde;", "ñ");
            response = response.Replace("&Ntilde;", "Ñ");
            response = response.Replace("&oacute;", "ó");
            response = response.Replace("&Oacute;", "Ó");
            response = response.Replace("&ocirc;", "ô");
            response = response.Replace("&Ocirc;", "Ô");
            response = response.Replace("&ograve;", "ò");
            response = response.Replace("&Ograve;", "Ò");
            response = response.Replace("&oslash;", "ø");
            response = response.Replace("&Oslash;", "Ø");
            response = response.Replace("&otilde;", "õ");
            response = response.Replace("&Otilde;", "Õ");
            response = response.Replace("&ouml;", "ö");
            response = response.Replace("&Ouml;", "Ö");
            response = response.Replace("&para;", "¶");
            response = response.Replace("&plusmn;", "±");
            response = response.Replace("&pound;", "£");
            response = response.Replace("&quot;", "\"");
            response = response.Replace("&rdquo;", "”");
            response = response.Replace("&reg;", "®");
            response = response.Replace("&rsquo;", "’");
            response = response.Replace("&sect;", "§");
            response = response.Replace("&szlig;", "ß");
            response = response.Replace("&trade;", "™");
            response = response.Replace("&uacute;", "ú");
            response = response.Replace("&Uacute;", "Ú");
            response = response.Replace("&ucirc;", "û");
            response = response.Replace("&Ucirc;", "Û");
            response = response.Replace("&ugrave;", "ù");
            response = response.Replace("&Ugrave;", "Ù");
            response = response.Replace("&uuml;", "ü");
            response = response.Replace("&Uuml;", "Ü");
            response = response.Replace("&yen;", "¥");
            response = response.Replace("&yuml;", "ÿ");
            return response;
        }

        public static string EscapeSequenceReverse(string response)
        {
            response = response.Replace("&", "&amp;");
            response = response.Replace("<", "&lt;");
            response = response.Replace(">", "&gt;");

            return response;
        }
        public static string InlineCSS(string html)
        {
            string url = @"http:
            string response = null;
            using (var wb = new WebClient())
            {
                var data = new NameValueCollection();
                data["source"] = html;
                data["returnraw"] = "true";

                byte[] response_bytes = wb.UploadValues(url, "POST", data);
                response = System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetString(response_bytes);
                response = EscapeSequences(response);

            }
            return response;
        }

        public class HTMLHelper
        {
            public string html;
            public List<object> var_list;
        }

        public static HTMLHelper ToHtml(DataSet results, string vars, string headers, string tables, bool use_default_formats, string server)
        {
            return ToHtml(results, vars, headers, tables, null);
        }



        public static HTMLHelper ToHtml(DataSet results, string vars, string headers, string tables, List<IFormatHelper> formats)
        {
            int table_no = 0;
            string html_body = "";
            List<object> var_list = new List<object>();

            foreach (DataTable t in results.Tables)
            {

                if (null != vars)
                {
                    string col = vars.Split('|')[table_no];
                    if (t.Columns.Contains(col) && t.Rows.Count > 0)
                    {
                        object o = t.Rows[0][col];
                        var_list.Add(o);
                    }
                }
                if (null != tables)
                {
                    
                    if (tables.Split('|').Length > table_no)
                        html_body += "<H3 style= font-family:Calibri;\">" + tables.Split('|')[table_no] + "</H3>";
                }
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(headers) && headers.Split('|').Length > table_no)
                    html_body += "<H4 style= font-family:Calibri;\">" + headers.Split('|')[table_no] + "</H4>";
                {
                    html_body += ToHtml(t, formats) + "<br><br>";
                }
                table_no++;
            }
            HTMLHelper hh = new HTMLHelper();
            hh.html = html_body;
            hh.var_list = var_list;
            return hh;
        }

        public static String ToCsv(DataTable dt)
        {
            var sb = new StringBuilder();
            
            for (var x = 0; x < dt.Columns.Count; x++)
            {
                if (x != 0) sb.Append(";");
                sb.Append(dt.Columns[x].ColumnName);
            }
            sb.AppendLine();
            
            foreach (DataRow row in dt.Rows)
            {
                for (var x = 0; x < dt.Columns.Count; x++)
                {
                    if (x != 0) sb.Append(";");
                    sb.Append(row[dt.Columns[x]]);
                }
                sb.AppendLine();
            }
            return sb.ToString();
        }
        public static string ToXml(DataTable dt)
        {
            var writer = new StringWriter();
            var name = dt.TableName;
            if (name == string.Empty)
            {
                dt.TableName = "XMLTABLE";
            }
            dt.WriteXml(writer, true);
            dt.TableName = name;
            return writer.ToString();
        }



        public static HTMLHelper QuickToHtml(DataTable dt, string vars, string csv_headers, string tables, List<IFormatHelper> fh)
        {
            DataSet ds = dt.DataSet;
            if (null == ds)
            {
                ds = new DataSet();
                ds.Tables.Add(dt.Copy());
            }
            HTMLUtils.HTMLHelper hh = HTMLUtils.ToHtml(ds, vars, csv_headers, tables, fh);
            return hh;
        }



        public static string ToHtml(DataTable dt, List<IFormatHelper> formats)
        {
            if (dt == null)
            {
                throw new ArgumentNullException("dt");
            }
            var builder = new StringBuilder();
            builder.Append("<html xmlns='http:
            builder.Append("<head>");
            builder.Append("<title>");
            builder.Append("Page-");
            builder.Append(Guid.NewGuid().ToString());
            builder.Append("</title>");
            builder.Append("</head>");
            builder.Append("<body>");
            builder.Append("<style> { border-left: 1px solid; border-color: silver; } </style>");
            builder.Append("<table border='1px' cellpadding='4' cellspacing='0'");
            builder.Append("style='border: solid 1px Silver; font-size: 13px; font-family:Calibri; >");

            builder.Append("<tr align='left' valign='top'>");
            foreach (DataColumn c in dt.Columns)
            {
                string column = UtilsLib.Clean.NiceColumnName(c);
                builder.Append("<td align='center' valign='top'><b>");
                builder.Append(column);
                builder.Append("</td></b>");
            }
            builder.Append("</tr>");
            foreach (DataRow r in dt.Rows)
            {
                builder.Append("<tr align='left' valign='top'>");
                foreach (DataColumn c in dt.Columns)
                {
                    builder.Append("<td align='left' valign='top'>");
                    object val = r[c.ColumnName];
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    if (null != formats)
                    {
                        foreach (IFormatHelper fh in formats)
                        {
                            if (fh.column.ToUpper() == c.ColumnName.ToUpper())
                            {
                                string fmt = "{0:" + fh.format + "}";
                                val = String.Format(fmt, val);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    string clean_html = UtilsLib.Clean.HtmlFormat(c, val);
                    builder.Append(clean_html);
                    builder.Append("</td>");
                }
                builder.Append("</tr>");
            }
            builder.Append("</table>");
            builder.Append("</body>");
            builder.Append("</html>");
            return builder.ToString();
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: Utils\Impersonation.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    [PermissionSet(SecurityAction.Demand, Name = "FullTrust")]
    public class Impersonation : IDisposable
    {
        private readonly SafeTokenHandle _handle;
        private readonly WindowsImpersonationContext _context;

        const int LOGON32_LOGON_NEW_CREDENTIALS = 9;

        public Impersonation(string domain, string username, string password)
        {
            var ok = LogonUser(username, domain, password,
                           LOGON32_LOGON_NEW_CREDENTIALS, 0, out this._handle);
            if (!ok)
            {
                var errorCode = Marshal.GetLastWin32Error();
                throw new ApplicationException(string.Format("Could not impersonate the elevated user.  LogonUser returned error code {0}.", errorCode));
            }

            this._context = WindowsIdentity.Impersonate(this._handle.DangerousGetHandle());
        }

        public void Dispose()
        {
            this._context.Dispose();
            this._handle.Dispose();
        }

        [DllImport("advapi32.dll", SetLastError = true, CharSet = CharSet.Unicode)]
        private static extern bool LogonUser(String lpszUsername, String lpszDomain, String lpszPassword, int dwLogonType, int dwLogonProvider, out SafeTokenHandle phToken);

        public sealed class SafeTokenHandle : SafeHandleZeroOrMinusOneIsInvalid
        {
            private SafeTokenHandle()
                : base(true) { }

            [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
            [ReliabilityContract(Consistency.WillNotCorruptState, Cer.Success)]
            [SuppressUnmanagedCodeSecurity]
            [return: MarshalAs(UnmanagedType.Bool)]
            private static extern bool CloseHandle(IntPtr handle);

            protected override bool ReleaseHandle()
            {
                return CloseHandle(handle);
            }
        }
    }
}

        [DllImport("user32.dll", SetLastError = true)]
        private static extern uint SendInput(uint numberOfInputs, INPUT[] inputs, int sizeOfInputStructure);
        public static void SendKeyPress(KeyCode keyCode)
        {
            INPUT input = new INPUT
            {
                Type = 1
            };
            input.Data.Keyboard = new KEYBDINPUT()
            {
                Vk = (ushort)keyCode,
                Scan = 0,
                Flags = 0,
                Time = 0,
                ExtraInfo = IntPtr.Zero,
            };

            INPUT input2 = new INPUT
            {
                Type = 1
            };
            input2.Data.Keyboard = new KEYBDINPUT()
            {
                Vk = (ushort)keyCode,
                Scan = 0,
                Flags = 2,
                Time = 0,
                ExtraInfo = IntPtr.Zero
            };
            INPUT[] inputs = new INPUT[] { input, input2 };
            if (SendInput(2, inputs, Marshal.SizeOf(typeof(INPUT))) == 0)
                throw new Exception();
        }
        public static void SendKeyDown(KeyCode keyCode)
        {
            INPUT input = new INPUT
            {
                Type = 1
            };
            input.Data.Keyboard = new KEYBDINPUT();
            input.Data.Keyboard.Vk = (ushort)keyCode;
            input.Data.Keyboard.Scan = 0;
            input.Data.Keyboard.Flags = 0;
            input.Data.Keyboard.Time = 0;
            input.Data.Keyboard.ExtraInfo = IntPtr.Zero;
            INPUT[] inputs = new INPUT[] { input };
            if (SendInput(1, inputs, Marshal.SizeOf(typeof(INPUT))) == 0)
            {
                throw new Exception();
            }
        }
        public static void SendKeyUp(KeyCode keyCode)
        {
            INPUT input = new INPUT
            {
                Type = 1
            };
            input.Data.Keyboard = new KEYBDINPUT();
            input.Data.Keyboard.Vk = (ushort)keyCode;
            input.Data.Keyboard.Scan = 0;
            input.Data.Keyboard.Flags = 2;
            input.Data.Keyboard.Time = 0;
            input.Data.Keyboard.ExtraInfo = IntPtr.Zero;
            INPUT[] inputs = new INPUT[] { input };
            if (SendInput(1, inputs, Marshal.SizeOf(typeof(INPUT))) == 0)
                throw new Exception();

        }
    }

--- FILE: Utils\Mail.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    using Word = Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word;


    public class Mail
    {

        
        
        
        
        
        

        private static string _my_email = null;
        public static string MyEmail
        {
            get
            {
                if (null == _my_email)
                {
                    Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Application app = new Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Application();
                    AddressEntry addrEntry = app.Session.CurrentUser.AddressEntry;
                    if (addrEntry.Type == "EX")
                    {
                        ExchangeUser currentUser = app.Session.CurrentUser.AddressEntry.GetExchangeUser();
                        _my_email = currentUser.PrimarySmtpAddress;
                        
                        
                        
                    }

                }
                return _my_email;
            }
        }
        public string _smtp_server;
        public string _smtp_user;
        public string _smtp_pass;
        public int _smtp_port;
        public string _from;

        MailServerConfig mp;
        public Mail(string mail_profile)
        {
            var mp = UtilsLib.Mail.MailProfiles.GetProfiles()[mail_profile];
            SetFromMailProfile(mp);
        }
        public Mail(MailServerConfig mp)
        {
            SetFromMailProfile(mp);
        }

        public void SetFromMailProfile(MailServerConfig mp)
        {
            _smtp_server = mp.server;
            _smtp_user = mp.user;
            _smtp_pass = mp.pass;
            _smtp_port = mp.port;
            this.mp = mp;
        }
        public Mail(string from, string smtp_server, string smpt_user, string smpt_pass, int? port)
        {
           
            this._from = from;
            this._smtp_server = smtp_server;
            this._smtp_user = smpt_user;
            this._smtp_pass = smpt_pass;
            this._smtp_port = null == port ? 25 : port.Value;
        }


        public static void CreateOutlookMail(string subject, string body, IEnumerable<string> attachments, IEnumerable<string> to, IEnumerable<string> cc, IEnumerable<string> bcc, bool body_html)
        {
            CreateOutlookMail(subject, body, attachments, to, cc, bcc, body_html, null, false, false, false,null,null);
        }
        public static void CreateOutlookMail(string subject, string body, IEnumerable<string> attachments, IEnumerable<string> to, IEnumerable<string> cc, IEnumerable<string> bcc, bool body_html, bool append_signature,string from_override,string signature_override)
        {
            CreateOutlookMail(subject, body, attachments, to, cc, bcc, body_html, null, false, false, append_signature,from_override,null,MailPriority.Normal, signature_override);
        }


        public static string GetCurrentUserEmail(Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Application app)
        {
            var currentUser = app.Session.CurrentUser.AddressEntry.GetExchangeUser();
            string from = null;
            if (currentUser != null)
            {
                from = currentUser.PrimarySmtpAddress;
            }
            return from;
        }

        
        public static void CreateOutlookMail(string subject, string body, IEnumerable<string> attachments, IEnumerable<string> to, IEnumerable<string> cc, IEnumerable<string> bcc, bool body_html, Nullable<DateTime> send_time, bool paste_body_from_clipboard, bool send, bool append_signature,string override_from,string reply_to, MailPriority mail_priority = MailPriority.Normal,string signature_override=null)
        {
            Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Application app = new Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Application();
            Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.MailItem mi = (Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.MailItem)app.CreateItem(Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.OlItemType.olMailItem);
            mi.Subject = subject;
            string from = GetCurrentUserEmail(app);
            
            
  
            if (paste_body_from_clipboard)
            {
                mi.Display();
                

                var ic = app.ActiveInspector().WordEditor;
                Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.WdProtectionType typ;
                int p = ic.ProtectionType;
                if (p != (int)Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.WdProtectionType.wdNoProtection)
                {
                    ic.UnProtect();
                }

                
                

                Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.MailItem currentMessage = app.ActiveInspector().CurrentItem;
                
                Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.Document doc = currentMessage.GetInspector.WordEditor;
                Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.Selection sel = doc.Windows[1].Selection;
                sel.PasteAndFormat(Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.WdRecoveryType.wdUseDestinationStylesRecovery);
                ClearClipboardSafe();
                
                


                
            }
            else
            {

                if (body_html)
                {
                    mi.HTMLBody = body;
                    if (append_signature)
                    {
                        string signature = ReadSignature(signature_override);
                        if (mi.HTMLBody.Contains("@signature@"))
                            mi.HTMLBody = mi.HTMLBody.Replace("@signature@", signature);
                        else
                            mi.HTMLBody += "<br><br>" + signature;
                    }
                }

                if (null != body && body_html == false)
                    mi.Body = body;
            }
            if (null != send_time)
                mi.DeferredDeliveryTime = send_time.Value;

            
            AddRecips(mi, to, OlMailRecipientType.olTo, from);
            AddRecips(mi, cc, OlMailRecipientType.olCC, from);
            AddRecips(mi, bcc, OlMailRecipientType.olBCC,null);

            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(override_from))
            {
                mi.SentOnBehalfOfName = override_from;
            }
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(reply_to))
            {
                mi.ReplyRecipients.Add(reply_to);
            }
            if (null != attachments)
            {
                foreach (string attachment in attachments)
                {
                    if (null != attachment)
                        mi.Attachments.Add(attachment);
                }
            }
            if (mi.Importance != OlImportance.olImportanceNormal)
                mi.Importance = (mail_priority == MailPriority.High ? OlImportance.olImportanceHigh : OlImportance.olImportanceLow);

            mi.Display();
            if (send)
                mi.Send();
        }


        private static string ReadSignature(string signature_name)
        {
            string appDataDir = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.ApplicationData) + "\\Microsoft\\Signatures";
            string signature = string.Empty;
            string sig_name = null == signature_name ? "Standard" : signature_name;

            DirectoryInfo diInfo = new DirectoryInfo(appDataDir);

            if (diInfo.Exists)
            {
                FileInfo[] fiSignature = diInfo.GetFiles("*.htm");
                foreach (FileInfo fi in fiSignature)
                {
                    if (fiSignature.Length > 0)
                    {
                        StreamReader sr = new StreamReader(fi.FullName, Encoding.Default);
                        signature = sr.ReadToEnd();
                        
                        sr.Close();
                        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(signature))
                        {
                            string fileName = fiSignature[0].Name.Replace(fiSignature[0].Extension, string.Empty);
                            signature = signature.Replace(fileName + "_files/", appDataDir + "/" + fileName + "_files/");
                            if (fileName == signature_name)
                                return signature;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return signature;
        }

        public static void ClearClipboardSafe()
        {
            
            var th = new Thread(ClearClipboard);
            th.SetApartmentState(ApartmentState.STA);
            th.IsBackground = true;
            th.Start();
        }

        public static void ClearClipboard()
        {
            System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.Clear();
        }


        public static void AddRecips(MailItem mi, IEnumerable<string> addresses, OlMailRecipientType mrt,string ignore_if)
        {
            if (null != addresses)
            {
                foreach (string s in addresses)
                {
                    if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(s) || (null != ignore_if && s.ToUpper() == ignore_if.ToUpper()))
                        continue;
                    foreach (string next in s.Split(';'))
                    {
                        if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(next))
                            continue;
                        Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Recipient oRecip = (Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Recipient)mi.Recipients.Add(next);
                        
                        
                        oRecip.Type = (int)mrt;
                        bool v = oRecip.Resolve();
                    }
                }
            }
        }


        public static void RemindMeIn(string subject, string body, DateTime date)
        {

            
            CreateAppointment(subject, body, null, date, date, new string[] { UtilsLib.Mail.MyEmail }, 0);
        }
        public static void CreateAppointment(string subject, string body, string location, DateTime start, DateTime end, IEnumerable<string> recipients, Nullable<int> reminder_interval)
        {
            Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Application app = null;
            Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.AppointmentItem appt = null;

            app = new Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Application();

            Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.TimeZones tzs = app.TimeZones;
            
            
            Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.TimeZone est = tzs["Eastern Standard Time"];

            appt = (Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.AppointmentItem)app.CreateItem(Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.OlItemType.olAppointmentItem);
            appt.Subject = subject;
            appt.Body = body;
            appt.Location = location;
            appt.Start = start;

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            

            

            if (null != recipients)
            {
                foreach (string s in recipients)
                {
                    if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(s))
                        appt.Recipients.Add(s);
                }
            }
            appt.End = end;
            if (null != reminder_interval)
            {
                appt.ReminderSet = true;
                appt.ReminderMinutesBeforeStart = reminder_interval.Value;
            }
            appt.BusyStatus = Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.OlBusyStatus.olFree;
            appt.MeetingStatus = OlMeetingStatus.olMeeting;

            appt.StartTimeZone = est;
            appt.EndTimeZone = est;

            appt.Display();
            
        }
        
        
        

        
        
        


        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        

        

        
        

        
        
        


        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        

        

        
        

        
        

        
        

        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        


        

        
        


        

        
        
        
        
        

        
        

        

        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        


        


        
        

        
        

        
        

        


        
        
        
        


        public void SendMail(string to, string cc, string bcc, string subject, string body, IEnumerable<string> attachments)
        {
            SendMail(to, cc, bcc, subject, body, attachments, true, true, null);
        }




        public void SendSMTPMail(string to, string cc, string bcc, string subject, string body, IEnumerable<string> attachments, bool html, bool send, string from, MailPriority mp = MailPriority.Normal)
        {

            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(from))
                from = Environment.UserName + "@" + CommonInterfaces.Constants.DEFAULT_EMAIL_DOMAIN;
            MailAddress _from = new MailAddress(from);
            MailMessage mail = new MailMessage();
            mail.From = _from;

            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(to))
            {
                foreach (string s in to.Split(';'))
                {
                    if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(s))
                        continue;
                    MailAddress _to = new MailAddress(s);
                    mail.To.Add(_to);
                }
            }

            
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(cc))
            {
                foreach (string s in cc.Split(';'))
                {
                    MailAddress _cc = new MailAddress(s);
                    mail.CC.Add(_cc);
                }
            }
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(bcc))
            {
                foreach (string s in bcc.Split(';'))
                {
                    MailAddress _bcc = new MailAddress(s);
                    mail.Bcc.Add(_bcc);
                }
            }

            mail.Priority = mp;
            
            


            
            
            
            


            
            
            
            

            
            
            
            

            SmtpClient client = new SmtpClient(_smtp_server, _smtp_port);
            
            
            
            

            
            





            

            if (587 == _smtp_port || 465 == _smtp_port) 
            {
                client.EnableSsl = true;
            }

            if (null != _smtp_user)
            {
                System.Net.NetworkCredential credentials = new System.Net.NetworkCredential(_smtp_user, _smtp_pass);
                client.UseDefaultCredentials = false;
                client.Credentials = credentials;
                
            }
            
            mail.Subject = subject;
            mail.Body = body;
            mail.IsBodyHtml = html;
            if (null != attachments)
            {
                foreach (string s in attachments)
                {
                    mail.Attachments.Add(new System.Net.Mail.Attachment(s));
                }
            }
            
            client.Send(mail);
        }

        public enum MAIL_PRIORITY { HIGH, LOW, NORMAL }

        private OlImportance PickPriority(MAIL_PRIORITY mp)
        {

            if (mp == MAIL_PRIORITY.LOW)
                return OlImportance.olImportanceLow;
            if (mp == MAIL_PRIORITY.HIGH)
                return OlImportance.olImportanceHigh;
            
            return OlImportance.olImportanceNormal; ;
        }
        public void SendMail(string to, string cc, string bcc, string subject, string body, IEnumerable<string> attachments, bool html, bool send, string from, MAIL_PRIORITY mp = MAIL_PRIORITY.NORMAL)
        {


            Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Application oApp = new Microsoft.Office.Interop.Outlook.Application();

            
            MailItem oMsg = (MailItem)oApp.CreateItem(OlItemType.olMailItem);



            
            
            oMsg.To = to;
            oMsg.CC = cc;
            oMsg.BCC = bcc;
            oMsg.Importance = PickPriority(mp);

            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(from))
                oMsg.SentOnBehalfOfName = from;



            if (!html)
            {
                oMsg.BodyFormat = OlBodyFormat.olFormatPlain;
                oMsg.Body = body;
            }
            else
            {
                oMsg.BodyFormat = OlBodyFormat.olFormatHTML;
                oMsg.HTMLBody = body;

            }
            

            
            oMsg.Subject = subject;


            if (null != attachments)
            {
                foreach (string s in attachments)
                {
                    
                    int iAttachType = (int)OlAttachmentType.olByValue;
                    oMsg.Attachments.Add(s, iAttachType);
                }
            }

            
            

            
            oMsg.Display();
            oMsg.Save();
            if (send)
            {
                oMsg.Send();
                oApp = null;
            }
            

            
            


            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            



            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            
            
            


            
            
            
            
            
            


            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

                }
                return _profiles;
            }


        }

--- FILE: Utils\Math.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class MathLib
    {
        public static double AddNullable(params Nullable<double>[] dbls)
        {
            double total = 0;
            foreach (Nullable<double> d in dbls)
            {
                if (null != d)
                    total += d.Value;
            }
            return total;
        }

        public static double AvgNullable(params Nullable<double>[] dbls)
        {
            double total = 0;
            int non_null = 0;
            foreach (Nullable<double> d in dbls)
            {
                if (null != d)
                {
                    total += d.Value;
                    non_null++;
                }

            }

            return total / non_null;
        }

        public static Nullable<double> Interpolate(double val, DataTable tbl, string val_col, string weight_col)
        {
            tbl.DefaultView.Sort = String.Format("{0} asc", val_col);
            DataTable sorted = tbl.DefaultView.ToTable();
            Nullable<double> last_slope = null;
            Nullable<double> last_val = null;
            for (int i = 0; i != tbl.Rows.Count; i++)
            {
                double row_val = System.Convert.ToDouble(tbl.Rows[i][val_col]);
                double row_weight = System.Convert.ToDouble(tbl.Rows[i][weight_col]);



                if (i == tbl.Rows.Count - 1 && val > row_val)
                {
                    return last_val;
                }
                double row_val_p1 = System.Convert.ToDouble(tbl.Rows[i + 1][val_col]);
                double row_weight_p1 = System.Convert.ToDouble(tbl.Rows[i + 1][weight_col]);

                last_slope = (row_weight_p1 - row_weight) / (row_val_p1 - row_val);
                last_val = row_weight + (val - row_val) * last_slope.Value;



                if (i == 0 && val < row_val)
                {
                    return last_val;
                }

                if (row_val <= val && val <= row_val_p1)
                {
                    
                    
                    
                    return last_val;
                    
                    
                }


            }

            return null;
        }



        public static int[] RankSimple(double[] numbers)
        {
            List<int> ranks = new List<int>();
            foreach (double d in numbers)
            {
                int rank = HowManyLower(d, numbers) + 1;
                ranks.Add(rank);
            }
            return ranks.ToArray();
        }
        public static int HowManyLower(double num, double[] numbers)
        {
            int count = 0;
            foreach (double d in numbers)
            {
                if (num < d)
                    count++;
            }
            return count;
        }



        public static Nullable<double> WeightedAverage(DataColumn values, DataColumn weights, bool ignoreZeroValues)
        {
            if (null == values || null == weights)
                return null;

            if (values.Table.Rows.Count != weights.Table.Rows.Count)
                return null;

            Nullable<double> value = 0;
            Nullable<double> weight = 0;
            for (int i = 0; i != values.Table.Rows.Count; i++)
            {
                if (null != values.Table.Rows[i] && null != weights.Table.Rows[i])
                {
                    double val = System.Convert.ToDouble(values.Table.Rows[i][values]);
                    double w = System.Convert.ToDouble(weights.Table.Rows[i][weights]);
                    if (ignoreZeroValues && val == 0.0)
                        continue;

                    value += val * w;
                    weight += w;
                }
            }
            if (null == value || null == weight)
                return null;
            double result = value.Value / weight.Value;

            if (Double.IsNaN(result))
                return 0.0;

            return result;

        }

        public static Nullable<double> WeightedAverage(object[] values, object[] weights, bool ignoreZeroValues)
        {
            if (null == values || null == weights)
                return null;

            if (values.Length != weights.Length)
                return null;

            Nullable<double> value = 0;
            Nullable<double> weight = 0;
            for (int i = 0; i != values.Length; i++)
            {
                if (null != values[i] && null != weights[i])
                {
                    double val;
                    if (null == values[i] || !Double.TryParse(values[i].ToString(), out val))
                        return null;
                    
                    double w = System.Convert.ToDouble(weights[i]);
                    if (ignoreZeroValues && val == 0.0)
                        continue;

                    value += val * w;
                    weight += w;
                }
            }
            if (null == value || null == weight)
                return null;
            double result = value.Value / weight.Value;

            if (Double.IsNaN(result))
                return 0.0;

            return result;
            
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: Utils\Misc.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public static class Misc
    {
        const char DELIM_FOR_TABLE_SETTINGS_VARS = '|';
        public static T getArrayValueIfIndxIsValidForTheArrayAndIfTheArrayExists<T>(T[] optArray, int indx)
        {
            T theVal;
            if (optArray == null)
            {
                theVal = default(T);
            }
            else if (indx >= optArray.Length)
            {
                
                theVal = default(T);
            }
            else
            {
                theVal = optArray[indx];
            }

            return theVal;
        }

        public static IEnumerable<DataTable> DataTableCollectionToEnumeration(DataTableCollection dataTableCollection)
        { 
            

            var dataTables = new List<DataTable>();
            foreach (DataTable dataTable in dataTableCollection)
            {
                dataTables.Add(dataTable);
            }
            return dataTables;
        }


        public static void loopThroughAndKeepCount<T>(IEnumerable<T> itemsToLoopThrough, int firstIndx, Action<int, T> funcHandleNextItem)
        { 
            int cnt = firstIndx;
            foreach (T item in itemsToLoopThrough)
            {
                funcHandleNextItem(cnt, item);
                cnt = cnt + 1;
            }
        }

        private static List<object> getValuesFromOneParticularColumnInEachTableAndThenStackThoseColumnsTogetherIntoASingleVector(string optDelimitedStringOfColumnNames, IEnumerable<DataTable> dataTables)
        {
            List<object> listForEachTableOf__valueInTheFirstRowOfTheTableForTheParticularColumnSpecified = new List<object>();
            string[] columnNameToUseForEachParticularTable__orNull = optDelimitedStringOfColumnNames == null ? null : optDelimitedStringOfColumnNames.Split(DELIM_FOR_TABLE_SETTINGS_VARS);

            Misc.loopThroughAndKeepCount(dataTables, 0, (table_no, dataTable) => {
                string colNameToUseForThisTable__orNulLIfWeShouldNotRetrieveValuesForThisTable = Misc.getArrayValueIfIndxIsValidForTheArrayAndIfTheArrayExists<string>(columnNameToUseForEachParticularTable__orNull, table_no);

                if (colNameToUseForThisTable__orNulLIfWeShouldNotRetrieveValuesForThisTable != null)
                {
                    string colName = colNameToUseForThisTable__orNulLIfWeShouldNotRetrieveValuesForThisTable;
                    if (dataTable.Columns.Contains(colName) && dataTable.Rows.Count > 0)
                    {
                        object valueInTheFirstRowOfTheTableForTheParticularColumnSpecified = dataTable.Rows[0][colName];
                        listForEachTableOf__valueInTheFirstRowOfTheTableForTheParticularColumnSpecified.Add(valueInTheFirstRowOfTheTableForTheParticularColumnSpecified);
                    }
                }
            });
            return listForEachTableOf__valueInTheFirstRowOfTheTableForTheParticularColumnSpecified;

        }

    }
}

namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class Network
    {
        public static string GetLocalIPAddress()
        {
            var host = Dns.GetHostEntry(Dns.GetHostName());
            foreach (var ip in host.AddressList)
            {
                if (ip.AddressFamily == AddressFamily.InterNetwork)
                {
                    return ip.ToString();
                }
            }
            throw new Exception("No network adapters with an IPv4 address in the system!");
        }
        public static string GetExternalIPAddress()
        {
            string externalIpString = new WebClient().DownloadString("http:
            var externalIp = IPAddress.Parse(externalIpString);
            return externalIpString;
        }
    }

--- FILE: Utils\PathLib.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    using File = System.IO.File;
    public class PathLib
    {
        public static string Combine(string path1,string path2)
        {
            string path_1_new = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(path1);
            string path_2_new = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(path2);
            return Path.Combine(path_1_new, path_2_new);
        }

        const int MAX_PATH = 260;

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", CharSet = CharSet.Auto)]
        public static extern int GetShortPathName([MarshalAs(UnmanagedType.LPTStr)] string path, [MarshalAs(UnmanagedType.LPTStr)] StringBuilder shortPath, int shortPathLength);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", CharSet = CharSet.Auto)]
        public static extern int GetLongPathName([MarshalAs(UnmanagedType.LPTStr)] string path, [MarshalAs(UnmanagedType.LPTStr)] StringBuilder longPath, int longPathLength);

        public static string LongToShortPath(string path)
        {
            var shortPath = new StringBuilder(MAX_PATH);
            GetShortPathName(path, shortPath, MAX_PATH);
            return shortPath.ToString();
        }

        public static string CreateNewTempDir()
        {
            string random = Path.GetRandomFileName();
            string temp = Path.GetTempPath();
            string final = Path.Combine(temp, random);
            
            Directory.CreateDirectory(final);
            return final;
        }
    }
}

using static UtilsLib.Keys;
namespace UtilsLib
