        public static string IRON_OCR_KEY = "IRONOCR.UNLOCK.25482-DF43F8EDD4-J7YEYXQIJRMQ2SXQ-3CJ7NZIBM2DV-XOT46LQP6R3D-JZEU2PZMGN64-EVPRDB53XYD3-FDD5ZW-TYPKG3DQVMCJUA-DEPLOYMENT.TRIAL-YHWOUZ.TRIAL.EXPIRES.25.MAY.2023";
        public static string IRON_PDF_KEY = "IRONPDF.UNLOCK.2706-9D0263A240-A3SGPJKPBG6NPNK-L7S7Q5B73MSZ-L2NXW4CJ4R6I-BMJFGPC7IJDT-4DNSEWMYDEAL-LZDL7E-T5MMFTVI7MKJUA-DEPLOYMENT.TRIAL-7QSZMO.TRIAL.EXPIRES.25.MAY.2023";
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public static string PDFSplitMerge(string full_pdf_source, IEnumerable<int> zero_based_pages_to_split_merge, string full_pdf_destination)
        {
            var targetDoc = new PdfDocument();
            using (var pdfDoc = PdfReader.Open(full_pdf_source, PdfDocumentOpenMode.Import))
            {
                foreach (int i in zero_based_pages_to_split_merge)
                    targetDoc.AddPage(pdfDoc.Pages[i]);
            }
            targetDoc.Save(full_pdf_destination);
            return full_pdf_destination;
        }

        public static void PDFSplitMergeIron(string full_pdf_source, IEnumerable<int> zero_based_pages_to_split_merge, string full_pdf_destination)
        {
            var doc = IronPdf.PdfDocument.FromFile(full_pdf_source);
            var new_doc = doc.CopyPages(zero_based_pages_to_split_merge);
            
           
            new_doc.SaveAs(full_pdf_destination);
        }


        public static int? PDFTotalPages(string filePath)
        {
            var pdf = IronPdf.PdfDocument.FromFile(filePath);
            
            return pdf.PageCount;
        }
        public static int? PDFContainsText(string filePath, string searchText)
        {

            try
            {
                
                
                
                
                IronPdf.License.LicenseKey = IRON_PDF_KEY;
                var pdf = IronPdf.PdfDocument.FromFile(filePath);
                 
                


                int i = 0;

                foreach (var p in pdf.Pages)
                {
                    string text = pdf.ExtractTextFromPage(i);
                    if (text.Contains(searchText))
                    {
                        
                        return i;
                    }
                    i++;
                }
            }
            catch(Exception n)
            {

            }
            return null;
        }


        public static bool PDFContainsOCRText(string filePath, string searchText)
        {

            
            IronTesseract ocr = new IronTesseract();
            using (OcrInput input = new OcrInput())
            {

                IronOcr.License.LicenseKey = IRON_OCR_KEY;
                
                
                

                
                input.AddPdf(filePath);
                OcrResult result = ocr.Read(input);
                string text = result.Text;

                if (text.Contains(searchText))
                {
                        
                        return true;
                }

            }

            return false;
        }


        public static bool HasSignature(string full_pdf_source)
        {
            var pdf = IronPdf.PdfDocument.FromFile(full_pdf_source);
            IronPdf.License.LicenseKey = IRON_PDF_KEY;

            
            bool contains_sig = pdf.GetVerifiedSignatures().Count > 0;
 

            return contains_sig;
        }

        public static string MergePDFs(string target_path, IEnumerable<string> pdfs)
        {
            string errorFile = Path.Combine(Path.GetDirectoryName(target_path), $"MergeErrorLog_{DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss")}.txt");
            var pdfList = pdfs.ToList();

            using (var targetDoc = new PdfDocument())
            {
                    foreach (var pdf in pdfList)
                    {
                        try
                        {
                            using (var pdfDoc = PdfReader.Open(pdf, PdfDocumentOpenMode.Import))
                            {
                                for (var i = 0; i < pdfDoc.PageCount; i++)
                                    targetDoc.AddPage(pdfDoc.Pages[i]);
                            }
                        }
                        catch (Exception e)
                        {
                            using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(errorFile, true))
                            {
                                writer.WriteLine($"{DateTime.Now} - Merge Error - The file named: {pdf} was not merged due to the following error:");
                                writer.WriteLine(e.Message.ToString());
                            }
                            continue;
                        }
                    }
                    try
                    {
                        targetDoc.Save(target_path);
                    }
                    catch (Exception)
                    {
                        using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(errorFile, true))
                            writer.WriteLine($"{DateTime.Now} - Save failed due to malformed PDF page data. Retrying with per-file validation...");
                        SaveWithValidation(target_path, pdfList, errorFile);
                    }
            }

            return target_path;
        }

        public static string MergePDFs(string target_path, IEnumerable<string> pdfs, string asset_id)
        {
            string errorFile = Path.Combine(Path.GetDirectoryName(target_path), asset_id, $"{asset_id}_ErrorLog.txt");
            string logFile = Path.Combine(Path.GetDirectoryName(target_path), asset_id, $"{asset_id}_MergeLog_{DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss")}.txt");
            var pdfList = pdfs.ToList();

            using (var targetDoc = new PdfDocument())
            {
                foreach (var pdf in pdfList)
                {
                    try
                    {
                        using (var pdfDoc = PdfReader.Open(pdf, PdfDocumentOpenMode.Import))
                        {
                            using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(logFile, true))
                                writer.WriteLine($"{asset_id} - The file named: {pdf} begins on page {targetDoc.PageCount}");
                            for (var i = 0; i < pdfDoc.PageCount; i++)
                                targetDoc.AddPage(pdfDoc.Pages[i]);
                            using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(logFile, true))
                                    writer.WriteLine($"{asset_id} - The file named: {pdf} ends on page {targetDoc.PageCount}");
                            }
                    }
                    catch (Exception e)
                    {
                        using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(errorFile, true))
                        {
                            writer.WriteLine($"{DateTime.Now} - {asset_id} - Merge Error - The file named: {pdf} was not merged due to the following error:");
                            writer.WriteLine(e.Message.ToString());
                        }
                        continue;
                    }
                }
                try
                {
                    targetDoc.Save(target_path);
                }
                catch (Exception)
                {
                    using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(errorFile, true))
                        writer.WriteLine($"{DateTime.Now} - {asset_id} - Save failed due to malformed PDF page data. Retrying with per-file validation...");
                    SaveWithValidation(target_path, pdfList, errorFile, logFile, asset_id);
                }
            }

            return target_path;
        }

        private static void SaveWithValidation(string target_path, List<string> pdfs, string errorFile, string logFile = null, string asset_id = null)
        {
            using (var targetDoc = new PdfDocument())
            {
                foreach (var pdf in pdfs)
                {
                    try
                    {
                        
                        using (var testDoc = new PdfDocument())
                        using (var pdfDoc = PdfReader.Open(pdf, PdfDocumentOpenMode.Import))
                        {
                            for (var i = 0; i < pdfDoc.PageCount; i++)
                                testDoc.AddPage(pdfDoc.Pages[i]);
                            using (var ms = new MemoryStream())
                                testDoc.Save(ms, false);
                        }

                        
                        using (var pdfDoc = PdfReader.Open(pdf, PdfDocumentOpenMode.Import))
                        {
                            for (var i = 0; i < pdfDoc.PageCount; i++)
                                targetDoc.AddPage(pdfDoc.Pages[i]);
                        }
                        if (logFile != null)
                            using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(logFile, true))
                                writer.WriteLine($"{asset_id} - (validated) {pdf} merged successfully");
                    }
                    catch (Exception e)
                    {
                        using (StreamWriter writer = new StreamWriter(errorFile, true))
                        {
                            writer.WriteLine($"{DateTime.Now} - {asset_id} - Skipping malformed PDF: {pdf}");
                            writer.WriteLine(e.Message);
                        }
                    }
                }
                if (targetDoc.PageCount > 0)
                    targetDoc.Save(target_path);
            }
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Utils\PDFOld.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class PDFParser
    {

        #region Fields

        #region _numberOfCharsToKeep
        private static int _numberOfCharsToKeep = 15;
        #endregion

        #endregion

        #region ExtractText


        public string ExtractText(string inFilename)
        {
            string output = "";
            try
            {
                
                PdfReader reader = new PdfReader(inFilename);

                Console.Write("Processing: ");

                int totalLen = 68;
                float charUnit = ((float)totalLen) / (float)reader.NumberOfPages;
                int totalWritten = 0;
                float curUnit = 0;

                for (int page = 1; page <= reader.NumberOfPages; page++)
                {

                    output += ExtractTextFromPDFBytes(reader.GetPageContent(page)) + " ";

                    
                    if (charUnit >= 1.0f)
                    {
                        for (int i = 0; i < (int)charUnit; i++)
                        {
                            Console.Write("#");
                            totalWritten++;
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        curUnit += charUnit;
                        if (curUnit >= 1.0f)
                        {
                            for (int i = 0; i < (int)curUnit; i++)
                            {
                                Console.Write("#");
                                totalWritten++;
                            }
                            curUnit = 0;
                        }

                    }
                }

                if (totalWritten < totalLen)
                {
                    for (int i = 0; i < (totalLen - totalWritten); i++)
                    {
                        Console.Write("#");
                    }
                }
            }
            catch
            {

            }
            finally
            {

            }
            return output;
        }
        public void ExtractText(string inFileName, string outFile)
        {
            string file = ExtractText(inFileName);
            File.WriteAllText(outFile, file);
        }
        #endregion

        #region ExtractTextFromPDFBytes
        private string ExtractTextFromPDFBytes(byte[] input)
        {
            if (input == null || input.Length == 0) return "";

            try
            {
                string resultString = "";

                
                bool inTextObject = false;

                
                
                bool nextLiteral = false;

                
                int bracketDepth = 0;

                
                char[] previousCharacters = new char[_numberOfCharsToKeep];
                for (int j = 0; j < _numberOfCharsToKeep; j++) previousCharacters[j] = ' ';


                for (int i = 0; i < input.Length; i++)
                {
                    char c = (char)input[i];

                    if (inTextObject)
                    {
                        
                        if (bracketDepth == 0)
                        {
                            if (CheckToken(new string[] { "TD", "Td" }, previousCharacters))
                            {
                                resultString += "\n\r";
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                if (CheckToken(new string[] { "'", "T*", "\"" }, previousCharacters))
                                {
                                    resultString += "\n";
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    if (CheckToken(new string[] { "Tj" }, previousCharacters))
                                    {
                                        resultString += " ";
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        
                        if (bracketDepth == 0 &&
                            CheckToken(new string[] { "ET" }, previousCharacters))
                        {

                            inTextObject = false;
                            resultString += " ";
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            
                            if ((c == '(') && (bracketDepth == 0) && (!nextLiteral))
                            {
                                bracketDepth = 1;
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                
                                if ((c == ')') && (bracketDepth == 1) && (!nextLiteral))
                                {
                                    bracketDepth = 0;
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    
                                    if (bracketDepth == 1)
                                    {
                                        
                                        
                                        if (c == '\\' && !nextLiteral)
                                        {
                                            nextLiteral = true;
                                        }
                                        else
                                        {
                                            if (((c >= ' ') && (c <= '~')) ||
                                                ((c >= 128) && (c < 255)))
                                            {
                                                resultString += c.ToString();
                                            }

                                            nextLiteral = false;
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    
                    
                    for (int j = 0; j < _numberOfCharsToKeep - 1; j++)
                    {
                        previousCharacters[j] = previousCharacters[j + 1];
                    }
                    previousCharacters[_numberOfCharsToKeep - 1] = c;

                    
                    if (!inTextObject && CheckToken(new string[] { "BT" }, previousCharacters))
                    {
                        inTextObject = true;
                    }
                }
                return resultString;
            }
            catch
            {
                return "";
            }
        }
        #endregion

        #region CheckToken
        private bool CheckToken(string[] tokens, char[] recent)
        {
            foreach (string token in tokens)
            {
                if ((recent[_numberOfCharsToKeep - 3] == token[0]) &&
                    (recent[_numberOfCharsToKeep - 2] == token[1]) &&
                    ((recent[_numberOfCharsToKeep - 1] == ' ') ||
                    (recent[_numberOfCharsToKeep - 1] == 0x0d) ||
                    (recent[_numberOfCharsToKeep - 1] == 0x0a)) &&
                    ((recent[_numberOfCharsToKeep - 4] == ' ') ||
                    (recent[_numberOfCharsToKeep - 4] == 0x0d) ||
                    (recent[_numberOfCharsToKeep - 4] == 0x0a))
                    )
                {
                    return true;
                }
            }
            return false;
        }
        #endregion
    }
}


--- FILE: Utils\PDFSharpExtensions.cs ---
public static class PdfSharpExtensions
{
    public static string GetText(string pdfFileName)
    {
        var result = new StringBuilder();
        using (var _document = PdfReader.Open(pdfFileName, PdfDocumentOpenMode.ReadOnly))
        {
            
            foreach (var page in _document.Pages)
            {
                ExtractText(ContentReader.ReadContent(page), result);
                result.AppendLine();
            }
            return result.ToString();
        }
    }


    public static string ExtractText(this PdfPage page)
    {
        var result = new StringBuilder();
        ExtractText(ContentReader.ReadContent(page), result);
        result.AppendLine();
        return result.ToString();
    }
    #region CObject Visitor
    private static void ExtractText(CObject obj, StringBuilder target)
    {
        if (obj is CArray)
            ExtractText((CArray)obj, target);
        else if (obj is CComment)
            ExtractText((CComment)obj, target);
        else if (obj is CInteger)
            ExtractText((CInteger)obj, target);
        else if (obj is CName)
            ExtractText((CName)obj, target);
        else if (obj is CNumber)
            ExtractText((CNumber)obj, target);
        else if (obj is COperator)
            ExtractText((COperator)obj, target);
        else if (obj is CReal)
            ExtractText((CReal)obj, target);
        else if (obj is CSequence)
            ExtractText((CSequence)obj, target);
        else if (obj is CString)
            ExtractText((CString)obj, target);
        else
            throw new NotImplementedException(obj.GetType().AssemblyQualifiedName);
    }

    private static void ExtractText(CArray obj, StringBuilder target)
    {
        foreach (var element in obj)
        {
            ExtractText(element, target);
        }
    }
    private static void ExtractText(CComment obj, StringBuilder target) {  }
    private static void ExtractText(CInteger obj, StringBuilder target) {  }
    private static void ExtractText(CName obj, StringBuilder target) {  }
    private static void ExtractText(CNumber obj, StringBuilder target) {  }
    private static void ExtractText(COperator obj, StringBuilder target)
    {
        if (obj.OpCode.OpCodeName == OpCodeName.Tj || obj.OpCode.OpCodeName == OpCodeName.TJ)
        {
            foreach (var element in obj.Operands)
            {
                ExtractText(element, target);
            }
            target.Append(" ");
        }
    }
    private static void ExtractText(CReal obj, StringBuilder target) {  }
    private static void ExtractText(CSequence obj, StringBuilder target)
    {
        foreach (var element in obj)
        {
            ExtractText(element, target);
        }
    }
    private static void ExtractText(CString obj, StringBuilder target)
    {
        target.Append(obj.Value);
    }
    #endregion
}

namespace UtilsLib

    public class ProcessHelper
    {

        [DllImport("user32.dll")]
        private static extern uint GetWindowThreadProcessId(IntPtr hWnd, out uint lpdwProcessId);

        public static void SpawnAsync(IEnumerable<string> files)
        {
            files.ForEach(n => SpawnAsync(n));
        }
        public static int? SpawnAsync(string filename)
        {
            Process p = new Process();
            p.StartInfo.FileName = filename;

            if(File.Exists(filename) || (null != filename && filename.ToUpper().Contains(":
                p.Start();
            else
            {

            }

            return null;
        }

        public static bool TryKillProcessByMainWindowHwnd(int hWnd)
        {
            uint processID;
            GetWindowThreadProcessId((IntPtr)hWnd, out processID);
            return KillProcess((int)processID);
        }

        public enum CONSOLE_TYPE { CITRIX, REMOTE_DESKTOP, CONSOLE, UNKNOWN }

        public static CONSOLE_TYPE ProcessRunningUnder()
        {
            switch (Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("SESSIONNAME").ToUpper().Substring(0, 3))
            {
                case "ICA":
                    return CONSOLE_TYPE.CITRIX;
                    break;
                case "RDP":
                    return CONSOLE_TYPE.REMOTE_DESKTOP;
                    break;
                case "CON":
                    return CONSOLE_TYPE.CONSOLE;
                    break;
            }
            return CONSOLE_TYPE.UNKNOWN;
        }

        public static Nullable<int> StartProcess(string filename, int? timeout_in_ms)
        {
            filename = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(filename);
            Process p = new Process();
            p.StartInfo.FileName = filename;
            p.Start();
            
            if (null != timeout_in_ms)
                p.WaitForInputIdle(timeout_in_ms.Value);
            return p.Id;
        }

        public static bool ProcessRunning(string full_name, int timeout_in_ms)
        {
            string just_app_name = System.IO.Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(full_name);
            Process[] orig = System.Diagnostics.Process.GetProcessesByName(just_app_name);
            int total = 0;
            int sleep = 100;
            while (orig.Length == 0 && (total < timeout_in_ms))
            {
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(sleep);
                orig = System.Diagnostics.Process.GetProcessesByName(just_app_name);
                total += sleep;
            }

            return orig.Length > 0;
        }

        public static Nullable<int> WaitForNewProcess(string filename, int timeout_in_ms)
        {
            int wait = 150;
            string just_app_name = System.IO.Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(filename);
            Process[] orig = System.Diagnostics.Process.GetProcessesByName(just_app_name);
            List<int> pids = orig.Select(x => x.Id).ToList();
            int total = 0;
            do
            {
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(wait);
                List<int> all = System.Diagnostics.Process.GetProcessesByName(filename).Select(x => x.Id).ToList();
                foreach (int i in all)
                {
                    if (!pids.Contains(i))
                        return i;
                }
                total++;
            } while (total < timeout_in_ms);

            return null;
        }


        public static bool KillProcess(string exe)
        {
            string just_name = System.IO.Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(exe);
            Process[] orig = System.Diagnostics.Process.GetProcessesByName(just_name);
            bool found = false;
            foreach (Process p in orig)
            {
                p.Kill();
                p.WaitForExit();
                found = true;
            }
            return true;
        }

        public static bool KillProcess(int process_id, Nullable<int> wait_for_ms = null)
        {
            if (process_id == 0 || process_id == -1)
                return false;
            try
            {
                var process = System.Diagnostics.Process.GetProcessById(process_id);
                if(!process.HasExited)
                    process.Kill();
                if (null != wait_for_ms)
                    process.WaitForExit(wait_for_ms.Value);

                System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine("Process Killed: " + process_id);
            }
            catch (ArgumentException)
            {
                return false;
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return false;
            }
            return true;

        }

        [DllImport("user32", EntryPoint = "OpenDesktopA",
             CharSet = CharSet.Ansi,
             SetLastError = true,
             ExactSpelling = true)]


        private static extern Int32 OpenDesktop(string lpszDesktop,
                                                Int32 dwFlags,
                                                bool fInherit,
                                                Int32 dwDesiredAccess);

        [DllImport("user32", CharSet = CharSet.Ansi,
                     SetLastError = true,

        private static extern Int32 SwitchDesktop(Int32 hDesktop);

        [DllImport("user32", CharSet = CharSet.Ansi,
                     SetLastError = true,
                     ExactSpelling = true)]
        private static extern Int32 CloseDesktop(Int32 hDesktop);



        public static int GetPIDbyHWIND(int hWnd)
        {
            uint processID;
            GetWindowThreadProcessId((IntPtr)hWnd, out processID);
            return System.Convert.ToInt32(processID);
        }


        public static bool IsWorkstationLocked()
        {
            const int DESKTOP_SWITCHDESKTOP = 256;
            int hwnd = -1;
            int rtn = -1;

            hwnd = OpenDesktop("Default", 0, false, DESKTOP_SWITCHDESKTOP);

            if (hwnd != 0)
            {
                rtn = SwitchDesktop(hwnd);
                if (rtn == 0)
                {
                    
                    CloseDesktop(hwnd);
                    return true;
                }
                else
                {
                    
                    CloseDesktop(hwnd);
                }
            }
            else
            {
                
            }
            return false;
        }

        public static string SpawnDirectoryWithFileSelect(string full_file_path, bool show_error)
        {
            if (!System.IO.File.Exists(full_file_path) && show_error)
            {
                System.Windows.Forms.MessageBox.Show("File Not Found: " + full_file_path);
                return null;
            }
            Process p = new Process();
            p.StartInfo.FileName = "explorer.exe";
            string argument = @"/select, """ + full_file_path + @"""";
            p.StartInfo.Arguments = argument;
            p.Start();
            return full_file_path;
        }
        public static string SpawnDirectory(string full_path, bool show_error)
        {
            full_path = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(full_path);
            if (!System.IO.Directory.Exists(full_path) && show_error)
            {
                System.Windows.Forms.MessageBox.Show("Directory Not Found: " + full_path);
                return null;
            }
            Process p = new Process();
            p.StartInfo.FileName = full_path;
            p.Start();
            return full_path;
        }

        public static void ClearClipboardAnyThread()
        {
            Thread staThread = new Thread(x =>
            {
                try
                {
                    Clipboard.Clear();
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    string error = ex.Message;
                }
            });
            staThread.SetApartmentState(ApartmentState.STA);
            staThread.Start();
            staThread.Join();
        }
        public static void SetClipboardAnyThread(string value_to_set)
        {
            Thread staThread = new Thread(x =>
            {
                try
                {
                    Clipboard.SetText(value_to_set);
                }
                catch (Exception ex)
                {
                    string error = ex.Message;
                }
            });
            staThread.SetApartmentState(ApartmentState.STA);
            staThread.Start();
            staThread.Join();
        }

--- FILE: Utils\SchemaGenerator.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class GenerateSchema
    {

        public static string GenerateFromType(Type t)
        {
            List<TableClass> tables = new List<TableClass>();

            

            
            
            {
                TableClass tc = new TableClass(t);
                tables.Add(tc);
            }


            StringBuilder sql = new StringBuilder();

            
            foreach (TableClass table in tables)
            {
                sql.AppendLine(table.CreateTableScript());
            }

            


            foreach (TableClass table in tables)
            {
                foreach (KeyValuePair<String, Type> field in table.Fields)
                {
                    foreach (TableClass t2 in tables)
                    {
                        if (field.Value.Name == t2.ClassName)
                        {
                            
                            sql.AppendLine("GO");
                            sql.AppendLine("ALTER TABLE " + table.ClassName + " WITH NOCHECK");
                            sql.AppendLine("ADD CONSTRAINT FK_" + field.Key + " FOREIGN KEY (" + field.Key + ") REFERENCES " + t2.ClassName + "(ID)");
                            sql.AppendLine("GO");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return sql.ToString();
        }
    }

    public class TableClass
    {
        private List<KeyValuePair<String, Type>> _fieldInfo = new List<KeyValuePair<String, Type>>();
        private string _className = String.Empty;

        private Dictionary<Type, String> dataMapper
        {
            get
            {
                
                Dictionary<Type, String> dataMapper = new Dictionary<Type, string>();
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(int), "int");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(string), "NVARCHAR(500)");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(bool), "BIT");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(DateTime), "DATETIME");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(float), "FLOAT");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(double), "FLOAT");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(decimal), "DECIMAL(18,0)");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(Guid), "UNIQUEIDENTIFIER");

                dataMapper.Add(typeof(Nullable<double>), "FLOAT");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(Nullable<int>), "INT");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(Nullable<bool>), "BIT");
                dataMapper.Add(typeof(Nullable<DateTime>), "DATETIME");


                return dataMapper;
            }
        }

        public List<KeyValuePair<String, Type>> Fields
        {
            get { return this._fieldInfo; }
            set { this._fieldInfo = value; }
        }

        public string ClassName
        {
            get { return this._className; }
            set { this._className = value; }
        }

        public TableClass(Type t)
        {
            this._className = t.Name;

            foreach (PropertyInfo p in t.GetProperties())
            {
                KeyValuePair<String, Type> field = new KeyValuePair<String, Type>(p.Name, p.PropertyType);

                this.Fields.Add(field);
            }

            foreach (FieldInfo f in t.GetFields())
            {
                KeyValuePair<String, Type> field = new KeyValuePair<String, Type>(f.Name, f.FieldType);

                this.Fields.Add(field);
            }
        }

        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        
        

        

        
        


        public string CreateTableScript()
        {

            return CreateTableScript(this.ClassName, this.Fields);
        }


        public string CreateTableScript(DataTable data)
        {
            return CreateTableScript("NotSure", data.DataSet);
        }

        public string CreateTableScript(string table_name, DataSet data)
        {
            List<KeyValuePair<string, Type>> fields = new List<KeyValuePair<string, Type>>();

            foreach (DataTable tbl in data.Tables)
            {
                foreach (DataColumn col in tbl.Columns)
                {
                    var column = new KeyValuePair<string, Type>(col.ColumnName, col.DataType);
                    fields.Add(column);
                }

            }

            return CreateTableScript(table_name, fields);
        }

        public string CreateTableScript(string table_name, List<KeyValuePair<string, Type>> fields)
        {
            System.Text.StringBuilder script = new StringBuilder();

            script.AppendLine("CREATE TABLE " + table_name);
            script.AppendLine("(");
            script.AppendLine("\t ID INT,");
            for (int i = 0; i < fields.Count; i++)
            {
                KeyValuePair<String, Type> field = fields[i];

                if (dataMapper.ContainsKey(field.Value))
                {
                    script.Append("\t " + field.Key + " " + dataMapper[field.Value]);
                }
                else
                {
                    
                    script.Append("\t " + field.Key + " int");
                }

                if (i != this.Fields.Count - 1)
                {
                    script.Append(",");
                }

                script.Append(Environment.NewLine);
            }

            script.AppendLine(")");

            return script.ToString();
        }

    }
}

--- FILE: Utils\Validate.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class Validate
    {

        public static bool EntireColumnBlank(DataTable tbl, string column)
        {
            if (!tbl.Columns.Contains(column))
                return false;
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                if (row[column] != DBNull.Value)
                    return false;
            }
            return true;
        }

        public static bool IsValidInput(string cusip)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(cusip))
                return false;
            if (cusip.Contains("#"))
                return false;
            return true;
        }
        public static bool IsCusip(string cusip)
        {

            
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(cusip) || (null != cusip && (cusip.Length != 9) || cusip.Contains(",") || cusip.Contains(".") || cusip.Contains(" ") || cusip.Contains("-") || cusip.Contains("*")))
                return false;
            int c;
            if (!int.TryParse(cusip.Substring(8, 1), out c)) 
                return false;

            int actual_check = System.Convert.ToInt32(cusip[8].ToString());

            int check_digit = CalculateCheckDigit(cusip.Substring(0, 8));

            bool all_same = (cusip.Distinct().Count() == 1);
            if (all_same)
                return false;
            
            
            


            return check_digit == actual_check;
        }


        public static bool IsCusipOLD(string cusip)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(cusip) || (null != cusip && (cusip.Contains("#") || cusip.Length != 9 || cusip.Contains(" ") || cusip.Contains("-") || cusip.Contains(".") || cusip.Contains(",") || cusip.Contains("$"))))
                return false;
            else
            {
                return true;
            }
            
        }

        public static bool IsBBGID(string bbg_id)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(bbg_id) || (null != bbg_id && (bbg_id.Length != 12)))
            {
                return false;
            }
            return bbg_id.Substring(0, 3).ToUpper() == "BBG";
        }
        public static bool IsISIN(string isin)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(isin))
                return false;
            bool cusip = IsCusip(isin);
            List<string> shelves = new List<string>(new string[] { "AU", "CA", "ES", "GB", "HU", "ID", "IL", "KY", "MX", "MY", "PL", "RU", "TH", "TR", "US", "XA", "XS", "ZA", "IT" });
            if ((isin.Length == 12 || isin.Length == 11) && !isin.Contains(" ") && shelves.Contains(isin.Substring(0, 2).ToUpper()))
                return true;
            if ((isin.Length == 9) && isin.Substring(0, 1).ToUpper() == "G" && !isin.Contains(' '))
                return true;
            if ((isin.Length == 12) && isin.Substring(0, 2).ToUpper() == "XS")
                return true;
            return false;
        }

        public static bool IsShortTicker(string ticker)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ticker))
                return false;
            if (ticker.Contains('-') && ticker.Split('-').Length == 2)
            {
                if (ticker.Split('-')[0].Contains(' ') && ticker.Split('-')[0].Split(' ').Length == 2)
                {
                    int i;
                    string year = ticker.Split('-')[0].Split(' ')[1];
                    if (year.Length != 2)
                        return false;
                    if (Int32.TryParse(year, out i))
                    {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }
            return false;
        }

        public static string ShortToLongTicker(string short_ticker)
        {

            bool is_short = IsShortTicker(short_ticker);
            if (is_short)
            {
                if (short_ticker.Contains('-') && short_ticker.Split('-').Length == 2)
                {
                    if (short_ticker.Split('-')[0].Contains(' ') && short_ticker.Split('-')[0].Split(' ').Length == 2)
                    {
                        int i;
                        string year = short_ticker.Split('-')[0].Split(' ')[1];
                        if (Int32.TryParse(year, out i))
                        {
                            string year_assumed = "20";
                            if (i > DateTime.Now.Year + 5)
                                year_assumed = "19";
                            string new_bond = String.Format("{0} {1} {2}", short_ticker.Split(' ')[0], year_assumed + String.Format("{0:00}", i).ToString() + "-" + short_ticker.Split(' ')[1].Split('-')[1], short_ticker.Split(' ')[2]);
                            return new_bond;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return null;
        }
        public static bool IsTicker(string ticker)
        {
            if (null != ticker)
                ticker = ticker.Trim();
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ticker))
                return false;
            if (ticker.Split(' ').Length == 3 && ticker.Split('-').Length == 2 && ticker.Length <= 21)
            {
                string shelf = ticker.Split(' ')[0];
                string middle = ticker.Split(' ')[1];
                string year = null;
                string series = null;
                string tranche = ticker.Split(' ')[2];
                if (middle.Split('-').Length == 2)
                {
                    year = middle.Split('-')[0];
                    int t;
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    series = middle.Split('-')[1];
                }
                return true;
            }

            List<string> agency_shelves = new List<string>(new string[] { "G2", "FN", "GN", "FG", "FH", "FR" });
            if (ticker.Split(' ').Length == 2 && (agency_shelves.Contains(ticker.Split(' ')[0].ToUpper())) && (ticker.Split(' ')[1].Length == 6 || (ticker.Split(' ')[1].Length == 4)))
            {
                return true;
            }
            if (ticker.Split(' ').Length == 3 && ticker.Split(' ')[0].ToUpper() == "FHR")
            {
                return true;
            }
            if (ticker.Split(' ').Length == 3)
            {
                return true;
            }

            return false;
        }

        public static string CalcCusipCheckDigit(string cusip)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(cusip))
                return "";
            if (cusip.Length == 9)
                return cusip;
            int check_digit = CalculateCheckDigit(cusip);
            return cusip + check_digit.ToString();
        }



        public static int CalculateCheckDigit(string cusip)
        {

            int sum = 0;
            char[] digits = cusip.ToUpper().ToCharArray();
            string alphabet = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ*@#";

            for (int i = 0; i < digits.Length; i++)
            {
                int val;
                if (!int.TryParse(digits[i].ToString(), out val))
                    val = alphabet.IndexOf(digits[i]) + 10;

                if ((i % 2) != 0)
                    val *= 2;

                val = (val % 10) + (val / 10);

                sum += val;
            }

            int check = (10 - (sum % 10)) % 10;

            return check;
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        public static bool AllColumnsContain<T>(DataTable tbl, string column, T[] valid_values)
        {

            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                if (DBNull.Value != row[column])
                {
                    T rowval = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(row[column], typeof(T));
                    bool one_equals = false;
                    foreach (T valid in valid_values)
                    {
                        if (rowval.Equals(valid))
                            one_equals = true; ;
                    }
                    if (!one_equals)
                        return false;
                }
            }
            return true;
        }
        public static bool IndexAndMIPCheck(DataTable tbl, string index_column, string mip_column)
        {

            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                if (DBNull.Value != row[index_column])
                {
                    string row_index_val = row[index_column].ToString();
                    double row_mip_val = Convert.ToDouble(row[mip_column].ToString());
                    if (row_index_val == "CMT_1YR" && row_mip_val != 0.50)
                    {
                        return false;
                    }

                }
            }
            return true;
        }
        public static bool ColumnsDoNotEqual<T>(DataTable tbl, string column, T o)
        {
            int i = 0;

            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                if (DBNull.Value != row[column])
                {
                    T rowval = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(row[column], typeof(T));
                    if (rowval.Equals(o))
                        return false;
                }
                i++;
            }
            return true;
        }


        public enum MatchType { LESS_THAN, LESS_THAN_OR_EQUAL, EQUAL }
        public static bool ColumnAlwaysLessThan(DataTable tbl, string column_that_should_be_less, string column_that_should_be_greater)
        {
            return ColumnCompare(tbl, column_that_should_be_less, column_that_should_be_greater, MatchType.LESS_THAN);
        }
        public static bool ColumnAlwaysLessThanOrEqual(DataTable tbl, string column_that_should_be_less_than_or_equal, string column_that_should_be_greater)
        {
            return ColumnCompare(tbl, column_that_should_be_less_than_or_equal, column_that_should_be_greater, MatchType.LESS_THAN_OR_EQUAL);
        }
        public static bool ColumnEqual(DataTable tbl, string one, string two)
        {
            return ColumnCompare(tbl, one, two, MatchType.EQUAL);
        }
        public static bool ColumnCompare(DataTable tbl, string one_col, string two_col, MatchType mt)
        {
            int i = 0;

            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                if (DBNull.Value != row[one_col])
                {
                    double one = System.Convert.ToDouble(row[one_col]);
                    double two = System.Convert.ToDouble(row[two_col]);
                    if (mt == MatchType.LESS_THAN)
                    {
                        if (!(one < two))
                            return false;
                    }
                    if (mt == MatchType.LESS_THAN_OR_EQUAL)
                    {
                        if (one > two)
                            return false;
                    }
                    if (mt == MatchType.EQUAL)
                    {
                        throw new NotImplementedException();
                        if (one == two)
                            return false;
                    }
                }
                i++;
            }
            return true;
        }


        public static bool ColumnsAllEqual<T>(DataTable tbl, string column, T o)
        {
            return !ColumnsDoNotEqual<T>(tbl, column, o);
        }

        public static bool EntireColumnPopulated(DataTable tbl, string column)
        {
            if (!tbl.Columns.Contains(column))
                return false;
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                if (row[column] == DBNull.Value)
                    return false;
            }
            return true;
        }

    }
}

namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class Windows
    {
        [DllImport("user32.dll")]
        public static extern IntPtr GetWindowThreadProcessId(IntPtr hWnd, out IntPtr ProcessId);

        public static void Activate(string title)
        {
            
            IntPtr hWnd = FindWindow(null, title);
            if (hWnd.ToInt32() > 0) 
            {
                SetForegroundWindow(hWnd); 
            }
        }

        public static string GetScreenshotActiveWindow(string filename_base)
        {
            Windows.ScreenCapture sc = new Windows.ScreenCapture();
            
            
            
            
            
            IntPtr window = Windows.GetForegroundWindow();
            string file = UtilsLib.FileLib.GetQuickUniqueFile(filename_base, ".jpg", false);
            try
            {
                if (File.Exists(file))
                    File.Delete(file);
                sc.CaptureWindowToFile(window, file, ImageFormat.Jpeg);
            }catch
            {

            }

            return file;
        }
        public static void MinimizeActiveProcessWindow()
        {
            var currentProcess = System.Diagnostics.Process.GetCurrentProcess();
            Console.WriteLine(currentProcess.MainWindowTitle);

            IntPtr hWnd = currentProcess.MainWindowHandle;
            if (hWnd != IntPtr.Zero)
            {
                
                ShowWindow(hWnd, 0); 
            }
        }

        public static void WriteConsoleStatusBar(string message)
        {
            System.Console.Title = message;
        }


        public static void MaximizeWindow(string title)
        {
            
            IntPtr hWnd = FindWindow(null, title);
            if (hWnd.ToInt32() > 0) 
            {
                ShowWindow(hWnd, 3); 
            }
        }

        [System.Runtime.InteropServices.DllImport("user32.dll")]
        static extern bool ShowWindow(IntPtr hWnd, int nCmdShow);

        [DllImport("user32.dll")]
        public static extern IntPtr GetForegroundWindow();


        
        [DllImport("User32.dll", EntryPoint = "FindWindow")]
        private static extern IntPtr FindWindowNative(string className, string windowName);

        
        [DllImport("User32.dll", EntryPoint = "SetForegroundWindow")]
        private static extern IntPtr SetForegroundWindowNative(IntPtr hWnd);

        public static IntPtr FindWindow(string className, string windowName)
        {
            return FindWindowNative(className, windowName);
        }

        public static IntPtr SetForegroundWindow(IntPtr hWnd)
        {
            return SetForegroundWindowNative(hWnd);
        }
        public class ScreenCapture
        {
            public Image CaptureScreen()
            {
                return CaptureWindow(User32.GetDesktopWindow());
            }
            public Image CaptureWindow(IntPtr handle)
            {
                
                IntPtr hdcSrc = User32.GetWindowDC(handle);
                
                User32.RECT windowRect = new User32.RECT();
                User32.GetWindowRect(handle, ref windowRect);
                int width = windowRect.right - windowRect.left;
                int height = windowRect.bottom - windowRect.top;
                
                IntPtr hdcDest = GDI32.CreateCompatibleDC(hdcSrc);
                
                
                IntPtr hBitmap = GDI32.CreateCompatibleBitmap(hdcSrc, width, height);
                
                IntPtr hOld = GDI32.SelectObject(hdcDest, hBitmap);
                
                GDI32.BitBlt(hdcDest, 0, 0, width, height, hdcSrc, 0, 0, GDI32.SRCCOPY);
                
                GDI32.SelectObject(hdcDest, hOld);
                
                GDI32.DeleteDC(hdcDest);
                User32.ReleaseDC(handle, hdcSrc);

                
                Image img = Image.FromHbitmap(hBitmap);
                
                GDI32.DeleteObject(hBitmap);

                return img;
            }
            public void CaptureWindowToFile(IntPtr handle, string filename, ImageFormat format)
            {
                Image img = CaptureWindow(handle);
                img.Save(filename, format);
            }
            public void CaptureScreenToFile(string filename, ImageFormat format)
            {
                Image img = CaptureScreen();
                img.Save(filename, format);
            }
            private class GDI32
            {

                public const int SRCCOPY = 0x00CC0020; 

                [DllImport("gdi32.dll")]
                public static extern bool BitBlt(IntPtr hObject, int nXDest, int nYDest,
                    int nWidth, int nHeight, IntPtr hObjectSource,
                    int nXSrc, int nYSrc, int dwRop);
                [DllImport("gdi32.dll")]
                public static extern IntPtr CreateCompatibleBitmap(IntPtr hDC, int nWidth,
                    int nHeight);
                [DllImport("gdi32.dll")]
                public static extern IntPtr CreateCompatibleDC(IntPtr hDC);
                [DllImport("gdi32.dll")]
                public static extern bool DeleteDC(IntPtr hDC);
                [DllImport("gdi32.dll")]
                public static extern bool DeleteObject(IntPtr hObject);
                [DllImport("gdi32.dll")]
                public static extern IntPtr SelectObject(IntPtr hDC, IntPtr hObject);
            }
            private class User32
            {
                [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
                public struct RECT
                {
                    public int left;
                    public int top;
                    public int right;
                    public int bottom;
                }

                [DllImport("user32.dll")]
                public static extern IntPtr GetDesktopWindow();
                [DllImport("user32.dll")]
                public static extern IntPtr GetWindowDC(IntPtr hWnd);
                [DllImport("user32.dll")]
                public static extern IntPtr ReleaseDC(IntPtr hWnd, IntPtr hDC);
                [DllImport("user32.dll")]
                public static extern IntPtr GetWindowRect(IntPtr hWnd, ref RECT rect);

            }


        }
    }

        {

        public void InsertHTML(string table_variable_name, string html)
        {

            if (null == tableLocation)
                return;
            string path = System.IO.Path.GetTempFileName();

        public Range FindRange(string table_variable_name)
        {
            var range = _doc.Range();
            Word.Range tableLocation = null;
            while (range.Find.Execute("{{" + table_variable_name + "}}"))
            {
                tableLocation = range;
            }
            if (null == tableLocation)
                return null;
            return tableLocation;
        }

        public int? FindLastPageContainingVariables()
        {
            var range = _doc.Range();
            Word.Range tableLocation = null;
            while (range.Find.Execute("*\\{\\{*\\}\\}*",false,false,true,false,false,true))
            {
                tableLocation = range;
            }
            if (null == tableLocation)
                return null;
            return tableLocation.Information[WdInformation.wdActiveEndPageNumber];
        }


        public static void ChopOffPagesAfterLastVariable(UtilsLib.WordLib w)
        {
            int? page = w.FindLastPageContainingVariables();
           if (null == page)
                return;
            w.DeleteAllPagesIncludingAndAfter(page.Value);
        }
        public void DeleteAllPagesIncludingAndAfter(int page)
        {
            
            int total_pages = _doc.ComputeStatistics(WdStatistic.wdStatisticPages, false);
            int pages_to_delete = total_pages - page;
            
           
           
            

            for (int i = 0; i != pages_to_delete; i++)
            {
                Range one;
                _app.Selection.GoTo(What: WdGoToItem.wdGoToPage, Which: Word.WdGoToDirection.wdGoToAbsolute, Count: page);
                
                _app.Selection.Bookmarks[@"\Page"].Select();
                
                
                
                
                
                
                _app.Selection.Delete();
                
                if (i == pages_to_delete-1)
                {
                    _app.Selection.TypeBackspace();
                    _app.Selection.TypeBackspace();
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                }
                
                
                
         

                
                
                
                
                

                
                


                
                
                
                

            }

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        
        public void InsertTable(string table_variable_name,System.Data.DataTable table, FieldLib.Fields f)
        {
            Range tableLocation = FindRange(table_variable_name);
            
            if (null == tableLocation)
                return;
            if(null != table && table.Columns.Count == 0)
            {
                tableLocation.Delete();
                return;
            }
            Word.Table tbl = tableLocation.Tables.Add(tableLocation,table.Rows.Count+1, table.Columns.Count);
            
            
            
            
            
 
            tbl.Range.Font.Name = "Calibri";
            tbl.Range.Font.Color = WdColor.wdColorBlack;
            tbl.Range.Font.Size = 7.5F;
            tbl.Range.Font.Bold = 0;
            
            
            
            
            tbl.Rows.Alignment = WdRowAlignment.wdAlignRowCenter;
            
            


            
            tbl.Borders.InsideLineStyle = WdLineStyle.wdLineStyleSingle;
            tbl.Borders.OutsideLineStyle = WdLineStyle.wdLineStyleSingle;

            
            for (int c = 0; c != table.Columns.Count; c++)
            {
                tbl.Cell(1, c + 1).Range.Text = table.Columns[c].Caption;
                tbl.Cell(1, c + 1).Range.Font.Bold = 1;
                tbl.Cell(1, c + 1).Range.ParagraphFormat.Alignment = WdParagraphAlignment.wdAlignParagraphCenter;
                
                int color = System.Drawing.ColorTranslator.ToOle(System.Drawing.Color.LightGray);
                tbl.Rows[1].Shading.BackgroundPatternColor = (WdColor) color;
                tbl.Columns.AutoFit();
            }

            for (int r = 0; r !=  table.Rows.Count; r++)
            {
                for(int c = 0; c != table.Columns.Count; c++)
                {
                    
                    string txt = GetCorrectFormatting(table.Columns[c].ColumnName, table.Rows[r][c],f);

                    if (txt.Contains("TOTAL") && table.Rows.Count == r+1)
                    {

                        
                        
                        
                        tbl.Rows[r + 2].Shading.BackgroundPatternColor = WdColor.wdColorGray05;
                        tbl.Rows[r + 2].Range.Font.Bold = 1;
                        tbl.Rows[r + 2].Borders[WdBorderType.wdBorderBottom].LineStyle = WdLineStyle.wdLineStyleNone;
                        tbl.Rows[r + 2].Borders[WdBorderType.wdBorderLeft].LineStyle = WdLineStyle.wdLineStyleNone;
                        tbl.Rows[r + 2].Borders[WdBorderType.wdBorderRight].LineStyle = WdLineStyle.wdLineStyleNone;
                        tbl.Cell(r + 2, c + 1).Borders[WdBorderType.wdBorderLeft].LineStyle = WdLineStyle.wdLineStyleNone;
                        tbl.Cell(r + 2, c + 1).Borders[WdBorderType.wdBorderRight].LineStyle = WdLineStyle.wdLineStyleNone;
                        tbl.Rows[r + 2].Borders.InsideLineStyle = WdLineStyle.wdLineStyleNone;
                        
                    }
                    tbl.Cell(r + 2, c + 1).Range.Text = txt;
                    
                    
                   
                }
                tbl.Rows[r + 2].HeightRule = WdRowHeightRule.wdRowHeightAuto;
            }

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            tbl.AllowAutoFit = true;
            tbl.AutoFitBehavior(Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.WdAutoFitBehavior.wdAutoFitContent);
            tbl.Columns.AutoFit();
            
            
            tbl.Range.Paragraphs.Alignment = WdParagraphAlignment.wdAlignParagraphCenter;
            tbl.Range.ParagraphFormat.Alignment = WdParagraphAlignment.wdAlignParagraphCenter;
            
        }

        public void SaveAs(string full_new_name, bool overwrite)

        public void SaveAsInternal(string full_new_name, WdSaveFormat fmt, bool overwrite)
        {

            UtilsLib.FileLib.CreateDirectoriesAsNeeded(full_new_name);
            if (_doc.FullName == full_new_name)
                _doc.Save();
            else
            {
                if (System.IO.File.Exists(full_new_name) && overwrite)
                    System.IO.File.Delete(full_new_name);
                _doc.SaveAs2(full_new_name, fmt);
            }
            
        }

        public string ClearAllMergeFields()
        {
            string cleared = "";
            foreach (Word.MailMergeField field in _doc.MailMerge.Fields)
            {

                Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.Range rngFieldCode = field.Code;
                String fieldText = rngFieldCode.Text;
                if (fieldText.StartsWith(" MERGEFIELD"))
                {
                    Int32 endMerge = fieldText.IndexOf("\\");
                    Int32 fieldNameLength = fieldText.Length - endMerge;
                    String fieldName = fieldText.Substring(11, endMerge - 11);
                    fieldName = fieldName.Trim();

                    cleared += fieldName + Environment.NewLine;
                    
                    {
                        
                        {
                            field.Select();
                            _app.Selection.TypeText(" ");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            return cleared;
        }

        
        public List<string> RemainingMergeFields()
        {

            List<string> missing = new List<string>();
            foreach (Word.MailMergeField field in _doc.MailMerge.Fields)
            {
                Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.Range rngFieldCode = field.Code;
                String fieldText = rngFieldCode.Text;
                
                if (fieldText.StartsWith(" MERGEFIELD"))
                {
                    Int32 endMerge = fieldText.IndexOf("\\");
                    if (endMerge == -1)
                    {
                        endMerge = fieldText.IndexOf("\\");
                    }
                    String fieldName = fieldText.Substring(11, endMerge - 11);
                    fieldName = fieldName.Trim();
                    missing.Add(fieldName);
                }
            }
            return missing;
        }



        public void ChangeSelectedColor()
        {
            
            _app.Selection.Font.Shading.BackgroundPatternColorIndex = WdColorIndex.wdYellow;
        }
        public void ChangeSelectedColorBlue()
        {
            
            _app.Selection.Font.Shading.BackgroundPatternColorIndex = WdColorIndex.wdBlue;
        }

        public delegate void ExtraActionMergeField();
        private List<string> RenameMergeField<T>(Word.Document doc, Dictionary<string,T> maps, ExtraActionMergeField eamf, FieldLib.Fields fieldHelper)
        {
            
            
            List<string> blanks = new List<string>();
            foreach (Word.MailMergeField field in doc.MailMerge.Fields)
            {

                Microsoft.Office.Interop.Word.Range rngFieldCode = field.Code;
                String fieldText = rngFieldCode.Text;
                System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine(fieldText);
                if (fieldText.StartsWith(" MERGEFIELD"))
                {
                    Int32 endMerge = fieldText.IndexOf("\\");
                    if(endMerge == -1)
                    {
                        endMerge = fieldText.IndexOf("\\");
                    }
                    Int32 fieldNameLength = fieldText.Length - endMerge;
                    String fieldName = fieldText.Substring(11, endMerge - 11);
                    fieldName = fieldName.Trim();
                    
                    
                    {
                        
                        
                        if(maps.ContainsKeyIns<string,T>(fieldName))
                        {
                            T raw = maps[fieldName];
                            string newName = maps.GetKeyIns<string, T>(fieldName)?.ToString();
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            newName = GetCorrectFormatting(fieldName, raw, fieldHelper);

                            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(newName))
                            {
                                
                                
                                    blanks.Add(fieldName);
                                continue;
                            }
                            field.Select();
                            if(null != eamf)
                            {
                                eamf();
                            }
                            _app.Selection.TypeText(newName);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            
            foreach (Shape s in doc.Shapes)
            {
                try
                {
                    ProcessOddballFields(s.TextFrame.TextRange, maps, fieldHelper);
                } catch(System.Exception n)
                {
                    Debug.WriteLine(n.Message);
                }
            }
            

            
            foreach (Section sec in doc.Sections)
            {
                Word.Range rngFooter = sec.Footers[Word.WdHeaderFooterIndex.wdHeaderFooterPrimary].Range;

                foreach (HeaderFooter f in sec.Footers)
                {
                    ProcessOddballFields(f.Range, maps, fieldHelper);
                }
            }
            
            
            



            

            return blanks;

        }

        public void ProcessOddballFields<T>(Range r,Dictionary<string,T> maps,FieldLib.Fields f)
        {
            foreach (var map in maps)
            {
                string field_hack = "{{" + map.Key + "}}";
                string txt = r.Text;
                if (txt.Contains(field_hack))
                {
                    object val = map.Value?.ToString();
                    if(null != val)
                    {
                        val = GetCorrectFormatting(map.Key, map.Value, f);
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        

                        
                        
                        
                        
                    }
                    doReplace(r.Find, field_hack, val?.ToString());
                }
            }
        }

        public string GetCorrectFormatting<T>(string key,T map,FieldLib.Fields f)
        {

            string val = map?.ToString();
            if (map?.GetType() == typeof(Decimal) || map?.GetType() == typeof(Double))
            {
                double dbl;
                string format = "";
                if (null != f && f.ContainsField(key))
                {
                    format = (null != f[key].excel_format) ? f[key].excel_format : f[key].display_format;
                    if (format == "#,##0")
                        format = "#,0.00";
                    if (Double.TryParse(map?.ToString(), out dbl))
                    {
                        val = dbl.ToString(format);
                    }
                }
                
            }
            else if (map?.GetType() == typeof(DateTime))
                val = System.Convert.ToDateTime(val).ToString("M/d/yyyy");
            
            return val;
        }
        
        public int ReplaceTextWithMergeFieldInShapes(string sFieldName, ref Word.ShapeRange oRng)
        {
            int iFieldCounter = 0;
            Word.Field fldMerge;
            bool bFound;
            foreach (Word.Shape shp in oRng)
            {
                if (shp.Type == Microsoft.Office.Core.MsoShapeType.msoTextBox)
                {
                    Word.Range rngText = shp.TextFrame.TextRange;
                    rngText.Find.ClearFormatting();
                    rngText.Find.Forward = true;
                    rngText.Find.Wrap = Word.WdFindWrap.wdFindStop;
                    rngText.Find.Format = false;
                    rngText.Find.MatchCase = false;
                    rngText.Find.MatchWholeWord = false;
                    rngText.Find.MatchWildcards = false;
                    rngText.Find.MatchSoundsLike = false;
                    rngText.Find.MatchAllWordForms = false;
                    rngText.Find.Text = "<<" + sFieldName + ">>";
                    bFound = rngText.Find.Execute();
                    while (bFound)
                    {
                        iFieldCounter = iFieldCounter + 1;
                        fldMerge = rngText.Fields.Add(rngText, Word.WdFieldType.wdFieldMergeField, sFieldName, false);
                        rngText = fldMerge.Result;
                        rngText.Collapse(Word.WdCollapseDirection.wdCollapseEnd);
                        rngText.MoveStart(Word.WdUnits.wdCharacter, 2);
                        rngText.End = shp.TextFrame.TextRange.End;
                        rngText.Find.Text = sFieldName;
                        bFound = rngText.Find.Execute();
                    }
                }
            }
            return iFieldCounter;
        }

        private void doReplace(Find fnd, string search, string replace)
        {
            fnd.ClearFormatting();
            fnd.Replacement.ClearFormatting();
            fnd.Forward = true;
            fnd.Wrap = WdFindWrap.wdFindContinue;
            fnd.Text = search ;
            if(null != replace && replace.Length > 255)
                replace = replace.Substring(0, 255);
            fnd.Replacement.Text = replace;
            fnd.Execute(Replace: WdReplace.wdReplaceAll);
        }
        private void doReplaceTest(Find fnd, string search, string replace)
        {
            fnd.ClearFormatting();
            fnd.Replacement.ClearFormatting();
            fnd.Forward = true;
            fnd.Wrap = WdFindWrap.wdFindContinue;
            fnd.Text = search;
            if (null != replace && replace.Length > 255)
                replace = replace.Substring(0, 255);
            fnd.Replacement.Text = replace;
            fnd.Execute(Replace: WdReplace.wdReplaceAll);
        }
    }


}


--- FILE: Utils\XML.cs ---
namespace UtilsLib
{
    public class XML
    {

        public static T Deserialzie<T>(string xml) where T : class
        {
            T obj = null;
            XmlSerializer serializer = new XmlSerializer(typeof(T));
            using (StringReader reader = new StringReader(xml))
            {
                obj = (T)serializer.Deserialize(reader);
            }
            return obj;
        }

        public static string Serialize<T>(T dataToSerialize)
        {
            try
            {
                var stringwriter = new System.IO.StringWriter();
                var serializer = new XmlSerializer(typeof(T));
                serializer.Serialize(stringwriter, dataToSerialize);
                return stringwriter.ToString();
            }
            catch
            {
                throw;
            }
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Extensions\Arrays.cs ---
namespace Extensions
{
    public static class Arrays
    {

        public static void Shuffle<T>(this IList<T> list)
        {
            Random rng = new Random();
            int n = list.Count;
            while (n > 1)
            {
                n--;
                int k = rng.Next(n + 1);
                T value = list[k];
                list[k] = list[n];
                list[n] = value;
            }
        }

        public static bool IsNullOrEmpty<T>(this IEnumerable<T> items)
        {
            return items == null || !items.Any();
        }

        public static bool ContainsAnyInList<T>(this IList<T> list, IList<T> other)
        {
            foreach (T t in other)
            {
                if (list.Contains(t))
                    return true;
            }
            return false;
        }



        public static void ReOrderAfter<T>(this List<T> lst, T insert_after, T item_to_insert_after)
        {
            if (lst.Contains(insert_after))
            {
                if (lst.Contains(item_to_insert_after))
                    lst.Remove(item_to_insert_after);
                int after = lst.IndexOf(insert_after);

                lst.Insert(after + 1, item_to_insert_after);
            }
        }
        public static string InsertStatementsHack<T>(this IList<T> list, string table)
        {
            List<string> things = new List<string>();
            foreach (T t in list)
            {
                string sql = DbWriteString(typeof(T), t);
                sql = String.Format("insert into @{1} values ({0})", sql, table);
                things.Add(sql);
            }
            return String.Join(Environment.NewLine, things.ToArray());
        }

        public static Nullable<T> GetMajorityItem<T>(this IList<T> list, Nullable<double> pct) where T : struct
        {
            if (list.Count() == 0)
                return null;
            Dictionary<T, int> results = new Dictionary<T, int>();
            int all = 0;
            foreach (T t in list)
            {
                if (!results.ContainsKey(t))
                {
                    results.Add(t, 0);
                }
                results[t]++;
                all++;
            }
            int max = results.Values.Max();
            Nullable<T> result = null;
            foreach (KeyValuePair<T, int> kvp in results)
            {
                if (kvp.Value == max)
                    result = kvp.Key;
            }
            if (null == pct)
                return result;
            else
            {
                double how = max / all;
                if (how > pct.Value)
                    return result;
                return null;
            }
            return result;
        }

        public static T GetMajorityItemNull<T>(this IList<T> list, Nullable<double> pct)
        {
            if (list.Count() == 0)
                return default(T);
            Dictionary<T, int> results = new Dictionary<T, int>();
            int all = 0;
            foreach (T t in list)
            {
                if (!results.ContainsKey(t))
                {
                    results.Add(t, 0);
                }
                results[t]++;
                all++;
            }
            int max = results.Values.Max();
            T result = default(T);
            foreach (KeyValuePair<T, int> kvp in results)
            {
                if (kvp.Value == max)
                    result = kvp.Key;
            }
            if (null == pct)
                return result;
            else
            {
                double how = max / all;
                if (how > pct.Value)
                    return result;
                return default(T);
            }
            return result;
        }

        
        public static string DbWriteString(Type t, object val)
        {
            if (null != val)
                val = val.ToString().Trim();
            if (null == val)
                return "null";
            if (t == typeof(string) || t == typeof(DateTime) || t == typeof(DateTimeOffset) || t == typeof(TimeSpan) || t == typeof(Char) || t == typeof(object) && (null != val && val.ToString().Length > 0))
            {
                val = "'" + val.ToString().Replace("'", "''") + "'";
            }
            else if (null != val && t == typeof(bool))
            {
                val = System.Convert.ToBoolean(val) ? 1 : 0;
            }
            if (null == val || val == DBNull.Value || String.IsNullOrEmpty(val.ToString()) || (null != val && val.ToString() == "''") || (t == typeof(double) && val.ToString() == "Infinity"))
                return "null";
            else
                return val.ToString();
        }



    }
}

namespace Extensions
