    public static class AssemblyHelper
    {
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        

        
        

        

        
        

        
        
        

        

        
        

        
        

        struct _IMAGE_FILE_HEADER
        {
            public ushort Machine;
            public ushort NumberOfSections;
            public uint TimeDateStamp;
            public uint PointerToSymbolTable;
            public uint NumberOfSymbols;
            public ushort SizeOfOptionalHeader;
            public ushort Characteristics;
        };

        public static DateTime GetLinkerDateTime(this Assembly assembly, TimeZoneInfo tzi = null)
        {
            var filePath = assembly.Location;
            const int c_PeHeaderOffset = 60;
            const int c_LinkerTimestampOffset = 8;

            var buffer = new byte[2048];

            using (var stream = new FileStream(filePath, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read))
                stream.Read(buffer, 0, 2048);

            var offset = BitConverter.ToInt32(buffer, c_PeHeaderOffset);
            var secondsSince1970 = BitConverter.ToInt32(buffer, offset + c_LinkerTimestampOffset);
            var epoch = new DateTime(1970, 1, 1, 0, 0, 0, DateTimeKind.Utc);

            var linkTimeUtc = epoch.AddSeconds(secondsSince1970);

            return linkTimeUtc;
        }
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
    }
}


--- FILE: Extensions\CloneHelper.cs ---
namespace Extensions
{
    public static class ObjectCopier
    {
        public static T Clone<T>(this T source)
        {
            if (!typeof(T).IsSerializable)
            {
                throw new ArgumentException("The type must be serializable.", "source");
            }

            
            if (Object.ReferenceEquals(source, null))
            {
                return default(T);
            }

            IFormatter formatter = new BinaryFormatter();
            Stream stream = new MemoryStream();
            using (stream)
            {
                formatter.Serialize(stream, source);
                stream.Seek(0, SeekOrigin.Begin);
                return (T)formatter.Deserialize(stream);
            }
        }



        public static T CloneAlt<T>(this T source)
        {
            T result = Activator.CreateInstance<T>();
            return result;
        }


    }
}

        public static bool EntireColumnBlank(this DataColumn col)
        {
            foreach(DataRow row in col.Table.Rows)
            {
                if (null != row[col] && row[col] != DBNull.Value)
                    return false;
            }
            return true;
        }
        public static T FirstNonNullValue<T>(this DataColumn col)
        {
            foreach (DataRow row in col.Table.Rows)
            {
                if (null != row[col] && row[col] != DBNull.Value)
                    return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(row[col], typeof(T));
            }
            return default(T);
        }

            {
                if (null != row[col] && row[col] != DBNull.Value)
                    return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(row[col], typeof(T));

            return null;

        public static bool EntireColumnOverValue(this DataColumn col,double max_value)
        {
            bool atleast_one = false;
            foreach (DataRow row in col.Table.Rows)
            {

                if (null != row[col] && row[col] != DBNull.Value)
                {
                    if(row[col].AsDouble() < max_value)
                        return false;
                    atleast_one = true;
                }
            }
            
            
            return true;
        }

        public static bool EntireColumnUnderValue(this DataColumn col, double min_value)
        {
            bool atleast_one = false;
            foreach (DataRow row in col.Table.Rows)
            {

                if (null != row[col] && row[col] != DBNull.Value)
                {
                    if (row[col].AsDouble() > min_value)
                        return false;
                    atleast_one = true;
                }
            }
            
            
            return true;
        }

        public static DataColumn InsertAt(this DataColumnCollection tbl, string column_name, Type t, object default_value = null, int? ordial = null)
        {
            DataColumn c = null;
            if (tbl.Count == 0)
            {
               
            } 
            else
            {
                c = tbl[0].Table.Columns.Add(column_name,t);
                if (null != default_value)
                {
                    foreach (DataRow row in c.Table.Rows)
                        row[c] = default_value;
                    
                }
                if (null != ordial)
                    c.SetOrdinal(ordial.Value);
            }
            return c;
        }


        public static List<T> UniqueValues<T>(this DataColumn column, bool unique_only = true, bool include_null = true)
        {
            DataTable tbl = column.Table;
            if (tbl.Rows.Count <= 100)
            {
                List<T> answer = new List<T>();
                foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
                {

                    if (DBNull.Value != row[column])
                    {
                        T o = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(row[column], typeof(T));
                        if (!answer.Contains(o) || unique_only == false)
                        {
                            if (include_null == false && null == o)
                                continue;
                            answer.Add(o);
                        }
                    }
                }
                return answer;
            }
            else
            {
                var results = tbl.AsEnumerable().Select(myRow => myRow.Field<T>(column)).ToList();
                if (!include_null)
                    results.RemoveAll(n => (n == null || null == DBNull.Value));
                if (unique_only)
                    return results.Distinct().ToList();
                return results.ToList();
            }
        }

        public static ConversionResult ChangeDataType(this DataColumn col, Type newtype)
        {
            return ChangeDataTypeInternal(col, newtype, true);
        }

        public class ConversionResult
        {
            public bool success;
            public object bad_value;
            public string column;
            public int row;
            public string message
            {
                get
                {
                    return $"Column={column} : Row={row} : Value={bad_value}";
                }
            }
        }

        public static void ChangeTypeCustom(this object o,Type newtype)
        {
            if ((null != o && o == DBNull.Value) || String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(o.ToString()))
                o = null;
            if (newtype == typeof(DateTime) && (null != o && DBNull.Value != o))
            {
                if (null != o)
                {
                    Double d;
                    if (Double.TryParse(o.ToString(), out d))
                    {
                        o = DateTime.FromOADate(d);
                    }
                }
            }
            if (newtype == typeof(bool) && (null != o && DBNull.Value != o))
            {
                if (o.ToString().ToUpper() == "Y" || o.ToString().ToUpper() == "N" || o.ToString().ToUpper() == "YES" || o.ToString().ToUpper() == "NO" || o.ToString().ToUpper() == "1" || o.ToString().ToUpper() == "0")
                {
                    if (o.ToString().ToUpper().Contains("Y") || o.ToString() == "1")
                        o = true;
                    else if (o.ToString().ToUpper().Contains("N") || o.ToString() == "0")
                        o = false;
                }
            }

        }
        public static ConversionResult ChangeDataTypeInternal(this DataColumn col, Type newtype,bool modify)
        {
            if (col.Table.Columns.Contains(col.ColumnName) == false)
                return null;
            if (col.Table.Columns[col.ColumnName].DataType == newtype)
                return new ConversionResult {  success = true };

            ConversionResult result = new ConversionResult();
            result.success = true;

            DataColumn column = col.Table.Columns[col.ColumnName];
            int ordial = column.Ordinal;
            if (column.DataType == newtype)
                return result;
            DataTable tbl_copy = col.Table;
            try
            {
                DataColumn newcolumn = new DataColumn("temporary", newtype);
                
                
                col.Table.Columns.Add(newcolumn);
                int row_num = 1;
                foreach (DataRow row in col.Table.Rows)
                {
                    try
                    {
                        object o = row[col.ColumnName];

                        
                        if (null != o && DBNull.Value != o)
                        {
                            
                            bool can_change_type = o.CanChangeType(newtype);
                            if(!can_change_type)
                            {
                                result.bad_value = o;
                                result.success = false;
                                result.column = col.ColumnName;
                                result.row = row_num;
                                break;
                                
                            }
                            if(modify)
                                row["temporary"] = Convert.ChangeType(o, newtype);
                        }
                        row_num++;
                    }
                    catch
                    {
                        return null;
                    }
                }
                if (modify)
                {
                    DataTable tbl = col.Table;
                    tbl.Columns.Remove(col.ColumnName);
                    newcolumn.ColumnName = col.ColumnName;
                    
                    newcolumn.SetOrdinal(ordial);
                }
                                
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {

                return result;
            }

            if (tbl_copy.Columns.Contains("temporary"))
                tbl_copy.Columns.Remove("temporary");
            return result;
        }
        public static void CleanBlankColumns(this DataColumn col, object replace_obj)
        {
            DataTable tbl = col.Table;
            if (col.DataType != replace_obj.GetType())
            {
               col.ChangeDataType(typeof(object));
            }
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {

                if (DBNull.Value == row[col.ColumnName])
                {

                    row[col.ColumnName] = replace_obj;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

        {
            if (coll.Contains(column_name))
                return coll[column_name];
            System.Data.DataColumn newColumn = new System.Data.DataColumn(column_name, typeof(T));
            newColumn.DefaultValue = default_value;
            coll.Add(newColumn);
            return newColumn;
        }

        {

                        return true;

namespace Extensions

    public static class DataRowHelper

        public static object GetRowValueEvenIfDeleted(this DataRow row, DataColumn col)
        {
            object rowval = null;
            if (row.RowState == DataRowState.Deleted)
            {
                rowval = row[col, DataRowVersion.Original];
                
            }
            else
                rowval = row[col];
            return rowval;
        }


        public static List<string> BlankColsFromCSV(this DataRow row, string csv_cols)
        {
            List<string> blank = new List<string>();
            foreach(string col in csv_cols.Split(','))
            {
                object o = row[col];
                if(DBNull.Value == o || null == o)
                {
                    blank.Add(col);
                }
            }
            return blank;
        }
        public static bool AllColumnsHaveValue(this DataRow dr,string csv_of_rows)
        {
            foreach(string s in csv_of_rows.Split(','))
            {
                if (null == dr[s] || DBNull.Value == dr[s])
                    return false;
            }
            return true;
        }
        public static bool EntireRowEmpty(this DataRow dr)
        {
            if (dr == null)
            {
                return true;
            }
            else
            {
                foreach (var value in dr.ItemArray)
                {
                    if (value != null && DBNull.Value != value)
                    {
                        return false;
                    }
                }
                return true;
            }
        }
        public static Dictionary<string, T> ToDictionary<T>(this DataRow row) where T : class
        {
            Dictionary<string, T> kvp = new Dictionary<string, T>();
            foreach (DataColumn c in row.Table.Columns)
            {
                object raw = null;
                if(row.RowState == DataRowState.Deleted)
                    raw = row[c.ColumnName,DataRowVersion.Original];
                else
                    raw = row[c.ColumnName];
                T val = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != raw)
                    val = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(raw, typeof(T));
                kvp.Add(c.ColumnName, val);
            }
            return kvp;
        }
        public static void SetSmartly(this DataRow row, string column, object value)
        {
            if (null != value)
            {
                row[column] = value;
            }
            if (null == value && DBNull.Value != row[column])
                row[column] = DBNull.Value;
        }

        public static bool CellUpdated(this DataRow row, string column_name, bool ignoreWhitespace)
        {
            bool isEqual = true;
            DataColumn col = row.Table.Columns[column_name];

            StringComparison stringComparison = StringComparison.InvariantCultureIgnoreCase;

            if (row[col, DataRowVersion.Original] != DBNull.Value && row[col, DataRowVersion.Current] != DBNull.Value)
            {
                if (ignoreWhitespace)
                    isEqual = row[col, DataRowVersion.Original].ToString().Trim().Equals(row[col, DataRowVersion.Current].ToString().Trim(), stringComparison);
                else
                    isEqual = row[col, DataRowVersion.Original].ToString().Equals(row[col, DataRowVersion.Current].ToString(), stringComparison);
            }
            else
                isEqual = row[col, DataRowVersion.Original].Equals(row[col, DataRowVersion.Current]);

            return !isEqual;

        }

        public static T RowDataHelper<T>(this DataRow row, string column_name)
        {
            return RowDataHelper<T>(row, column_name, false);
        }
        public static T RowDataHelper<T>(this DataRow row, string column_name, bool trim)
        {
            T s = default(T);
            object o = row[column_name];
            if (DBNull.Value != row[column_name])
            {
                if (o.GetType() == typeof(string))
                {
                    o = row[column_name].ToString().Trim();
                }
                s = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType((T)o, typeof(T));
            }
            return s;
        }

    }
}

namespace Extensions
{
    public static partial class DataSetHelper
    {
        public static string ToXml(this DataSet ds)
        {
            using (var memoryStream = new MemoryStream())
            {
                using (TextWriter streamWriter = new StreamWriter(memoryStream))
                {
                    var xmlSerializer = new XmlSerializer(typeof(DataSet));
                    xmlSerializer.Serialize(streamWriter, ds);
                    return Encoding.UTF8.GetString(memoryStream.ToArray());
                }
            }
        }



    }

}

        public static void AppendTotals(this DataTable table,IEnumerable<string> cols_to_total)
        {
            DataRow totalRow = table.NewRow();

            foreach (DataColumn col in table.Columns)
            {
                if (null == cols_to_total)
                {
                    if (col.DataType == typeof(int) || col.DataType == typeof(double))
                    {
                        totalRow[col] = table.Compute($"SUM({col.ColumnName})", string.Empty);
                    }
                }
                else if(cols_to_total.Contains(col.ColumnName))
                {
                    totalRow[col] = table.Compute($"SUM({col.ColumnName})", string.Empty);
                }
            }

            table.Rows.Add(totalRow);
        }

        
        public static bool RowExists(this DataTable tbl, string lookup_column, string lookup_key)
        {
            DataRow row = GetSingleRow(tbl, lookup_column, lookup_key);
            if (null == row)
                return false;
            return true;
        }
        public static void AppendColumnsToTable(this DataTable source,IEnumerable<DataColumn> cols_2_append)
        {
            DataTable tbl = new DataTable();
            foreach(DataColumn col in cols_2_append)
            {
                if (!source.Columns.Contains(col.ColumnName))
                    throw new Exception("Columns not contained in source table");
                tbl.Columns.Add(col.ColumnName, col.DataType);
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in cols_2_append.First().Table.Rows)
            {
                DataRow new_row = source.Rows.Add();
                foreach (DataColumn col in cols_2_append)
                {
                    new_row[col.ColumnName] = row[col.ColumnName];
                }
            }
            source.AcceptChanges();
        }

        public static void CleanBlankColumns(this DataTable tbl, IEnumerable<string> cols, object replace_obj)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i != tbl.Columns.Count; i++)
            {
                DataColumn col = tbl.Columns[i];
                if (cols.Contains(col.ColumnName))
                {
                    col.CleanBlankColumns(replace_obj);
                }
            }
        }

        public static void ChangeColumnsAsNeeded(this DataTable tbl,Dictionary<string,Type> overrides)
        {
            foreach(var ovr in overrides)
            {
                if (tbl.Columns.Contains(ovr.Key) && (tbl.Columns[ovr.Key].DataType != ovr.Value))
                { 
                    tbl.Columns[ovr.Key].ChangeDataType(ovr.Value);
                }
            }
        }

        public static void TrimBlankColumns(this DataTable tbl)
        {
            List<string> cols_2_remove = new List<string>();
            foreach(DataColumn col in tbl.Columns)
            {
                bool all_empty = col.EntireColumnBlank();
                if (all_empty)
                    cols_2_remove.Add(col.ColumnName);
            }
            foreach(string s in cols_2_remove)
            {
                tbl.Columns.Remove(s);
            }
        }

        {
            List<string> cols = cols_2_keep.Select(n => n.ColumnName).ToList();
            return CopyAndTrimColumns(tbl,cols);

        public static DataSet CopyAndTrimColumns(this DataSet set, string csv)
        {
            string[] visible_cols_table = csv.Split('|');
            int which_tbl = 0;
            DataSet set_cpy = new DataSet();
            foreach (DataTable tbl in set.Tables)
            {
                DataTable t = tbl.CopyAndTrimColumns(visible_cols_table[which_tbl]);
                which_tbl++;
                set_cpy.Tables.Add(t.Copy());
            }

            return set_cpy;
        }

        public static void TrimBlankRows(this DataTable tbl)
        {

            List<DataRow> rows = tbl.Rows.Cast<DataRow>().Where(row => row.EntireRowEmpty()).ToList();
            rows.ForEach(n => tbl.Rows.Remove(n));
            if (rows.Count > 0)
                tbl.AcceptChanges();
            
        }
        public static DataTable CopyAndTrimColumns(this DataTable tbl,List<string> cols_2_keep)
        {
            if (cols_2_keep.Count() == 0 || (cols_2_keep.Count() == 1 && String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(cols_2_keep[0])))
                return tbl;
            List<DataColumn> cols2remove = new List<DataColumn>();
            DataTable copy = tbl.Copy();
            foreach(DataColumn col in copy.Columns)
            {
                if (!cols_2_keep.Contains(col.ColumnName))
                    cols2remove.Add(col);
            }

            foreach (var remove in cols2remove)
                copy.Columns.Remove(remove);
            return copy;
        }
        public static List<T> ToList<T>(this DataTable tbl, string column)
        {

            if (null == column)
                column = tbl.Columns[0].ColumnName;
            return tbl.Columns[column].ToList<T>();
        }

        public static Dictionary<T,K> ToDictionaryUnique<T,K>(this DataTable tbl, string key_column,string value_column)
        {
            Dictionary<T, K> ret = new Dictionary<T, K>();
            foreach(DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                if(DBNull.Value != row[key_column])
                {
                    T key = (T)row[key_column];
                    if(!ret.ContainsKey(key) && (null != row[value_column] && DBNull.Value != row[value_column]))
                    {
                        K val = (K)row[value_column];
                        ret.Add(key, val);
                    }
                }
            }
            return ret;
        }

        public static Dictionary<T, List<K>> ToDictionaryListUnique<T, K>(this DataTable tbl, string key_column, string value_column)
        {
            Dictionary<T, List<K>> ret = new Dictionary<T, List<K>>();
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                if (DBNull.Value != row[key_column])
                {
                    T key = (T)row[key_column];
                    if ((null != row[value_column] && DBNull.Value != row[value_column]))
                    {
                        if(!ret.ContainsKey(key))
                            ret.Add(key, new List<K>());
                        K val = (K)row[value_column];
                        if(!ret[key].Contains(val))
                            ret[key].Add(val);
                        
                    }
                }
            }
            return ret;
        }

        public static bool RowsAllHaveValue(this DataTable tbl, string csv_of_cols)
        {
            foreach (DataRow dr in tbl.Rows)
            {
                bool has_value = dr.AllColumnsHaveValue(csv_of_cols);
                if(!has_value)
                    return false;
            }
            return true;
        }

            return result;
        }

        public static void ExportTabDelimited(this DataTable tbl, string filename)
        {
            StringBuilder str = new StringBuilder();
            
            foreach (DataColumn c in tbl.Columns)
            {
                str.Append("\"" + c.ColumnName.ToString() + "\"\t");
            }
            str.Append("\r\n");

            
            foreach (DataRow dr in tbl.Rows)
            {
                foreach (var field in dr.ItemArray)
                {
                    str.Append("\"" + field.ToString() + "\"\t");
                }
                str.Append("\r\n");
            }

            System.IO.File.WriteAllText(filename, str.ToString());

        }

        public static void RemoveRowsInternal<T>(this DataSet set, string column, List<T> values, bool remove_if_not_in)
        {
            foreach (DataTable t in set.Tables)
            {
                t.RemoveRowsInternal<T>(column, values, remove_if_not_in);
            }
            set.AcceptChanges();
        }
        public static void RemoveRowsInternal<T>(this DataTable t, string column, List<T> values,bool remove_if_not_in)
        {

            
            {
                List<DataRow> rows_2_delete = new List<DataRow>();
                foreach (DataRow row in t.Rows)
                {
                    if (remove_if_not_in)
                    {
                        if (!values.Contains((T)row[column]))
                            rows_2_delete.Add(row);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        if (values.Contains((T)row[column]))
                            rows_2_delete.Add(row);
                    }
                }

                foreach (DataRow r in rows_2_delete)
                {
                    r.Delete();
                }
                t.AcceptChanges();
            }
            
        }
        public static List<T> ListBasedOnID<T, Y>(this DataTable table, List<Y> ids, string searchCol, string retCal)
        {
            List<T> products = new List<T>();
            foreach (DataRow row in table.Rows)
            {
                T list_type = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(row[retCal], typeof(T));
                Y bwic_id = (Y)row[searchCol];

                if (!products.Contains(list_type) && ids.Contains(bwic_id))
                    products.Add(list_type);
            }
            return products;
        }

        public static T? GetMaxBasedOnThreshold<T>(this DataTable tbl, string label_column, string count_column, double threshold) where T : struct  
        {
            string s = GetMaxBasedOnThresholdNullable(tbl, label_column, count_column, threshold);
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(s))
                return null;

            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(s, typeof(T));
        }
        public static string GetMaxBasedOnThresholdNullable(this DataTable tbl, string label_column, string count_column, double threshold)
        {

            Dictionary<string, double> results = new Dictionary<string, double>();

            double total = 0;
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                string col = row[label_column].ToString();
                if (DBNull.Value == row[count_column])
                    continue;
                double val = System.Convert.ToDouble(row[count_column]);
                total += val;
                if (!results.ContainsKey(col))
                    results.Add(col, 0);
                results[col] += val;

            }
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, double> kvp in results)
            {
                double pct = kvp.Value / total;
                if (pct > threshold)
                    return kvp.Key;
            }
            return null;
        }



        public static List<T> GetUniqueList<T>(this DataTable tbl, string column)
        {
            List<T> list = new List<T>();
            foreach (DataRow r in tbl.Rows)
            {
                if (DBNull.Value == r[column])
                    continue;
                T t = (T)r[column];
                if (!list.Contains(t))
                    list.Add(t);
            }
            return list;
        }

        private enum MAXMIN { MAX, MIN };
        private static Nullable<int> MinMaxInternal(DataTable table, string column, MAXMIN m)
        {
            int minAccountLevel = int.MaxValue;
            int maxAccountLevel = int.MinValue;
            foreach (DataRow dr in table.Rows)
            {
                int accountLevel = dr.Field<int>("AccountLevel");
                if (m == MAXMIN.MIN)
                    minAccountLevel = Math.Min(minAccountLevel, accountLevel);
                if (m == MAXMIN.MAX)
                    maxAccountLevel = Math.Max(maxAccountLevel, accountLevel);
            }
            return m == MAXMIN.MAX ? maxAccountLevel : minAccountLevel;
        }

        public static DataRow GetSingleRow(this DataTable tbl, string lookup_column, string lookup_key)
        {
            string sql = String.Format("{0} = '{1}'", lookup_column, lookup_key);
            DataRow[] rows = tbl.Select(sql);
            if (rows.Length == 1)
                return rows[0];
            if (rows.Length > 1)
                throw new Exception("Multiple Rows Found");
            return null;
        }
        public static DataRow GetSingleRowAny(this DataTable tbl, string lookup_column, string lookup_key)
        {
            string sql = String.Format("{0} = '{1}'", lookup_column, lookup_key);
            DataRow[] rows = tbl.Select(sql);
            if (rows.Length == 0)
                throw new Exception("No Rows Found");
            if (rows.Length > 0)
                return rows[0];

            return null;
        }


        public static void RemoveSingleRow(this DataTable tbl, int zero_based_row_index)
        {
            tbl.Rows[zero_based_row_index].Delete();
            tbl.AcceptChanges();
        }

        public static DataTable Transpose(this DataTable inputTable)
        {
            if (inputTable.Rows.Count == 0)
                return null;
            DataTable outputTable = new DataTable();
            outputTable.Columns.Add("HEADER", typeof(string));
            for (int i = 1; i <= inputTable.Rows.Count; i++) outputTable.Columns.Add(string.Format("ROW{0}",i), typeof(object));

            foreach (DataColumn col in inputTable.Columns)
            {
                DataRow row = outputTable.Rows.Add();
                row[0] = col.Caption;
                for (int i = 1; i<= inputTable.Rows.Count; i++)
                    row[i] = col.Table.Rows[i-1][col];
                
            }
            return outputTable;
        }
        public static List<DataColumn> GetChangedColumns(this DataTable table)

        public static List<DataColumn> GetChangedColumns(this DataTable table, StringComparison stringComparison, bool ignoreWhitespace)
        {
            if (table == null) throw new ArgumentNullException("table");

            List<DataColumn> columnsChanged = new List<DataColumn>();
            foreach (DataRow row in table.GetChanges().Rows)
            {
                if (row.RowState == DataRowState.Added)
                {

                }
                foreach (DataColumn col in row.Table.Columns)
                {
                    
                    bool test = hasColumnChanged(stringComparison, ignoreWhitespace, row, col);
                    
                    {
                        columnsChanged.Add(col);
                    }
                }
                
            }
            return columnsChanged;
        }

        public static List<DataColumn> GetChangedColumns(this DataRow row)
        {
            return row.GetChangedColumns(StringComparison.InvariantCultureIgnoreCase, false);
        }
        public static List<DataColumn> GetChangedColumns(this DataRow row, bool ignoreWhitespace)
        {
            return row.GetChangedColumns(StringComparison.InvariantCultureIgnoreCase, ignoreWhitespace);
        }
        public static List<DataColumn> GetChangedColumns(this DataRow row, StringComparison stringComparison, bool ignoreWhitespace)
        {
            if (row == null) throw new ArgumentNullException("row");

            List<DataColumn> columnsChanged = new List<DataColumn>();
            foreach (DataColumn col in row.Table.Columns)
            {
                if (!columnsChanged.Contains(col) && hasColumnChanged(stringComparison, ignoreWhitespace, row, col))
                    columnsChanged.Add(col);
            }
            return columnsChanged;
        }

        private static bool hasColumnChanged(StringComparison stringComparison, bool ignoreWhitespace, DataRow row, DataColumn col)
        {
            bool isEqual = true;
            if (!row.HasVersion(DataRowVersion.Original))
            {
                return false;
            }
            else if (row.RowState == DataRowState.Deleted)
            {
                return false;
            }
            if (row[col, DataRowVersion.Original] != DBNull.Value && row[col, DataRowVersion.Current] != DBNull.Value)
            {
                if (ignoreWhitespace)
                    isEqual = row[col, DataRowVersion.Original].ToString().Trim().Equals(row[col, DataRowVersion.Current].ToString().Trim(), stringComparison);
                else
                    isEqual = row[col, DataRowVersion.Original].ToString().Equals(row[col, DataRowVersion.Current].ToString(), stringComparison);
            }
            else
                isEqual = row[col, DataRowVersion.Original].Equals(row[col, DataRowVersion.Current]);

            return !isEqual;
        }

        public static void ReOrder<T>(this DataTable tbl, string column, List<T> values,bool throw_error)
        {
            if (null == values)
                return;
            if(values.Count != tbl.Rows.Count)
            {
                if (throw_error)
                    throw new Exception("Row Count Mismatch");
                else
                    return;
            }
            DataSet set = tbl.DataSet.Copy();
            DataTable cpy = tbl.Copy();
            DataTable newTbl = tbl.Clone();
            tbl.Clear();
            foreach (T s in values)
            {
                
                string sql = String.Format("{0} = '{1}'", column, s.ToString());
                DataRow[] rows = cpy.Select(sql);
                foreach (DataRow row in rows)
                    tbl.Rows.Add(row.ItemArray);
            }

            
        }
        public static DataTable TrimColumms(this DataTable tbl, string csv_format)
        {
            DataTable t = tbl.Copy();
            
            
            List<string> cols = new List<string>(csv_format.Split(','));
            List<string> duplicates = cols.GroupBy(x => x).Where(g => g.Count() > 1).Select(g => g.Key).ToList();
            if(duplicates.Count> 0)
            {
                throw new Exception("Duplicate Columns in CSV Format");
            }
            List<DataColumn> removes = new List<DataColumn>();
            foreach (DataColumn col in t.Columns)
            {
                if (!cols.Contains(col.ColumnName))
                    removes.Add(col);
            }
            foreach (DataColumn s in removes)
            {
                t.Columns.Remove(s);
            }
            foreach (string s in cols)
            {
                DataColumn col = t.Columns[s];
                if (null == col)
                    col = t.Columns.Add(s);
            }

            foreach (DataColumn col in t.Columns)
            {
                if (!cols.Contains(col.ColumnName))
                {

                }
            }

            int count = 0;
            foreach (string s in cols)
            {
                DataColumn col = t.Columns[s];
                col.SetOrdinal(count);
                count++;
            }
            return t;
        }


        public static Dictionary<string, T> SingleRowToDict<T>(this DataTable tbl)
        {
            Dictionary<string, T> t = new Dictionary<string, T>();

            for (int i = 0; i != tbl.Columns.Count; i++)
            {
                string column = tbl.Columns[i].ColumnName;
                T value = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(tbl.Rows[0][i], typeof(T));
                if (null != value && value.ToString() == "")
                    value = default(T);
                t.Add(column, value);
            }
            return t;
        }

        public static void Sort(this DataTable tbl, string column, bool asc)
        {
            tbl.DefaultView.Sort = column + (asc ? " ASC" : " DESC");
            tbl.DefaultView.ToTable();
        }

        public static DataSet SplitByRowsIntoTables<T>(this DataTable tbl, string split_by_column, string table_name_prefix,bool include_nulls)
        {
            IEnumerable<T> splits = tbl.UniqueValues<T>(split_by_column, include_nulls);
            DataSet ds = new DataSet();
            int table_num = 0;
            foreach (var split in splits)
            {
                var rows = tbl.Select($"[{split_by_column}] = '{split}'");
                var tbl_clean = tbl.Clone();
                tbl_clean.TableName = $"{table_name_prefix}_{table_num++}";
                ds.Tables.Add(tbl_clean);
                foreach (var row in rows)
                {
                    tbl_clean.ImportRow(row);
                }
            }
            return ds;
        }
    }

namespace Extensions
{
    public static class DateTimeHelper
    {

        public static DateTime RoundTime(this DateTime dt, TimeSpan d)
        {
            return new DateTime(((dt.Ticks + d.Ticks - 1) / d.Ticks) * d.Ticks);
        }

        public static DateTime RoundTime(this DateTime dt, int minutes)
        {
            TimeSpan ts = new TimeSpan(0, minutes, 0);
            return dt.RoundTime(ts);
        }

        public static DateTime GetNextWeekday(this DateTime start, DayOfWeek day)
        {
            
            int daysToAdd = ((int)day - (int)start.DayOfWeek + 7) % 7;
            return start.AddDays(daysToAdd);
        }
        public static DateTime SetDay(this DateTime dt, int day)
        {
            return new DateTime(dt.Year, dt.Month, day);
        }
        public static DateTime SetYear(this DateTime dt, int year)
        {
            return new DateTime(year, dt.Month, dt.Day);
        }

        public static DateTime SetTime(this DateTime dt, int army_hour, int minutes)
        {
            return new DateTime(dt.Year, dt.Month, dt.Day).AddHours(army_hour).AddMinutes(minutes);
        }

        public static int DaysDiff(this DateTime one, DateTime two)
        {
            DateTime first = new DateTime(one.Year, one.Month, one.Day);
            DateTime second = new DateTime(two.Year, two.Month, two.Day);

            return System.Convert.ToInt32((first - second).TotalDays);
        }

        public static DateTime LastDayOfMonth(this DateTime dt)
        {
            return new DateTime(dt.Year, dt.Month, 1).AddMonths(1).AddDays(-1);
        }

        public static DateTime FirstDayOfMonth(this DateTime dt)
        {
            return new DateTime(dt.Year, dt.Month, 1);
        }
        public static DateTime FirstDayOfYear(this DateTime dt)
        {
            return new DateTime(dt.Year, 1, 1);
        }
        public static DateTime LastDayOfYear(this DateTime dt)
        {
            return new DateTime(dt.Year + 1, 1, 1).AddDays(-1);
        }

        public static bool SameMonth(this DateTime one, DateTime two)
        {
            if (one.Month == two.Month && one.Year == two.Year)
                return true;
            return false;
        }

        public static int MonthsApart(this DateTime date1, DateTime date2)
        {
            return ((date1.Year - date2.Year) * 12) + date1.Month - date2.Month;
        }


        public static bool BetweenMonths(this DateTime dateinquestion, DateTime begin, DateTime end)
        {
            if (dateinquestion >= begin && dateinquestion <= end)
                return true;
            return false;
        }

        public static bool SameDay(this DateTime one, DateTime two)
        {
            if (one.Month == two.Month && one.Year == two.Year && one.Day == two.Day)
                return true;
            return false;
        }


        public static int Days360(this DateTime? date, DateTime? initialDate)
        {
            return Days360(date.Value, initialDate.Value);
        }

        public static int Days360(this DateTime date, DateTime initialDate)
        {
            var dateA = initialDate;

            var dateB = date;

            var dayA = dateA.Day;

            var dayB = dateB.Day;

            if (lastDayOfFebruary(dateA) && lastDayOfFebruary(dateB))
                dayB = 30;

            if (dayA == 31 && lastDayOfFebruary(dateA))
                dayA = 30;

            if (dayA == 30 && dayB == 31)
                dayB = 30;

            int days = (dateB.Year - dateA.Year) * 360 +
                ((dateB.Month + 1) - (dateA.Month + 1)) * 30 + (dayB - dayA);

            return days;

        }

        private static bool lastDayOfFebruary(DateTime date)
        {

            int lastDay = DateTime.DaysInMonth(date.Year, 2);

            return date.Day == lastDay;
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Extensions\DeepCopyByExpressionTrees.cs ---
namespace DeepCopyExtensions
{
    public static class DeepCopyByExpressionTrees
    {
        private static readonly object IsStructTypeToDeepCopyDictionaryLocker = new object();
        private static Dictionary<Type, bool> IsStructTypeToDeepCopyDictionary = new Dictionary<Type, bool>();

        private static readonly object CompiledCopyFunctionsDictionaryLocker = new object();
        private static Dictionary<Type, Func<object, Dictionary<object, object>, object>> CompiledCopyFunctionsDictionary =
            new Dictionary<Type, Func<object, Dictionary<object, object>, object>>();

        private static readonly Type ObjectType = typeof(Object);
        private static readonly Type ObjectDictionaryType = typeof(Dictionary<object, object>);
        public static T DeepCopyByExpressionTree<T>(this T original, Dictionary<object, object> copiedReferencesDict = null)
        {
            return (T)DeepCopyByExpressionTreeObj(original, false, copiedReferencesDict ?? new Dictionary<object, object>(new ReferenceEqualityComparer()));
        }

        private static object DeepCopyByExpressionTreeObj(object original, bool forceDeepCopy, Dictionary<object, object> copiedReferencesDict)
        {
            if (original == null)
            {
                return null;
            }

            var type = original.GetType();

            if (IsDelegate(type))
            {
                return null;
            }

            if (!forceDeepCopy && !IsTypeToDeepCopy(type))
            {
                return original;
            }

            object alreadyCopiedObject;

            if (copiedReferencesDict.TryGetValue(original, out alreadyCopiedObject))
            {
                return alreadyCopiedObject;
            }

            if (type == ObjectType)
            {
                return new object();
            }

            var compiledCopyFunction = GetOrCreateCompiledLambdaCopyFunction(type);

            object copy = compiledCopyFunction(original, copiedReferencesDict);

            return copy;
        }

        private static Func<object, Dictionary<object, object>, object> GetOrCreateCompiledLambdaCopyFunction(Type type)
        {
            
            
            
            

            Func<object, Dictionary<object, object>, object> compiledCopyFunction;

            if (!CompiledCopyFunctionsDictionary.TryGetValue(type, out compiledCopyFunction))
            {
                lock (CompiledCopyFunctionsDictionaryLocker)
                {
                    if (!CompiledCopyFunctionsDictionary.TryGetValue(type, out compiledCopyFunction))
                    {
                        var uncompiledCopyFunction = CreateCompiledLambdaCopyFunctionForType(type);

                        compiledCopyFunction = uncompiledCopyFunction.Compile();

                        var dictionaryCopy = CompiledCopyFunctionsDictionary.ToDictionary(pair => pair.Key, pair => pair.Value);

                        dictionaryCopy.Add(type, compiledCopyFunction);

                        CompiledCopyFunctionsDictionary = dictionaryCopy;
                    }
                }
            }

            return compiledCopyFunction;
        }

        private static Expression<Func<object, Dictionary<object, object>, object>> CreateCompiledLambdaCopyFunctionForType(Type type)
        {
            ParameterExpression inputParameter;
            ParameterExpression inputDictionary;
            ParameterExpression outputVariable;
            ParameterExpression boxingVariable;
            LabelTarget endLabel;
            List<ParameterExpression> variables;
            List<Expression> expressions;

            InitializeExpressions(type,
                                  out inputParameter,
                                  out inputDictionary,
                                  out outputVariable,
                                  out boxingVariable,
                                  out endLabel,
                                  out variables,
                                  out expressions);

            IfNullThenReturnNullExpression(inputParameter, endLabel, expressions);

            MemberwiseCloneInputToOutputExpression(type, inputParameter, outputVariable, expressions);

            if (IsClassOtherThanString(type))
            {
                StoreReferencesIntoDictionaryExpression(inputParameter, inputDictionary, outputVariable, expressions);
            }

            FieldsCopyExpressions(type,
                                  inputParameter,
                                  inputDictionary,
                                  outputVariable,
                                  boxingVariable,
                                  expressions);

            if (IsArray(type) && IsTypeToDeepCopy(type.GetElementType()))
            {
                CreateArrayCopyLoopExpression(type,
                                              inputParameter,
                                              inputDictionary,
                                              outputVariable,
                                              variables,
                                              expressions);
            }

            var lambda = CombineAllIntoLambdaFunctionExpression(inputParameter, inputDictionary, outputVariable, endLabel, variables, expressions);

            return lambda;
        }

        private static void InitializeExpressions(Type type,
                                                  out ParameterExpression inputParameter,
                                                  out ParameterExpression inputDictionary,
                                                  out ParameterExpression outputVariable,
                                                  out ParameterExpression boxingVariable,
                                                  out LabelTarget endLabel,
                                                  out List<ParameterExpression> variables,
                                                  out List<Expression> expressions)
        {

            inputParameter = Expression.Parameter(ObjectType);

            inputDictionary = Expression.Parameter(ObjectDictionaryType);

            outputVariable = Expression.Variable(type);

            boxingVariable = Expression.Variable(ObjectType);

            endLabel = Expression.Label();

            variables = new List<ParameterExpression>();

            expressions = new List<Expression>();

            variables.Add(outputVariable);
            variables.Add(boxingVariable);
        }

        private static void IfNullThenReturnNullExpression(ParameterExpression inputParameter, LabelTarget endLabel, List<Expression> expressions)
        {

            var ifNullThenReturnNullExpression =
                Expression.IfThen(
                    Expression.Equal(
                        inputParameter,
                        Expression.Constant(null, ObjectType)),
                    Expression.Return(endLabel));

            expressions.Add(ifNullThenReturnNullExpression);
        }

        private static void MemberwiseCloneInputToOutputExpression(
            Type type,
            ParameterExpression inputParameter,
            ParameterExpression outputVariable,
            List<Expression> expressions)
        {

            var memberwiseCloneMethod = ObjectType.GetMethod("MemberwiseClone", BindingFlags.NonPublic | BindingFlags.Instance);

            var memberwiseCloneInputExpression =
                Expression.Assign(
                    outputVariable,
                    Expression.Convert(
                        Expression.Call(
                            inputParameter,
                            memberwiseCloneMethod),
                        type));

            expressions.Add(memberwiseCloneInputExpression);
        }

        private static void StoreReferencesIntoDictionaryExpression(ParameterExpression inputParameter,
                                                                          ParameterExpression inputDictionary,
                                                                          ParameterExpression outputVariable,
                                                                          List<Expression> expressions)
        {

            var storeReferencesExpression =
                Expression.Assign(
                    Expression.Property(
                        inputDictionary,
                        ObjectDictionaryType.GetProperty("Item"),
                        inputParameter),
                    Expression.Convert(outputVariable, ObjectType));

            expressions.Add(storeReferencesExpression);
        }

        private static Expression<Func<object, Dictionary<object, object>, object>> CombineAllIntoLambdaFunctionExpression(
            ParameterExpression inputParameter,
            ParameterExpression inputDictionary,
            ParameterExpression outputVariable,
            LabelTarget endLabel,
            List<ParameterExpression> variables,
            List<Expression> expressions)
        {
            expressions.Add(Expression.Label(endLabel));

            expressions.Add(Expression.Convert(outputVariable, ObjectType));

            var finalBody = Expression.Block(variables, expressions);

            var lambda = Expression.Lambda<Func<object, Dictionary<object, object>, object>>(finalBody, inputParameter, inputDictionary);

            return lambda;
        }

        private static void CreateArrayCopyLoopExpression(Type type,
                                                          ParameterExpression inputParameter,
                                                          ParameterExpression inputDictionary,
                                                          ParameterExpression outputVariable,
                                                          List<ParameterExpression> variables,
                                                          List<Expression> expressions)
        {

            var rank = type.GetArrayRank();

            var indices = GenerateIndices(rank);

            variables.AddRange(indices);

            var elementType = type.GetElementType();

            var assignExpression = ArrayFieldToArrayFieldAssignExpression(inputParameter, inputDictionary, outputVariable, elementType, type, indices);

            Expression forExpression = assignExpression;

            for (int dimension = 0; dimension < rank; dimension++)
            {
                var indexVariable = indices[dimension];

                forExpression = LoopIntoLoopExpression(inputParameter, indexVariable, forExpression, dimension);
            }

            expressions.Add(forExpression);
        }

        private static List<ParameterExpression> GenerateIndices(int arrayRank)
        {

            var indices = new List<ParameterExpression>();

            for (int i = 0; i < arrayRank; i++)
            {
                var indexVariable = Expression.Variable(typeof(Int32));

                indices.Add(indexVariable);
            }

            return indices;
        }

        private static BinaryExpression ArrayFieldToArrayFieldAssignExpression(
            ParameterExpression inputParameter,
            ParameterExpression inputDictionary,
            ParameterExpression outputVariable,
            Type elementType,
            Type arrayType,
            List<ParameterExpression> indices)
        {

            var indexTo = Expression.ArrayAccess(outputVariable, indices);

            var indexFrom = Expression.ArrayIndex(Expression.Convert(inputParameter, arrayType), indices);

            var forceDeepCopy = elementType != ObjectType;

            var rightSide =
                Expression.Convert(
                    Expression.Call(
                        DeepCopyByExpressionTreeObjMethod,
                        Expression.Convert(indexFrom, ObjectType),
                        Expression.Constant(forceDeepCopy, typeof(Boolean)),
                        inputDictionary),
                    elementType);

            var assignExpression = Expression.Assign(indexTo, rightSide);

            return assignExpression;
        }

        private static BlockExpression LoopIntoLoopExpression(
            ParameterExpression inputParameter,
            ParameterExpression indexVariable,
            Expression loopToEncapsulate,
            int dimension)
        {

            var lengthVariable = Expression.Variable(typeof(Int32));

            var endLabelForThisLoop = Expression.Label();

            var newLoop =
                Expression.Loop(
                    Expression.Block(
                        new ParameterExpression[0],
                        Expression.IfThen(
                            Expression.GreaterThanOrEqual(indexVariable, lengthVariable),
                            Expression.Break(endLabelForThisLoop)),
                        loopToEncapsulate,
                        Expression.PostIncrementAssign(indexVariable)),
                    endLabelForThisLoop);

            var lengthAssignment = GetLengthForDimensionExpression(lengthVariable, inputParameter, dimension);

            var indexAssignment = Expression.Assign(indexVariable, Expression.Constant(0));

            return Expression.Block(
                new[] { lengthVariable },
                lengthAssignment,
                indexAssignment,
                newLoop);
        }

        private static BinaryExpression GetLengthForDimensionExpression(
            ParameterExpression lengthVariable,
            ParameterExpression inputParameter,
            int i)
        {

            var getLengthMethod = typeof(Array).GetMethod("GetLength", BindingFlags.Public | BindingFlags.Instance);

            var dimensionConstant = Expression.Constant(i);

            return Expression.Assign(
                lengthVariable,
                Expression.Call(
                    Expression.Convert(inputParameter, typeof(Array)),
                    getLengthMethod,
                    new[] { dimensionConstant }));
        }

        private static void FieldsCopyExpressions(Type type,
                                                  ParameterExpression inputParameter,
                                                  ParameterExpression inputDictionary,
                                                  ParameterExpression outputVariable,
                                                  ParameterExpression boxingVariable,
                                                  List<Expression> expressions)
        {
            var fields = GetAllRelevantFields(type);

            var readonlyFields = fields.Where(f => f.IsInitOnly).ToList();
            var writableFields = fields.Where(f => !f.IsInitOnly).ToList();

            bool shouldUseBoxing = readonlyFields.Any();

            if (shouldUseBoxing)
            {
                var boxingExpression = Expression.Assign(boxingVariable, Expression.Convert(outputVariable, ObjectType));

                expressions.Add(boxingExpression);
            }

            foreach (var field in readonlyFields)
            {
                if (IsDelegate(field.FieldType))
                {
                    ReadonlyFieldToNullExpression(field, boxingVariable, expressions);
                }
                else
                {
                    ReadonlyFieldCopyExpression(type,
                                                field,
                                                inputParameter,
                                                inputDictionary,
                                                boxingVariable,
                                                expressions);
                }
            }

            if (shouldUseBoxing)
            {
                var unboxingExpression = Expression.Assign(outputVariable, Expression.Convert(boxingVariable, type));

                expressions.Add(unboxingExpression);
            }

            foreach (var field in writableFields)
            {
                if (IsDelegate(field.FieldType))
                {
                    WritableFieldToNullExpression(field, outputVariable, expressions);
                }
                else
                {
                    WritableFieldCopyExpression(type,
                                                field,
                                                inputParameter,
                                                inputDictionary,
                                                outputVariable,
                                                expressions);
                }
            }
        }

        private static FieldInfo[] GetAllRelevantFields(Type type, bool forceAllFields = false)
        {
            var fieldsList = new List<FieldInfo>();

            var typeCache = type;

            while (typeCache != null)
            {
                fieldsList.AddRange(
                    typeCache
                        .GetFields(BindingFlags.Instance | BindingFlags.Public | BindingFlags.NonPublic | BindingFlags.FlattenHierarchy)
                        .Where(field => forceAllFields || IsTypeToDeepCopy(field.FieldType)));

                typeCache = typeCache.BaseType;
            }

            return fieldsList.ToArray();
        }

        private static FieldInfo[] GetAllFields(Type type)
        {
            return GetAllRelevantFields(type, forceAllFields: true);
        }

        private static readonly Type FieldInfoType = typeof(FieldInfo);
        private static readonly MethodInfo SetValueMethod = FieldInfoType.GetMethod("SetValue", new[] { ObjectType, ObjectType });

        private static void ReadonlyFieldToNullExpression(FieldInfo field, ParameterExpression boxingVariable, List<Expression> expressions)
        {
            
            

            var fieldToNullExpression =
                    Expression.Call(
                        Expression.Constant(field),
                        SetValueMethod,
                        boxingVariable,
                        Expression.Constant(null, field.FieldType));

            expressions.Add(fieldToNullExpression);
        }

        private static readonly Type ThisType = typeof(DeepCopyByExpressionTrees);
        private static readonly MethodInfo DeepCopyByExpressionTreeObjMethod = ThisType.GetMethod("DeepCopyByExpressionTreeObj", BindingFlags.NonPublic | BindingFlags.Static);

        private static void ReadonlyFieldCopyExpression(Type type,
                                                        FieldInfo field,
                                                        ParameterExpression inputParameter,
                                                        ParameterExpression inputDictionary,
                                                        ParameterExpression boxingVariable,
                                                        List<Expression> expressions)
        {
            
            

            var fieldFrom = Expression.Field(Expression.Convert(inputParameter, type), field);

            var forceDeepCopy = field.FieldType != ObjectType;

            var fieldDeepCopyExpression =
                Expression.Call(
                    Expression.Constant(field, FieldInfoType),
                    SetValueMethod,
                    boxingVariable,
                    Expression.Call(
                        DeepCopyByExpressionTreeObjMethod,
                        Expression.Convert(fieldFrom, ObjectType),
                        Expression.Constant(forceDeepCopy, typeof(Boolean)),
                        inputDictionary));

            expressions.Add(fieldDeepCopyExpression);
        }

        private static void WritableFieldToNullExpression(FieldInfo field, ParameterExpression outputVariable, List<Expression> expressions)
        {

            var fieldTo = Expression.Field(outputVariable, field);

            var fieldToNullExpression =
                Expression.Assign(
                    fieldTo,
                    Expression.Constant(null, field.FieldType));

            expressions.Add(fieldToNullExpression);
        }

        private static void WritableFieldCopyExpression(Type type,
                                                        FieldInfo field,
                                                        ParameterExpression inputParameter,
                                                        ParameterExpression inputDictionary,
                                                        ParameterExpression outputVariable,
                                                        List<Expression> expressions)
        {

            var fieldFrom = Expression.Field(Expression.Convert(inputParameter, type), field);

            var fieldType = field.FieldType;

            var fieldTo = Expression.Field(outputVariable, field);

            var forceDeepCopy = field.FieldType != ObjectType;

            var fieldDeepCopyExpression =
                Expression.Assign(
                    fieldTo,
                    Expression.Convert(
                        Expression.Call(
                            DeepCopyByExpressionTreeObjMethod,
                            Expression.Convert(fieldFrom, ObjectType),
                            Expression.Constant(forceDeepCopy, typeof(Boolean)),
                            inputDictionary),
                        fieldType));

            expressions.Add(fieldDeepCopyExpression);
        }

        private static bool IsArray(Type type)
        {
            return type.IsArray;
        }

        private static bool IsDelegate(Type type)
        {
            return typeof(Delegate).IsAssignableFrom(type);
        }

        private static bool IsTypeToDeepCopy(Type type)
        {
            return IsClassOtherThanString(type)
                   || IsStructWhichNeedsDeepCopy(type);
        }

        private static bool IsClassOtherThanString(Type type)
        {
            return !type.IsValueType && type != typeof(String);
        }

        private static bool IsStructWhichNeedsDeepCopy(Type type)
        {
            
            
            
            

            bool isStructTypeToDeepCopy;

            if (!IsStructTypeToDeepCopyDictionary.TryGetValue(type, out isStructTypeToDeepCopy))
            {
                lock (IsStructTypeToDeepCopyDictionaryLocker)
                {
                    if (!IsStructTypeToDeepCopyDictionary.TryGetValue(type, out isStructTypeToDeepCopy))
                    {
                        isStructTypeToDeepCopy = IsStructWhichNeedsDeepCopy_NoDictionaryUsed(type);

                        var newDictionary = IsStructTypeToDeepCopyDictionary.ToDictionary(pair => pair.Key, pair => pair.Value);

                        newDictionary[type] = isStructTypeToDeepCopy;

                        IsStructTypeToDeepCopyDictionary = newDictionary;
                    }
                }
            }

            return isStructTypeToDeepCopy;
        }

        private static bool IsStructWhichNeedsDeepCopy_NoDictionaryUsed(Type type)
        {
            return IsStructOtherThanBasicValueTypes(type)
                   && HasInItsHierarchyFieldsWithClasses(type);
        }

        private static bool IsStructOtherThanBasicValueTypes(Type type)
        {
            return type.IsValueType
                   && !type.IsPrimitive
                   && !type.IsEnum
                   && type != typeof(Decimal);
        }

        private static bool HasInItsHierarchyFieldsWithClasses(Type type, HashSet<Type> alreadyCheckedTypes = null)
        {
            alreadyCheckedTypes = alreadyCheckedTypes ?? new HashSet<Type>();

            alreadyCheckedTypes.Add(type);

            var allFields = GetAllFields(type);

            var allFieldTypes = allFields.Select(f => f.FieldType).Distinct().ToList();

            var hasFieldsWithClasses = allFieldTypes.Any(IsClassOtherThanString);

            if (hasFieldsWithClasses)
            {
                return true;
            }

            var notBasicStructsTypes = allFieldTypes.Where(IsStructOtherThanBasicValueTypes).ToList();

            var typesToCheck = notBasicStructsTypes.Where(t => !alreadyCheckedTypes.Contains(t)).ToList();

            foreach (var typeToCheck in typesToCheck)
            {
                if (HasInItsHierarchyFieldsWithClasses(typeToCheck, alreadyCheckedTypes))
                {
                    return true;
                }
            }

            return false;
        }

        public class ReferenceEqualityComparer : EqualityComparer<Object>
        {
            public override bool Equals(object x, object y)
            {
                return ReferenceEquals(x, y);
            }

            public override int GetHashCode(object obj)
            {
                if (obj == null) return 0;

                return obj.GetHashCode();
            }
        }
    }
}

namespace Extensions

    public static partial class Extensions
    {
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public static bool ContainsKeyIns<T,Z>(this Dictionary<T,Z> dict, T case_insensitve_key)
        {
            if (typeof(T) == typeof(int))
                return dict.ContainsKey(case_insensitve_key);
            foreach(var kvp in dict)
            {
                if(kvp.Key.ToString().ToUpper() == case_insensitve_key.ToString().ToUpper())
                {
                    return true;
                }
            }
            return false;
        }


        public static Z GetKeyIns<T, Z>(this Dictionary<T, Z> dict, T case_insensitve_key)
        {
            if (typeof(T) == typeof(int))
                return dict[case_insensitve_key];
            foreach (var kvp in dict)
            {
                if (kvp.Key.ToString().ToUpper() == case_insensitve_key.ToString().ToUpper())
                {
                    return kvp.Value;
                }
            }
            throw new Exception("Key Not Found");
        }

        public static void AddRange<T, S>(this Dictionary<T, S> source, Dictionary<T, S> collection)
        {
            if (collection == null)
            {
                throw new ArgumentNullException("Collection is null");
            }

            foreach (var item in collection)
            {
                if (!source.ContainsKey(item.Key))
                {
                    source.Add(item.Key, item.Value);
                }
                else
                {
                    
                }
            }
        }

        public static void RenameKey<TKey, TValue>(this Dictionary<TKey, TValue> dic,
                                      TKey fromKey, TKey toKey)
        {
            TValue value = dic[fromKey];
            dic.Remove(fromKey);
            dic[toKey] = value;
        }


    }
}

namespace Extensions
{
    public static class IEnumerableHelper
    {
        public static void RemoveRange<T>(this List<T> list, IEnumerable<T> list_to_remove)
        {
            list_to_remove.Select(n => list.Remove(n));
        }

        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        public static DataTable ToDataTable<T>(this IEnumerable<T> list, string column_name)
        {
            DataTable dt = new DataTable();
            
            {
                dt.Columns.Add(new DataColumn(column_name, typeof(T)));
            }
            foreach (T t in list)
            {
                DataRow row = dt.NewRow();
                row[column_name] = t;
                dt.Rows.Add(row);
            }
            return dt;
        }

        public static double WeightedAverage<T>(this IEnumerable<T> records, Func<T, double> value, Func<T, double> weight)
        {
            if (records == null)
                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(records), $"{nameof(records)} is null.");

            int count = 0;
            double valueSum = 0;
            double weightSum = 0;

            foreach (var record in records)
            {
                count++;
                double recordWeight = weight(record);

                valueSum += value(record) * recordWeight;
                weightSum += recordWeight;
            }

            if (count == 0)
                throw new ArgumentException($"{nameof(records)} is empty.");

            if (count == 1)
                return value(records.Single());

            if (weightSum != 0)
                return valueSum / weightSum;
            else
                throw new DivideByZeroException($"Division of {valueSum} by zero.");
        }
    }
}

namespace Extensions
{
    public static class ListHelper
    {
        public static List<List<T>> SplitIntoChunks<T>(this List<T> source, int chunkSize)
        {
            return source
                .Select((x, i) => new { Index = i, Value = x })
                .GroupBy(x => x.Index / chunkSize)
                .Select(x => x.Select(v => v.Value).ToList())
                .ToList();
        }

        
        
        
        
    }

namespace Extensions

    {

        public static List<T> ToListSingle<T>(this object value)
        {
            List<T> t = new List<T>();
            t.Add((T) value);
            return t;
        }
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public static bool CanChangeType(this object value, Type type)
        {

            if (null == value || type == null) return false;
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            if (type == typeof(String))
                return true;
            if(type == typeof(DateTime))
            {
                DateTime d;
                return DateTime.TryParse(value.ToString(), out d);
            }
            if(type == typeof(Double))
            {
                double d;
                return Double.TryParse(value.ToString(), out d);
            }
            if (type == typeof(Int64))
            {
                Int64 d;
                return Int64.TryParse(value.ToString(), out d);
            }
            if (type == typeof(Int32))
            {
                Int32 d;
                return Int32.TryParse(value.ToString(), out d);
            }

            if (type == typeof(bool))
            {
                bool d;
                return bool.TryParse(value.ToString(), out d);
            }

            return false;

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }
        public static double? AsDouble(this object value)
        {
            if(null != value)
            {
                double d;
                if (Double.TryParse(value.ToString(), out d))
                    return d;
            }
            return null;
        }
        public static long? AsLong(this object value)
        {
            if (null != value)
            {
                long d;
                if (long.TryParse(value.ToString(), out d))
                    return d;
            }
            return null;
        }
        public static bool? AsBool(this object value)
        {
            if (null != value)
            {
                bool d;
                if (Boolean.TryParse(value.ToString(), out d))
                    return d;
            }
            return null;
        }

        public static int? AsInt(this object value,int? value_if_null = null)
        {
            if (null != value)
            {
                int d;
                if (Int32.TryParse(value.ToString(), out d))
                    return d;
            }
            return value_if_null;
        }

        public static DateTime? AsDate(this object value)
        {
            if (null != value)
            {
                DateTime d;
                if (DateTime.TryParse(value.ToString(), out d))
                    return d;
            }
            return null;
        }

--- FILE: Extensions\OrdialStringComparer.cs ---
namespace Extensions
{
    public class OrdinalStringComparer : IComparer<string>
    {
        private bool _ignoreCase = true;
        public OrdinalStringComparer()
            : this(true)
        {
        }
        public OrdinalStringComparer(bool ignoreCase)
        {
            _ignoreCase = ignoreCase;
        }
        public int Compare(string x, string y)
        {
            
            if (x == null && y == null)
            {
                return 0;
            }
            if (x == null)
            {
                return -1;
            }
            if (y == null)
            {
                return 1;
            }

            StringComparison comparisonMode = _ignoreCase ? StringComparison.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase : StringComparison.CurrentCulture;

            string[] splitX = Regex.Split(x.Replace(" ", ""), "([0-9]+)");
            string[] splitY = Regex.Split(y.Replace(" ", ""), "([0-9]+)");

            int comparer = 0;

            for (int i = 0; comparer == 0 && i < splitX.Length; i++)
            {
                if (splitY.Length <= i)
                {
                    comparer = 1; 
                }

                int numericX = -1;
                int numericY = -1;
                if (int.TryParse(splitX[i], out numericX))
                {
                    if (int.TryParse(splitY[i], out numericY))
                    {
                        comparer = numericX - numericY;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        comparer = 1; 
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    comparer = String.Compare(splitX[i], splitY[i], comparisonMode);
                }
            }

            return comparer;
        }
    }
}
