--- FILE: Extensions\StringHelper.cs ---
namespace Extensions
{
    public static class StringHelper
    {
        public static string ReplaceIns(this string str, string oldValue, string newValue)
        {
            return ReplaceIns(str, oldValue, newValue, StringComparison.CurrentCultureIgnoreCase);
        }

        public static bool IsInt(this string str)
        {
            foreach (char c in str)
            {
                if (c < '0' || c > '9')
                    return false;
            }

            return true;
        }
        public static string ReplaceIns(this string str, string oldValue, string newValue, StringComparison comparison)
        {
            StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();

            int previousIndex = 0;
            int index = str.IndexOf(oldValue, comparison);
            while (index != -1)
            {
                sb.Append(str.Substring(previousIndex, index - previousIndex));
                sb.Append(newValue);
                index += oldValue.Length;

                previousIndex = index;
                index = str.IndexOf(oldValue, index, comparison);
            }
            sb.Append(str.Substring(previousIndex));

            return sb.ToString();
        }

        public static string ReplaceMultipleTimes(this string str,string replace_string,string replace_with,int how_many_times)
        {
            var regex = new Regex(Regex.Escape(replace_string));
            var newText = regex.Replace(str, replace_with, how_many_times);
            return newText;
        }
        public class MixedNumbersAndStringsComparer : IComparer<string>
        {
            public int Compare(string x, string y)
            {
                double xVal, yVal;

                if (double.TryParse(x, out xVal) && double.TryParse(y, out yVal))
                    return xVal.CompareTo(yVal);
                else
                    return string.Compare(x, y);
            }
        }

        public static bool IsWildcardMatch(this string s, string wildcard, bool case_sensitive)
        {
            
            
            String pattern = "^" + Regex.Escape(wildcard).Replace(@"\*", ".*").Replace(@"\?", ".") + "$";

            
            Regex regex;
            if (case_sensitive)
                regex = new Regex(pattern);
            else
                regex = new Regex(pattern, RegexOptions.IgnoreCase);

            return (regex.IsMatch(s));
        }

        public static IEnumerable<string> ToIEnumerable(this string str)
        {
            return new string[] { str };
        }

        public static List<string> ToList(this string str)
        {
            return new List<string>(new string[] { str });
        }

        public static string LettersFromTheLeft(this string source)
        {
            string ret = null;
            for (int i = 0; i != source.Length; i++)
            {
                if (Char.IsLetter(source[i]))
                {
                    if (null == ret)
                        ret = "";
                    ret += source[i];
                }
                else
                    return ret;
            }
            return ret;
        }


        public static string LettersFromTheRight(this string source)
        {
            string ret = null;
            for (int i = source.Length - 1; i != 0; i--)
            {
                if (Char.IsLetter(source[i]))
                {
                    if (null == ret)
                        ret = "";
                    ret = ret.Insert(0, source[i].ToString());
                }
                else
                    return ret;
            }
            return ret;
        }

        public static void SortAlphaNumeric(this List<string> strings)
        {
            Regex digitPart = new Regex(@"^\d+", RegexOptions.Compiled);
            strings.OrderBy(x => int.Parse(digitPart.Match(x).Value));
            
        }
        public static bool ContainsSameValues<T>(this IEnumerable<T> list_one, IEnumerable<T> list_two)
        {
            IEnumerable<T> difference = list_one.Except(list_two);
            return !difference.Any();
        }
        public static string[] Split(this string str, string delimter)
        {
            return str.Split(new string[] { delimter }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        }

        public static List<string> SplitAndTrim(this string line, char delimiter)
        {
            List<string> parts = line.Split(delimiter).Select(p => p.Trim()).ToList();
            return parts;
        }
        public static List<string> SplitAndTrim(this string line, string delimiter)
        {
            List<string> parts = line.Split(delimiter).Select(p => p.Trim()).ToList();
            return parts;
        }

        public static bool ContainsIns(this string str, string contains)
        {
            return str.IndexOf(contains, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) >= 0;
        }

        public static string SwitchCase(this string str)
        {
            string answer = "";
            foreach (char c in str.ToCharArray())
            {
                if (Char.IsUpper(c))
                    answer += Char.ToLower(c).ToString();
                else
                    answer += Char.ToUpper(c).ToString();
            }
            return answer;
        }

        public static string PadRight(this char str, int length, char pad_char = ' ')
        {
            return str.PadRight(length, pad_char);
        }

        public static string PadCenter(this string str, int length, char pad_char = ' ')
        {
            int spaces = length - str.Length;
            int padLeft = spaces / 2 + str.Length;
            return str.PadLeft(padLeft, pad_char).PadRight(length, pad_char);
        }
        public static string TitleCase(this string title)
        {
            TextInfo textInfo = new CultureInfo("en-US", false).TextInfo;
            title = textInfo.ToTitleCase(title); 
            return title;
        }

        public static string CollapseDuplicateCharacters(this string str, char which, Nullable<char> replace_with)
        {
            List<char> chars = new List<char>();
            Nullable<char> last = null;
            int count = 0;
            bool wrote_last = false;
            foreach (char c in str.ToCharArray())
            {
                if (null == last || (null != last && c != last.Value) || c != which)
                {
                    chars.Add(c);
                    wrote_last = true;
                }
                else
                {
                    chars[chars.Count - 1] = replace_with.Value;
                    wrote_last = false;
                }
                last = c;
                count++;
            }
            return new string(chars.ToArray());
        }
        public static IOrderedEnumerable<string> OrderByOrdinal(this IEnumerable<string> strings, Func<string, string> keySelector)
        {
            return strings.OrderBy(keySelector, new OrdinalStringComparer());
        }
        public static IOrderedEnumerable<string> OrderByOrdinal(this IEnumerable<string> strings, Func<string, string> keySelector, bool ignoreCase)
        {
            return strings.OrderBy(keySelector, new OrdinalStringComparer(ignoreCase));
        }
        public static IOrderedEnumerable<string> OrderByOrdinalDescending(this IEnumerable<string> strings, Func<string, string> keySelector)
        {
            return strings.OrderByDescending(keySelector, new OrdinalStringComparer());
        }
        public static IOrderedEnumerable<string> OrderByOrdinalDescending(this IEnumerable<string> strings, Func<string, string> keySelector, bool ignoreCase)
        {
            return strings.OrderByDescending(keySelector, new OrdinalStringComparer(ignoreCase));
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        

    }

--- FILE: CommonToolkitLib\CommandBars.cs ---
namespace CommonTKLib
{
    public static class CommandBars
    {
        public static void FormatSheet(XLHelper xlh,string server)
        {
            FieldLib.Fields fields = new FieldLib.Fields(server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);
            string used_rage = xlh.UsedRangeAddressFull(null);
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, used_rage);
            xlt.SelectEntireRow(1);
            xlh.SetPreferredHeadersInternal(null, xlt.GetRowRange(1).Address);
            int last = xlh.LastUsedColumnNumber(null, used_rage);
            for (int i = 0; i != last; i++)
            {
                foreach (var col in xlt.GetHeaderArray())
                {
                    string col_name = col.ToUpper();
                    if (fields.ContainsField(col_name))
                    {
                        var fh = fields[col.ToUpper()];
                        string header_range = xlt.GetRangeEntireColumnRangeFromHeader(col.ToUpper(),false).Address;
                        
                        if (!String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fh.display_format))
                            xlh.FormatRange(header_range, fh.display_format);
                    }
                }
            }

            FixToadFormat(xlh);
            xlh.SetZoom(null, used_rage, 85);

        }

        public static void FixToadFormat(XLHelper xlh)
        {
            xlh.SearchAndReplace("Unchecked", "FALSE");
            xlh.SearchAndReplace("Checked", "TRUE");
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: CommonToolkitLib\Distance.cs ---
namespace CommonTKLib
{
    public static class Distance
    {

        public sealed class Cache
        {
            private static readonly Lazy<Cache> lazy = new Lazy<Cache>(() => new Cache());

            public static Cache Instance { get { return lazy.Value; } }

            public Dictionary<string, object> _cache = new Dictionary<string, object>();
            private Cache()
            {

            }
        }
        public static object GetCrowFlyDistance(string address_1, string address_2)
        {
            string hash = address_1 + "|" + address_2;
            double? miles = null;


            if (Cache.Instance._cache.ContainsKey(hash))
            {
                return Cache.Instance._cache[hash];
            }
            try
            {
                var locationService = new GoogleLocationService("AIzaSyBX4oR2LAxl88qON-X2qbQgIg1Y14EK6vQ");
                var point_1 = locationService.GetLatLongFromAddress(address_1);

                var latitude_1 = point_1.Latitude;
                var longitude_1 = point_1.Longitude;

                var point_2 = locationService.GetLatLongFromAddress(address_2);

                var latitude_2 = point_2.Latitude;
                var longitude_2 = point_2.Longitude;

                var sCoord = new GeoCoordinate(latitude_1, longitude_1);
                var eCoord = new GeoCoordinate(latitude_2, longitude_2);

                double meters = sCoord.GetDistanceTo(eCoord);
                miles = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.ConvertMetersToMiles(meters);
            }
            finally
            {
                Cache.Instance._cache.Add(hash, miles);
            }

            return miles;
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: CommonToolkitLib\Mail.cs ---
namespace CommonTKLib
{
    public class MailTemplate
    {
        public static void SendBulkEmailInternal(XLHelper xlh, string range_name)
        {
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, range_name);
            var rows = xlt.AllRows("VALID");
            if (xlt.ContainsColumn("ERROR"))
                xlt.ClearColumn("ERROR");
            string from = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExist<string>("email_from_override", null);
            string signature = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExist<string>("mail_signature_override", null);
            foreach (XLTableRow row in rows)
            {
                string to = row["TO"];
                string cc = row["CC"];
                string bcc = row["BCC"];

                string subject = row["SUBJECT"];
                string body = row["BODY"];

                if (File.Exists(body))
                {

                    string[] variables = row?["VARIABLES"].Split('|');
                    Dictionary<string, string> vars = new Dictionary<string, string>();
                    body = File.ReadAllText(body);
                    vars.Add(variables[0], variables[1]);
                    foreach (var v in vars)
                    {
                        body = body.Replace(v.Key, v.Value); ;
                    }

                }
                List<string> attachments = row["ATTACH"]?.Split(';').ToList();


                body = body.Replace("\n", "<br>");
                
                if (null != attachments)
                {
                    foreach (string attach in attachments)
                    {
                        if (row.ContainsColumn("ERROR") && !String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(attach) && !File.Exists(attach))
                        {
                            row.Update("ERROR", "File doesn't exist (no mail spawned)");
                            continue;
                        }
                    }
                }

                UtilsLib.Mail.CreateOutlookMail(subject, body, attachments, new string[] { to }, new string[] { cc }, new string[] { bcc }, true, true, from, signature);
            }

        }


    }
}


--- FILE: CommonToolkitLib\MailTemplates.cs ---
namespace CommonTKLib
{
    public class MailTemplates
    {
        public static DataTable GetAllTemplates(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vMailTemplates order by template";
            Query q = new Query(sql,server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static void SaveTemplate(string server,int mailtemplate_id,string subject,string body)
        {
            string sql = "update MailTemplates set subject=@subject, body=@body where id = @mailtemplate_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql,server);
            q.AddParameter("@mailtemplate_id", mailtemplate_id);
            q.AddParameter("@subject", subject);
            q.AddParameter("@body", body);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static DataRow GetSingleMailTemplate(string server,int mailtemplate_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vMailTemplates m where m.mailtemplate_id = @mailtemplate_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@mailtemplate_id", mailtemplate_id);
            return q.ExecuteTableSingleRow();
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: CommonToolkitLib\PDF.cs ---
namespace CommonTKLib
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;
    public class PDF
    {
        public static string PDFAndSpawnInternal(XLHelper xlh, string worksheet, string file_name_base, bool quiet, string base_folder, bool generate_excel = false)
        {

            if (null == base_folder)
                base_folder = Path.GetTempPath();


            string active_workbook = worksheet;
            if (null == active_workbook)
                active_workbook = xlh.ActiveWorksheetName();




            string filename_base = $"{file_name_base}.pdf";
            string filename_base_xls = $"{file_name_base}.xlsx";

            
            string filename_pdf = Path.Combine(base_folder, filename_base);
            string filename_xls = Path.Combine(base_folder, filename_base_xls);

            string full_path_pdf = xlh.SaveWorksheetAsPDF(active_workbook, filename_pdf, false);
            if (generate_excel)
            {
                xlh.ExportSheetsBETA(new string[] { worksheet }.ToList(), filename_xls, false, XLHelper.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSX, true);
            }
            if (!quiet)
            {
                var msg = DXHelper.DXMessageBox.Show("Spawn File?", "Quick Question", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
                
                if (msg == System.Windows.Forms.DialogResult.Yes)
                {
                    
                    UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnAsync(full_path_pdf);
                }
                
                UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectoryWithFileSelect(full_path_pdf, true);
            }
            return full_path_pdf;
        }

    }
}

--- FILE: CommonToolkitLib\Utils.cs ---
namespace CommonTKLib
{
    public static class Utils
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static double Extrapolate(double val, double[] vals, double[] nums)
        {
            if (vals.Length != nums.Length)
                return -99999999999999;

            DataTable tbl = new DataTable();
            tbl.Columns.Add("vals", typeof(double));
            tbl.Columns.Add("nums", typeof(double));
            for (int i = 0; i != vals.Length; i++)
            {
                tbl.Rows.Add(vals[i], nums[i]);
            }

            return MathLib.Interpolate(val, tbl, "vals", "nums").Value;
        }

    }
}

--- FILE: FieldLib\Fields.cs ---
namespace FieldLib
{
    public class Fields : ICloneable
    {
        private static Fields _fields;
      
        public static Fields GetInstance(string server, GetFieldsDelegate del)
        {
            if (null == _fields)
            {
                _fields = new Fields(server, del);
            }
            return _fields;
        }

        public object Clone()
        {
            return this.MemberwiseClone();
        }

        private string _server;

        public void ClearCache()
        {
            _fields = null;
            _cache = null;
        }
        public Fields(string server, GetFieldsDelegate del)
        {
            _server = server;
            _del = del;
        }

        public static string GetAcceptableNameFieldNameField(IEnumerable<string> fields)
        {
            List<string> acceptable_name_fields = new List<string>(new string[] { "name_simple" });
            foreach (string s in fields)
            {
                if (acceptable_name_fields.Contains(s))
                    return s;
            }
            return null;
        }

        public void FormatColumnNames(DataTable tbl,bool upper_case)
        {
            foreach(DataColumn col in tbl.Columns)
            {
                string col_name = col.ColumnName;
                if (this.ContainsField(col.ColumnName) && !String.IsNullOrEmpty(this[col.ColumnName].display_name))
                {
                    col_name = this[col.ColumnName].display_name;
                }
                else
                {
                    col_name = col_name.Replace("_", " ").TitleCase();
                }
                if (upper_case)
                    col_name = col_name.ToUpper();
                if(col.Caption != col_name)
                    col.Caption = col_name;
            }
        }
        public string GetDisplayName(string db_field)
        {
            

            FieldHelper fh = this[db_field];
            if (null != fh)
                return fh.display_name;
            return null;
        }

        public string GetDataDictionaryDisplayName(string db_field)
        {
            
            FieldHelper fh = this[db_field];
            if (null != fh)
                return fh.display_format;
            return null;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        


        internal List<FieldHelper> _cache = null;

        private List<FieldHelper> cache
        {
            get
            {
                if (null == _cache)
                {
                    return this.PopulateFieldHelpers();
                }
                else
                    return _cache;
            }
        }

        public void RemoveField(string field)
        {
            if (null != this[field])
                cache.Remove(this[field]);
        }
        public List<FieldHelper> GetFields()
        {
            return cache;
        }

        
        
        
        



        public GetFieldsDelegate _del;
        public delegate DataTable GetFieldsDelegate(string server);
        public List<FieldHelper> PopulateFieldHelpers()
        {
            DataTable table = null;
            if(null != _del)
                table = _del(_server);
            _cache = new List<FieldHelper>();
            foreach (DataRow row in table.Rows)
            {
                string field = row["field"].ToString();
                string display_format = row["display_format"].ToString();
                string bold = row["bold"].ToString();
                string display_name = row["display_name"].ToString();
                string alignment = row["alignment"].ToString();
                bool hide = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["hide"]);
                Nullable<int> force_width = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["force_width"])
                    force_width = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["force_width"]);

                FieldHelper fh = new FieldHelper();
                fh.field_name = field;
                fh.display_format = display_format;
                fh.bold = System.Convert.ToBoolean(bold);
                fh.hide = hide;
                fh.display_name = display_name;
                fh.alignment = alignment;
                fh.force_width = force_width;
                fh.pivot = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["pivot"]);
                fh.wavg_field = row["wavg_field"]?.ToString();
                fh.pivot_area = row["pivot_area"]?.ToString();
                fh.pivot_group_interval = row["pivot_group_interval"]?.ToString();
                fh.min_value = row["min_value"].AsDouble();
                fh.max_value = row["max_value"].AsDouble();
                fh.correction_mult = row["correction_mult"].AsDouble();
                fh.long_name = row["long_name"].ToString();
                if(DBNull.Value != row["excel_format"])
                    fh.excel_format = row["excel_format"]?.ToString();
                if (DBNull.Value != row["data_dictionary_display"])
                    fh.data_dictionary_display = row["data_dictionary_display"]?.ToString();
                if (DBNull.Value != row["excel_col_width"])
                    fh.excel_col_width = row["excel_col_width"].AsInt();
                _cache.Add(fh);
            }
            return _cache;
        }



        public bool ContainsField(string key)
        {
            return (null != this[key]);
        }
        public FieldHelper this[string key]
        {
            get
            {
                foreach (FieldHelper fh in cache)
                {
                    if (fh.field_name.ToUpper() == key.ToUpper())
                        return fh;
                }
                return null;
            }
        }
    }

}
